{PB, 1, 1}
oṃ mahan me voco bhargo me voco yaśo me vocaḥ stomaṃ me voco bhuktiṃ me vocaḥ sarvaṃ me vocas tan māvatu tan māviśatu tena bhukṣiṣīya | [PB, 1, 1 1]
devo devam etu somaḥ somam etv ṛtasya pathā | [PB, 1, 1 2]
vihāya dauṣkṛtyam | [PB, 1, 1 3]
badvā nāmāsi sṛtiḥ somasaraṇī somaṃ gameyam | [PB, 1, 1 4]
pitaro bhūḥ pitaro bhūḥ pitaro bhūḥ | [PB, 1, 1 5]
nṛmaṇa ūrdhvabharasaṃ tvordhvabharā dṛśeyam | [PB, 1, 1 6]

iṣa ūrja āyuṣe varcase ca | [PB, 1, 1 9]
{PB, 1, 2}
yunajmi te pṛthivīm agninā saha yunajmi vācaṃ saha sūryeṇa yukto vāto 'ntarikṣeṇa te saha yuktās tisro vimṛjaḥ sūryasya | [PB, 1, 2 1]
ṛtasya sadane sīdāmi | [PB, 1, 2 2]
ṛtapātram asi | [PB, 1, 2 3]
vānaspatyo 'si bārhaspatyo 'si prājāpatyo 'si prajāpater mūrdhāsy atyāyupātram asīdam ahaṃ māṃ prāñcaṃ prohāmi tejase brahmavarcasāya | [PB, 1, 2 4]
maruto napāto 'pāṃ kṣayāḥ parvatānāṃ kakubhaḥ śyenā ajirā endraṃ vagnunā vahata ghoṣeṇāmīvāṃ cātayadhvaṃ yuktā stha vahata | [PB, 1, 2 5]
idam aham amuṃ yajamānaṃ paśuṣv adhyūhāmi paśuṣu ca māṃ brahmavarcase ca | [PB, 1, 2 6]
vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā saṃmṛjantu rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā saṃmṛjantv ādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā saṃmṛjantu | [PB, 1, 2 7]
pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspate prabhur gātrāṇi paryeṣi viśvato 'taptatanūr na tad āmo aśnute śṛtāsa id vahantaḥ saṃ tad āśata | [PB, 1, 2 8]
pra śukraitu devī manīṣāsmad rathaḥ sutaṣṭo na vājy āyuṣe me pavasva varcase me pavasva viduḥ pṛthivyā divo janitrācchṛṇvantv āpo 'dhaḥ kṣarantīḥ somehodgāya mām āyuṣe mama brahmavarcasāya yajamānasyarddhyā amuṣya rājyāya | [PB, 1, 2 9]
{PB, 1, 3}
bekurānāmāsi juṣṭā devebhyo namo vāce namo vācaspataye devi vāg yat te vāco madhumat tasmin mā dhāḥ sarasvatyai svāhā | [PB, 1, 3 1]
sūryo mā divyābhyo nāṣṭrābhyaḥ pātu vāyur antarikṣābhyo 'gniḥ pārthivābhyaḥ svāhā | [PB, 1, 3 2]
yo 'dya saumyo vadho 'ghāyūnām udīrate viṣūkuhasya dhanvanāpa tān varuṇo 'padhamatu | [PB, 1, 3 3]
yo ma ātmā yā me prajā ye me paśavas tair ahaṃ mano vācaṃ prasīdāmi | [PB, 1, 3 4]
agnes tejasendrasyendriyeṇa sūryasya varcasā bṛhaspatis tvā yunaktu devebhyaḥ prāṇāyāgnir yunaktu tapasā somaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu | [PB, 1, 3 5]
annaṃ kariṣyāmy annaṃ praviṣyāmy annaṃ janayiṣyāmi | [PB, 1, 3 6]
annam akaram annam abhūd annam ajījanam | [PB, 1, 3 7]
śyeno 'si gāyatracchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃ pārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam | [PB, 1, 3 8]
saṃ varcasā payasā saṃ tapobhir aganmahi manasā saṃ śivena saṃ vijñānena manasaś ca satyair yathā vo 'haṃ cārutamaṃ vadānīndro vo dṛśe bhūyāsaṃ sūryaś cakṣuṣe vātaḥ prāṇāya somo gandhāya brahma kṣatrāya | [PB, 1, 3 9]
namo gandharvāya viṣvagvādine varcodhā asi varco mayi dhehi | [PB, 1, 3 10]
{PB, 1, 4}
adhvanām adhvapate svasti me 'dyāsmin devayāne pathi bhūyāt | [PB, 1, 4 1]
samrāḍ asi kṛśānuḥ | [PB, 1, 4 2]
tutho 'si janadhāyo nabho 'si pratakvāsaṃmṛṣṭo 'si havyasūdanaḥ | [PB, 1, 4 3]
vibhur asi pravāhaṇaḥ | [PB, 1, 4 4]
vahnir asi havyavāhanaḥ | [PB, 1, 4 5]
śvātro 'si pracetāḥ | [PB, 1, 4 6]
tutho 'si viśvavedā uśig asi kavir aṅghārir asi bambhārir avasyur asi duvasvān | [PB, 1, 4 7]
śundhyur asi mārjālīyaḥ | [PB, 1, 4 8]
ṛtadhāmāsi svarjyotiḥ | [PB, 1, 4 9]

ajo 'sy ekapāt | [PB, 1, 4 12]

kavyo 'si kavyavāhanaḥ | [PB, 1, 4 14]
pāta māgnayo raudreṇānīkena piṣṭata mā namo vo 'stu mā mā hiṃsiṣṭa | [PB, 1, 4 15]
{PB, 1, 5}
ṛtasya dvārau stho mā mā saṃtāptam | [PB, 1, 5 1]
namaḥ sakhibhyaḥ pūrvasadbhyo namo 'parasadbhyaḥ | [PB, 1, 5 2]
śyeno nṛcakṣā agneṣṭvā cakṣuṣāvapaśyāmi | [PB, 1, 5 3]
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvato gāyatracchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 5 4]
ūrdhvaḥ sapta ṛṣīn upatiṣṭhasvendrapīto vācaspate saptartvijo 'bhyucchrayasva juṣasva lokam mārvāg avagāḥ | [PB, 1, 5 5]
soma rārandhi no hṛdi pitā no 'si mama tan mā mā hiṃsīḥ | [PB, 1, 5 6]
soma gīrbhiṣṭvā vayaṃ vardhayāmo vācovidaḥ sumṛḍīko na āviśa | [PB, 1, 5 7]
āpyāyasva sametu te viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyaṃ bhavā vājasya saṃgathe | [PB, 1, 5 8]
avamais ta ūrvais te kāvyais te pitṛbhir bhakṣitasya madhumato nārāśaṃsasya sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 5 9]
dīkṣāyai varṇena tapaso rūpeṇa manaso mahimnā vāco vibhūtyā prajāpatis tvā yunaktu prajābhyo 'pānāya | [PB, 1, 5 10]
vāyur yunaktu manasā stomaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu | [PB, 1, 5 11]
vṛṣako 'si triṣṭupchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃpārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam | [PB, 1, 5 12]
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvatastriṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 5 13]
sūryo yunaktu vācā stomaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu | [PB, 1, 5 14]
svaro 'si gayo 'si jagacchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃpārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam | [PB, 1, 5 15]
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvatastriṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 5 16]
āyur me prāṇe manasi me prāṇa āyupatnyām ṛci yan me mano yamaṃ gataṃ yad vā me aparāgataṃ rājñā somena tad vayaṃ punar asmāsu dadhmasi | [PB, 1, 5 17]
yan me yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ mano jagāma dūragās tan ma āvartayā punar jīvātave na martave 'tho ariṣṭatātaye | [PB, 1, 5 18]
yenā hyājim ajayad vicakṣya yena śyenaṃ śakunaṃ suparṇaṃ yad āhuś cakṣur aditāv anantaṃ somo nṛcakṣā mayi tad dadhātu | [PB, 1, 5 19]
{PB, 1, 6}
aindraṃ saho 'sarji tasya ta indavindrapītasyendriyāvato 'nuṣṭupchandaso harivataḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 6 1]
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvato 'nuṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 6 2]
stutasya stutam asy ūrjasvat payasvad ā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam | [PB, 1, 6 3]
iṣṭayajuṣas te deva soma stutastomasya śastokthasya tirohnyasya yo 'śvasanir gosanir bhakṣas tasyopahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 6 4]
ṛtasya tvā deva stomapade viṣṇor dhāmani vimuñcāmy etat tvaṃ deva stomān avakaram agann aśīmahi vayaṃ pratiṣṭhām | [PB, 1, 6 5]
somehānu mehi soma saha sadasa indriyeṇa | [PB, 1, 6 6]
subhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmir devānāṃ saṃsad devānāṃ yātur yayā tanvā brahma jinvasi tayā mā jinva tayā mā janaya prakāśaṃ mā kuru | [PB, 1, 6 7]
apāṃ puṣpam asy oṣadhīnāṃ rasa indrasya priyatamaṃ haviḥ svāhā | [PB, 1, 6 8]
hāriyojanasya te deva someṣṭayajuṣaḥ stutastomasya śastokthasya yo 'śvasanir gosanir bhakṣas tasyopahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 1, 6 9]
devakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi pitṛkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi manuṣyakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asy asmatkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi yad divā ca naktaṃ cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi yat svapantaś ca jāgrataś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi yad vidvāṃsaś cāvidvāṃsaś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asy enasa enaso 'vayajanam asi | [PB, 1, 6 10]
apsu dhautasya te deva soma nṛbhiḥ sutasya | [PB, 1, 6 11]
madhumantaṃ bhakṣaṃ karomi | [PB, 1, 6 12]
śam adbhya oṣadhībhyaḥ | [PB, 1, 6 13]
kāma kāmaṃ ma āvartaya | [PB, 1, 6 14]
ūrg asy ūrjam mayi dhehi | [PB, 1, 6 15]
prāṇa somapīthe me jāgṛhi | [PB, 1, 6 16]
dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇor aśvasya vājinaḥ surabhi no mukhā karat pra na āyūṃṣi tāriṣat | [PB, 1, 6 17]
{PB, 1, 7}
aśvo 'sy atyo 'si mayo 'si hayo 'si vājy asi saptir asy arvāgasi vṛṣāsi | [PB, 1, 7 1]
ādityānāṃ patmānvihi namas te 'stu mā mā hiṃsīḥ | [PB, 1, 7 2]
vāyoṣṭvā tejasā pratigṛhṇāmi nakṣatrāṇāṃ tvāṃ rūpeṇa pratigṛhṇāmi sūryasya tvā varcasā pratigṛhṇāmi | [PB, 1, 7 3]
rathantaram asi vāmadevyam asi bṛhad asi | [PB, 1, 7 4]
aṅkā nyaṅkū abhito rathaṃ yau dhvāntaṃ vātāgram abhisaṃcaratau dūre hetir indriyavān patatrī te no 'gnayaḥ paprayaḥ pārayantu | [PB, 1, 7 5]
vaiśvānaraḥ pratnathā nākam āruhad divaḥ pṛṣṭhe mandamānaḥ sumanmabhiḥ sa pūrvavaj jantave dhanaṃ samānam ayman paryeti jāgṛviḥ | [PB, 1, 7 6]
gidaiṣa te ratha eṣa vām aśvinā ratho 'riṣṭo viśvabheṣajaḥ | [PB, 1, 7 7]
kṛśāno savyān āyaccha | [PB, 1, 7 8]
dāsano dakṣiṇān avagṛhāṇa | [PB, 1, 7 9]
{PB, 1, 8}
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ pratigṛhṇāmi | [PB, 1, 8 1]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe varuṇāyāśvaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 2]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe rudrāya gāṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 3]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe 'gnaye 'jam | [PB, 1, 8 4]
agnaye hiraṇyam | [PB, 1, 8 5]
agnīṣomābhyām ajāṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 6]
annasyānnapatiḥ prādād anamīvasya śuṣmiṇo namo viśvajanasya kṣāmāya bhuñjati mā mā hiṃsīḥ | [PB, 1, 8 7]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe tvaṣṭre 'viṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 8]
gnās tvā 'kṛntann apaso 'tanvata vayitryo 'vayan | [PB, 1, 8 9]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe bṛhaspataye vāsas tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 10]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe uttānāyāṅgirasāyāprāṇat tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 11]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe pūṣṇa uṣṭram | [PB, 1, 8 12]
vāyave mṛgaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 13]
prajāpataye hastinaṃ prajāpataye varāhaṃ prajāpataye vrīhiyavāṃs tair amṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 14]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe kṣetrapataye tilamāṣās tair amṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 15]
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe savitre 'śvataraṃ vāśvatarīṃ vā tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre | [PB, 1, 8 16]
ka idaṃ kasmā adāt kāmaḥ kāmāyādāt kāmo dātā kāmaḥ pratigrahītā kāmaḥ samudram āviśat kāmena tvā pratigṛhṇāmi kāmaitat te | [PB, 1, 8 17]
{PB, 1, 9}
raśmir asi kṣayāya tvā kṣayaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 1]
pretir asi dharmaṇe tvā dharmaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 2]
anvitir asi dive tvā divaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 3]
saṃdhir asy antarikṣāya tvāntarikṣaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 4]
pratidhir asi pṛthivyai tvā pṛthivīṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 5]
viṣṭambho 'si vṛṣṭyai tvā vṛṣṭiṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 6]
prāco 'sy ahne tvāhar jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 7]
anvāsi rātryai tvā rātriṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 8]
uśig asi vasubhyas tvā vasūn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 9]
praketo 'si rudrebhyas tvā rudrān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 10]
sudītir asy ādityebhyas tvādityān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 11]
ojo 'si pitṛbhyas tvā pitṝn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 9 12]
{PB, 1, 10}
tantur asi prajābhyas tvā prajā jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 1]
revad asy oṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 2]
pṛtanāṣāḍ asi paśubhyas tvā paśūn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 3]
abhijid asi yuktagrāvendrāya tvendraṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 4]
adhipatir asi prāṇāya tvā prāṇān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 5]
dharuṇo 'sy apānāya tvāpānān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 6]
saṃsarpo 'si cakṣuṣe tvā cakṣur jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 7]
vayodhā asi śrotrāya tvā śrotraṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 8]
trivṛd asi trivṛte tvā savṛd asi savṛte tvā pravṛd asi pravṛte tvānuvṛd asy anuvṛte tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 9]
niroho 'si nirohāya tvā saṃroho 'si saṃrohāya tvā praroho 'si prarohāya tvānuroho 'sy anurohāya tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 10]
vasuko 'si vasyaṣṭir asi veṣaśrīr asi savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 11]
ākramo 'sy ākramāya tvā saṃkramo 'si saṃkramāya tvotkramo 'sy utkramāya tvotkrāntir asy utkrāntyai tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta | [PB, 1, 10 12]
{PB, 2, 1}
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa prathamayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa madhyamayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa uttamayodyatī trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ | [PB, 2, 1 1]
jyeṣṭho jyaiṣṭhineya stuvīta | [PB, 2, 1 2]
agrād agraṃ rohaty abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva | [PB, 2, 1 3]
pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtir vipāpmanā vartate ya etayā stute nāvagato 'parudhyate nāparuddho 'vagacchati | [PB, 2, 1 4]
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 1 5]
{PB, 2, 2}
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ parivartinī triviṣṭutiḥ | [PB, 2, 2 1]
praparīvartam āpnoti ya etayā stute saṃtatā viṣṭutiḥ prāṇo 'pāno vyānas ta ṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa saṃtanoti | [PB, 2, 2 2]
ślakṣṇeva tu vā īśvarā paśūn nirmṛjaḥ saiṣā ca parācota śreyān bhavaty uta yādṛg eva tādṛṅ net tu pāpīyān | [PB, 2, 2 3]
tām etāṃ bhāllavaya upāsate tasmāt te pratigṛhṇantaḥ parīvartān na cyavante | [PB, 2, 2 4]
{PB, 2, 3}
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti yā madhyamā sā prathamā yottamā sā madhyamā yā prathamā sottamā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti yottamā sā prathamā yā prathamā sā madhyamā yā madhyamā sottamā kulāyinī trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ | [PB, 2, 3 1]
prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā stuvīta prajā vai kulāyaṃ paśavaḥ kulāyaṃ kulāyam eva bhavati | [PB, 2, 3 2]
etām evānujāvarāya kuryād etāsām evāgraṃ pariyatīnāṃ prajānām agraṃ paryeti | [PB, 2, 3 3]
etām eva bahubhyo yajamānebhyaḥ kuryāt yat sarvā agriyā bhavanti sarvā madhye sarvā uttamāḥ sarvān evainān samāvadbhājaḥ karoti nānyonyam apaghnate sarve samāvadindriyā bhavanti | [PB, 2, 3 4]
varṣukaḥ parjanyo bhavatīme hi lokās tṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa vyatiṣajati | [PB, 2, 3 5]
pāpavasīyasaṃ tu bhavati | [PB, 2, 3 6]
adharottaram apāvagato rudhyateva gacchaty aparuddhaḥ pāpīyān śreyāṃsam abhyārohati janatā janatām abhyety anyonyasya prajā ādadate na yathākṣetraṃ kalpante | [PB, 2, 3 7]
{PB, 2, 4}
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ pañcapañcinī pañcapañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ | [PB, 2, 4 1]
pāṅktaḥ puruṣaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavas tayā puruṣaṃ ca paśūṃś cāpnoti vajro vai pañcadaśo yat pañca pañca vyūhati vajram eva tad vyūhati śāntyā eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā pañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 4 2]
{PB, 2, 5}
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ | [PB, 2, 5 1]
trīn stomān prativihitā brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta | [PB, 2, 5 2]
pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tisṛbhis trivṛtaṃ saptabhiḥ saptadaśam | [PB, 2, 5 3]
vīryaṃ vai stomā vīryam eva tad ekadhā samūhate brahmavarcasasyāvaruddhyai tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 5 4.1]
{PB, 2, 6}
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir udyatī pañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ | [PB, 2, 6 1]
etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃllokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 2, 6 2]
abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva | [PB, 2, 6 3]
{PB, 2, 7}
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir daśasaptā saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ | [PB, 2, 7 1]
etayā vai devā asurān atyakrāmann ati pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ krāmati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 7 2]
abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva | [PB, 2, 7 3]
garbhiṇī viṣṭutiḥ pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 7 4]
viḍ vai saptadaśas tasyā rājā garbho viśa eva tad rājānaṃ garbhaṃ karoti | [PB, 2, 7 5]
nāvagato 'parudhyate nāparuddho 'vagacchati | [PB, 2, 7 6]
annaṃ vai saptadaśo yat sapta madhye bhavanti pañca pañcābhito 'nnam eva tan madhyato dhīyate 'naśanāyuko yajamāno bhavaty anaśanāyukāḥ prajāḥ | [PB, 2, 7 7]
vairājo vai puruṣaḥ sapta grāmyāḥ paśavo yad daśa pūrvā bhavanti saptottamā yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 2, 7 8]
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 7 9]
{PB, 2, 8}
eṣa eva vyūhaḥ saptaikamadhyā | [PB, 2, 8 1]
brahmaṇo vā āyatanaṃ prathamā kṣatrasya madhyamā viśa uttamā yat prathamā bhūyiṣṭhā bhājayati brahmaṇy eva tad ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti brahmaṇa eva tat kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti kṣatrasyāsya prakāśo bhavati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 8 2]
tām etāṃ trikharvā upāsate tasmāt te spardhamānā na vlīyante | [PB, 2, 8 3]
{PB, 2, 9}
saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti parācībhiḥ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ saptāsthitā | [PB, 2, 9 1]
bhrātṛvyavāṁ stuvīta yathā saptāsthitena matyena samīkaroty evaṃ pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ prarujati | [PB, 2, 9 2]
etām eva bahubhyo yajamānebhyaḥ kuryād yaḥ prathamo hiṅkāraḥ sa prathamāyā yat tāṃ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti tena sā sapta bhajate yat saptaiva madhye sampadyante tena sā sapta bhajate ya uttamo hiṅkāraḥ sa uttamayā yat tāṃ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti tena sā sapta bhajate sarvān evainān samāvadbhājaḥ karoti nānyonyam apaghnate samāvadindriyā bhavanti | [PB, 2, 9 3]
tām etām abhipratāriṇa upāsate tasmāt ta ojiṣṭhā svānām | [PB, 2, 9 4]
{PB, 2, 10}
eṣa eva vyūha ubhayaḥ saptaikamadhyā nirmadhyā | [PB, 2, 10 1.1]
ānujāvara stuvītāloko vā eṣa yad ānujāvaro yat sapta prathamāḥ saptottamās tisro madhye tryakṣaraḥ puruṣo lokam evāsmai tan madhyataḥ karoti tasmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 2, 10 1.2]
etām eva prajākāmāya kuryān madhyato vā eṣa saṃrūḍho yaḥ prajāṃ na vindate lokam evāsmai taṃ madhyataḥ karoti taṃ lokaṃ prajayā ca paśubhiś cānuprajāyate | [PB, 2, 10 1.3]
etām evāparuddharājanyāya kuryād viḍ vai saptadaśas tasyā rājā garbho viśa eva tad rājānaṃ nirhantyapāvagato 'parudhyate 'vagacchaty aparuddhaḥ | [PB, 2, 10 1.4]
etām evābhicaryamāṇāya kuryāt prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim eva madhyataḥ praviśanty astṛtyai | [PB, 2, 10 1.5]
{PB, 2, 11}

catura stomān prativihitā brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tisṛbhis trivṛtaṃ navabhis triṇavaṃ svayaṃ saptadaśaḥ sampanno vīryaṃ vai stomā vīryam eva tad ekadhā samūhate brahmavarcasasyāvaruddhyai tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 11 2]

{PB, 2, 13}
saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa ekayā sa tisṛbhir bhastrāvācīnabilā | [PB, 2, 13 1]

{PB, 2, 15}

etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva | [PB, 2, 15 2]
saiṣā trivṛtprāyaṇā trivṛdudayanā yat trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati navaitā ekaviṃśasyottamā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān eva tad ubhayato dadhāti tasmād ayam ardhabhāg avākprāṇa uttareṣāṃ prāṇānāṃ sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 15 3]

{PB, 2, 16}

navabhis trivṛtaṃ pratiṣṭauti pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ saptabhiḥ saptadaśaṃ svayam ekaviṃśaḥ sampannaḥ | [PB, 2, 16 2]
ya eva stomā yajñaṃ vahanti tān uttame stotre saṃtarpayati yathānaḍuho vāśvān vāśvatarān voḍhuṣaḥ saṃtarpayed evam etad uttame stotre stomān saṃtarpayati tṛpyati prajayā paśubhir ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 16 3]
etām eva purodhākāmāya kuryād brahma vai trivṛt kṣatram ekaviṃśo yat trivṛtaikaviṃśaṃ pratipadyate brahma tat kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti gacchati purodhāṃ na purodhāyāś cyavate ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 16 4]

{PB, 2, 17}

brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta tejo vai trivṛt tryakṣaraḥ puruṣo yat trivṛtāv abhito bhavatas tisro madhye yathā hi hiraṇyaṃ niṣṭaped evam enaṃ trivṛtau niṣṭapatas tejase brahmavarcasāya | [PB, 2, 17 2]
apaśavyeva tu vā īśvarā paśūn nirdahaḥ kilāsatvān nūbhayamati hi niṣṭapataḥ | [PB, 2, 17 3]
etām evābhiśasyamānāya kuryācchamalaṃ vā etam ṛcchati yam aślīlā vāg ṛcchati yaivainam asāv aślīlaṃ vāg vadati tām asya trivṛtau niṣṭapatas tejasvī bhavati ya etayā stute | [PB, 2, 17 4]

{PB, 3, 2}

{PB, 3, 3}

anto vai trayastriṃśaḥ paramo vai trayastriṃśa stomānāṃ saptabhir vihitaikā paricarā sapta grāmyāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yat saptabhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tad antataḥ paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā trayastriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 3 2]
{PB, 3, 4}

anto vai trayastriṃśo yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmaty evam etan nedīyaḥsaṃkramayā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmati | [PB, 3, 4 2]
pañcabhir vihitās tisraḥ paricarāḥ pāṅktāḥ paśava etāvān puruṣo yadātmā prajā jāyā yat pañcabhir vidadhāti tisraḥ paricarā bhavanti yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati paśumān bhavati ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 4 3]
{PB, 3, 5}

{PB, 3, 6}

yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā śākhāyāḥ śākhām ālambham upāvarohed evam etayemaṃ lokam upāvarohati pratiṣṭhityai | [PB, 3, 6 2]
trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 6 3]

{PB, 3, 7}

yo vai trayastriṃśam ekaviṃśe pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda pratitiṣṭhati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśaḥ stomānāṃ yad etāḥ sapta trayastriṃśasyottamā bhavanti saptavidhaikaviṃśasya viṣṭutir ekaviṃśa eva tat trayastriṃśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 7 2]
{PB, 3, 8}
aṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa catasṛbhiḥ sa ekayāṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa catasṛbhir aṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti sa catasṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ | [PB, 3, 8 1]
paśavo vai chandomā yad aṣṭābhyo 'ṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti | [PB, 3, 8 2]
catasṛbhir vihitaikā paricarā catuṣpādāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yaccatasṛbhir vidadhātyekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā caturviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 8 3]
{PB, 3, 9}
pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā caturdaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ | [PB, 3, 9 1]
brahmaṇo vā āyatanaṃ prathamā kṣatrasya madhyamā viśa uttamā yat pañcadaśinyau pūrve bhavataś caturdaśottamā brahmaṇi caiva tat kṣatre caujo vīryaṃ dadhāti brahmaṇe caiva tat kṣatrāya ca viśam anugāṃ karoti kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 9 2]
astomā vā ete yacchandomā ayujo hi stomā yugmanti chandāṃsi yad eṣā yujinī catuścatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutis tenāstomāḥ | [PB, 3, 9 3]
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā catuścatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 9 4]
{PB, 3, 10}
caturdaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ sa ekayā pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhir nirmadhyā | [PB, 3, 10 1]
astīva vā ayaṃ loko 'stīvāsau chidram ivedam antarikṣaṃ yad eṣā nirmadhyā bhavatīmān eva lokān anuprajāyate pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya etayā stute | [PB, 3, 10 2]
{PB, 3, 11}
pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ caturdaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa daśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ | [PB, 3, 11 1]

{PB, 3, 12}
ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa dvādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa dvādaśabhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa dvādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ | [PB, 3, 12 1]

{PB, 3, 13}

{PB, 5, 2}

yo vai mahāvrate sahasraṃ protaṃ veda pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti | [PB, 5, 2 2]
tasya prācī dik śiras tac chandobhiḥ sahasram asāv anyataraḥ pakṣaḥ sa nakṣatraiḥ sāhasro 'yam anyataraḥ pakṣaḥ sa oṣadhibhiś ca vanaspatibhiś ca sāhasro 'ntarikṣam ātmā tad vayobhiḥ sāhasraṃ pratīcī dik pucchaṃ tad agnibhiś ca raśmibhiś ca sāhasraṃ pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 5, 2 3]

rājanaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryam | [PB, 5, 2 6]

{PB, 5, 5}

{PB, 5, 6}
sarve sahartvijo mahāvratena stuvīran | [PB, 5, 6 1]

tad yady evaṃ kuryur ekaikayā stotrīyayāstutayodgātāram abhisameyuḥ | [PB, 5, 6 3]
tisṛbhir udgātātmana udgīyātha yā śirasaḥ stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyād aparābhis tisṛbhir udgīyātha yā dakṣiṇasya pakṣasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyād aparābhis tisṛbhir udgīyātha yottarasya pakṣasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyāt tisṛbhir vaikayā vā stutaṃ syād atha yā pucchasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyāt | [PB, 5, 6 4]
ātmany eva tad aṅgāni pratidadhati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [PB, 5, 6 5]
atho khalv āhuḥ katham adhvaryur bahvṛcaḥ sāma gāyed ity udgātaiva sarveṇodgāyet tad eva samṛddhaṃ samṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti | [PB, 5, 6 6]
havirdhāne śirasā stutvā saṃrabdhāḥ pratyañca eyus te dakṣiṇena dhiṣṇyān parītya paścān maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyasyopaviśya rathantareṇa pañcadaśena stuvīraṃs ta udañcaḥ saṃsarpeyur jaghanena hotur dhiṣṇyaṃ paścād brāhmaṇācchaṃsino dhiṣṇyasyopaviśya bṛhatā saptadaśena stuvīraṃs te yenaiva prasarpeyus tena punar niḥsṛpyottareṇāgnīdhraṃ parītya paścād gārhapatyasyopaviśya pucchenaikaviṃśena stuvīraṃs te yenaiva niḥsarpeyus tena punaḥ prasṛpya yathāyatanam upaviśyāsandīm āruhyodgātātmanodgāyati | [PB, 5, 6 7]
taṃ patnyo 'paghāṭilābhir upagāyanty ārtvijyam eva tat patnyaḥ kurvanti saha svargaṃ lokam ayāmeti | [PB, 5, 6 8]
kule kule 'nnaṃ kriyate tad yat pṛccheyuḥ kim idaṃ kurvantītīme yajamānā annam atsyantīti brūyuḥ | [PB, 5, 6 9]
yo vai dīkṣitānāṃ pāpaṃ kīrtayati tṛtīyam evāṃśaṃ pāpmano haraty annādas tṛtīyaṃ pipīlikās tṛtīyam | [PB, 5, 6 10]
parimādbhiś caranti tvak ca vā etal loma ca mahāvratasya yat parimādas tvacaṃ caiva tal loma ca mahāvratasyāptvāvarundhate | [PB, 5, 6 11]
vāṇaṃ vitanvanty anto vai vāṇo 'nto mahāvratam antenaiva tad antam abhivādayanti | [PB, 5, 6 12]
śatatantrīko bhavati śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ śatavīryaḥ | [PB, 5, 6 13]

pari kumbhinyo mārjālīyaṃ yantīdaṃ madhv idaṃ madhv iti saghoṣā eva tad vayo bhūtvā saha svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti | [PB, 5, 6 15]
{PB, 5, 7}
devā vai vācaṃ vyabhajanta tasyā yo raso 'tyaricyata tad gaurīvitam abhavad anuṣṭubham anu pariplavate vāg anuṣṭub vāco raso gaurīvitam | [PB, 5, 7 1]

svarṇidhanam anvahaṃ bhavati | [PB, 5, 7 7]
devakṣetraṃ vā ete 'bhyārohanti ye svarṇidhanam upayanti sa u vai sattriṇaḥ sattram upanayed ity āhur ya enān devakṣetram abhyārohayed iti na vai devakṣetra āsīna ārtim ārchati yat svarṇidhanam anvahaṃ bhavati naiva kāṃcanārtim ārchanti | [PB, 5, 7 8]
cyavante vā ete 'smāllokād ity āhur ye svarṇidhanam upayantīti yad ṛcā svarūpaṃ yanty asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhanti yad ekāro 'ntarikṣe yat sāmnāmuṣmin sarveṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti svarṇidhanena tuṣṭuvānāḥ | [PB, 5, 7 9]
sujñānaṃ bhavati | [PB, 5, 7 10]

{PB, 5, 8}

okonidhanaṃ ṣaḍahamukhe bhavati | [PB, 5, 8 7]

{PB, 5, 9}
ekāṣṭakāyāṃ dīkṣeran | [PB, 5, 9 1]
eṣā vai saṃvvatsarasya patnī yad ekāṣṭakaitasyāṃ vā etāṃ rātriṃ vasati sākṣād eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante | [PB, 5, 9 2]

caturahe purastāt paurṇamāsyā dīkṣeran | [PB, 5, 9 12]
teṣām ekāṣṭakāyāṃ krayaḥ sampadyate tenaikāṣṭakāṃ na saṃvaṭkurvanti | [PB, 5, 9 13]
teṣāṃ pūrvapakṣe sutyā sampadyate pūrvapakṣe māsāḥ saṃtiṣṭhamānā yanti pūrvapakṣa uttiṣṭhanti tān uttiṣṭhataḥ paśava oṣadhayo 'nūttiṣṭhanti tān kalyāṇī vāg abhivadaty arātsur ime sattriṇa iti te rādhnuvanti | [PB, 5, 9 14]
{PB, 5, 10}
ā vā ete saṃvvatsaraṃ pyāyayanti ya utsṛjanti | [PB, 5, 10 1]

tataḥ paśupuroḍāśenaikādaśakapālena tataḥ savanīyenaikādaśakapālena tato marutvatīyenaikādaśakapālena tataś caruṇaindreṇa tan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate | [PB, 5, 10 10]

pṛṣadājyena pracarya patnīs saṃyājayanti | [PB, 5, 10 12]

eṣa vāva yajño yad agniṣṭomaḥ | [PB, 6, 3 1]

dvādaśa stotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nu prajāyante tena paśavyaḥ samṛddhaḥ | [PB, 6, 3 3]
dvādaśa stotrāṇi dvādaśa śastrāṇi taccaturviṃśatiś caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nuprajāyante tena paśavyaḥ samṛddhaḥ | [PB, 6, 3 4]
agnau stotram agnau śastraṃ pratitiṣṭhati tena brahmavarcasyaḥ | [PB, 6, 3 5]
kiṃ jyotiṣṭomasya jyotiṣṭomatvam ity āhur virājaṃ saṃstutaḥ sampadyate virāḍ vai chandasāṃ jyotiḥ | [PB, 6, 3 6]

yat tv ity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kva tarhi turīyaṃ chando 'nuṣṭub iti | [PB, 6, 3 11]
chandasāṃ vā anvavaluptiṃ yajamāno 'nvavalupyate | [PB, 6, 3 12]
aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī hiṅkāro navama ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub dvādaśākṣarā jagatī chandobhirevānuṣṭubham āpnoti yajamānasyānavalopāya | [PB, 6, 3 13]
yo vā anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvatrāpiṃ savanāny anvāyattāṃ veda sarvatrāsyāpir bhavaty eṣā vā anuṣṭup sarvatrāpiḥ savanāny anvāyattā tad ya evaṃ veda sarvatrāpir bhavati | [PB, 6, 3 14]

{PB, 6, 4}
prajāpatir devebhya ūrjaṃ vyabhajat tata udumbaraḥ samabhavat prājāpatyo vā udumbaraḥ prājāpatya udgātā yad udgātaudumbarīṃ prathamena karmaṇānvārabhate svayaiva tad devatayātmānam ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte | [PB, 6, 4 1]
tām ucchrayati dyutānas tvā māruta ucchrayatūd divaṃ stabhānāntarikṣaṃ pṛṇa dṛṃha pṛthivīm | [PB, 6, 4 2]
tām anvārabhata āyoṣ ṭvā sadane sādayāmy avataś chāyāyāṃ samudrasya hṛdaya iti | [PB, 6, 4 3]
yajño vā āyus tasya tat sadanaṃ kriyate | [PB, 6, 4 4]
yajño vā avati tasya sā chāyā kriyate | [PB, 6, 4 5]
madhyato vā ātmano hṛdayaṃ tasmān madhye sadasa audumbarī mīyate | [PB, 6, 4 6]
namaḥ samudrāya namaḥ samudrasya cakṣuṣa ity āha vāg vai samudro manaḥ samudrasya cakṣus tābhyām eva tan namas karoti | [PB, 6, 4 7]
mā mā yūnarvā hāsīd ity āha sāma vai yūnarvā sāmna eva tan namaskaroty ārtvijyaṃ kariṣyan | [PB, 6, 4 8]
yo vā evaṃ sāmne namaskṛtya sāmnārtvijyaṃ karoti na sāmno hīyate nainaṃ sāmāpahate | [PB, 6, 4 9]
ya enam anuvyāharati sa ārtim ārchati | [PB, 6, 4 10]
ūrg asy ūrjodā ūrjaṃ me dehy ūrjaṃ me dhehy annaṃ me dehy annaṃ me dhehi prajāpater vā etad udaraṃ yat sada ūrg udumbaro yad audumbarī madhye sadaso mīyate madhyata eva tat prajābhyo 'nnam ūrjaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 6, 4 11]
tasmād yatraiṣā yātayāmā kriyate tat prajā aśanāyavo bhavanti | [PB, 6, 4 12]
sāma devānām annaṃ sāmany eva tad devebhyo 'nna ūrjaṃ dadhāti sa eva tad ūrji śritaḥ prajābhya ūrjaṃ vibhajati | [PB, 6, 4 13]
udaṅṅ āsīna udgāyaty udīcīṃ tad diśam ūrjā bhājayati pratyaṅṅ āsīnaḥ prastauti pratīcīṃ tad diśam ūrjā bhājayati dakṣiṇāsīnaḥ pratiharati dakṣiṇāṃ tad diśam ūrjā bhājayati prāñco 'nya ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvanti tasmād eṣā diśāṃ vīryavattamaitāṃ hi bhūyiṣṭhāḥ prīṇanti | [PB, 6, 4 14]
brahmavādino vadanti kasmāt satyāt prāñco 'nya ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti viparikramyodgātāra iti diśām abhīṣṭyai diśām abhiprītyā iti brūyāt tasmāt sarvāsu dikṣv annaṃ vidyate sarvā hy abhīṣṭāḥ prītāḥ | [PB, 6, 4 15]
{PB, 6, 5}
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti so 'śocat tasya śocata ādityo mūrdhno 'sṛjyata so 'sya mūrdhānam udahan sa droṇakalaśo 'bhavat tasmin devāḥ śukram agṛhṇata tāṃ vai sa āyuṣārtim atyajīvat | [PB, 6, 5 1]
āyuṣārtim atijīvati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 6, 5 2]
taṃ prohed vānaspatyo 'si bārhaspatyo 'si prājāpatyo 'si prajāpater mūrdhāsy atyāyupātram asīdam ahaṃ māṃ prāñcaṃ prohāmi tejase brahmavarcasāyeti | [PB, 6, 5 3]
yad āha vānaspatya iti satyenaivainaṃ tat prohati | [PB, 6, 5 4]

yad āha prājāpatya iti prājāpatyo hy eṣa devatāyā yad droṇakalaśo yad āha prajāpater mūrdheti prajāpater hy eṣa mūrdhna udahanyata | [PB, 6, 5 6]
yad āhātyāyupātram ity ati hy etad anyāni pātrāṇi yad droṇakalaśo devapātraṃ droṇakalaśaḥ | [PB, 6, 5 7]
devapātrī bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 6, 5 8]
brāhmaṇaṃ pātre na mīmāṃseta yaṃ brāhmaṇam iva manyate pra devapātram āpnoti na manuṣyapātrāc chidyate | [PB, 6, 5 9]
vāg vai devebhyo 'pakrāmat sāpaḥ prāviśat tāṃ devāḥ punar ayācaṃs tā abruvan yat punar dadyāma kiṃ nas tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayadhva ity abruvaṃs tā abruvan yad evāsmāsu manuṣyā apūtaṃ praveśayāṃs tenāsaṃsṛṣṭā asāmeti | [PB, 6, 5 10]
śuddhā asmā āpaḥ pūtā bhavanti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 6, 5 11]
sā punarttātyakrāmat sā vanaspatīn prāviśat tān devāḥ punar ayācaṃs tāṃ na punar adadus tān aśapan svena vaḥ kiṣkuṇā vajreṇa vṛścān iti tasmād vanaspatīn svena kiṣkuṇā vajreṇa vṛścanti devaśaptā hi | [PB, 6, 5 12]
tāṃ vanaspatayaś caturdhā vācaṃ vinyadadhur dundubhau vīṇāyām akṣe tūṇave tasmād eṣā vadiṣṭhaiṣā valgutamā vāg yā vanaspatīnāṃ devānāṃ hy eṣā vāg āsīt | [PB, 6, 5 13]
adho 'dho 'kṣaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ prohanti tasyā vāco 'varuddhyā uparyupary akṣaṃ pavitraṃ prayacchanty ubhayata eva vācaṃ parigṛhṇanti | [PB, 6, 5 14]
yasya kāmayetāsuryam asya yajñaṃ kuryāṃ vācaṃ vṛñjīyeti droṇakalaśaṃ prohan bāhubhyām akṣam upaspṛśed asuryam asya yajñaṃ karoti vācaṃ vṛṅkte yo 'sya priyaḥ syād anupaspṛśann akṣaṃ prohet prāṇā vai droṇakalaśaḥ prāṇān evāsya kalpayati | [PB, 6, 5 15]
yan nv ity āhur vācānyān ṛtvijo vṛṇate kasmād udgātāro 'vṛtā ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti | [PB, 6, 5 16]
yad droṇakalaśam upasīdanti tenodgātāro vṛtāḥ | [PB, 6, 5 17]
prājāpatyā vā udgātāraḥ prājāpatyo droṇakalaśo droṇakalaśa evainām ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte | [PB, 6, 5 18]
prāñca upasīdanti prāñco yajñasyāgre karavāmeti | [PB, 6, 5 19]
anabhijitā vā eṣodgātṝṇāṃ dig yat prācī yad droṇakalaśaṃ prāñcaṃ prohanti diśo 'bhijityai | [PB, 6, 5 20]
yannvityāhur antarāśvaḥ prāsevau yujyate 'ntarā śamye anaḍvān ka udgātṝṇāṃ yoga iti yad droṇakalaśam upasīdanti sa eṣāṃ yogas tasmād yuktair evopasadyaṃ na hy ayukto vahati | [PB, 6, 5 21]
{PB, 6, 6}
grāvnaḥ saṃsādya droṇakalaśam adhyūhanti viḍ vai grāvāṇo 'nnaṃ somo rāṣṭraṃ droṇakalaśo yad grāvasu droṇakalaśam adhyūhanti viśy eva tad rāṣṭram adhyūhanti | [PB, 6, 6 1]
yaṃ dviṣyād vimukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyā viśo 'muṣmād annādyān nirūhāmīti nirūhed viśa evainam annādyān nirūhati | [PB, 6, 6 2]
yo 'sya priyaḥ syāt saṃmukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvedam aham āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyāṃ viśy amuṣminn annādye 'dhyūhāmīty adhyūhed viśy evainam annādye 'dhyūhati | [PB, 6, 6 3]
atho tad ubhayam anādṛtyedam ahaṃ māṃ tejasi brahmavarcase 'dhyūhāmīty adhyūhet tejasy eva brahmavarcasa ātmānam adhyūhati | [PB, 6, 6 4]
yaḥ kāmayeta viśā rāṣṭraṃ hanyām iti vyūhya grāvṇo 'dho droṇakalaśaṃ sādayitvopāṃśusavanam upariṣṭād abhinidadhyād idam aham amuyā viśā 'do rāṣṭraṃ hanmīti viśaiva tad rāṣṭraṃ hanti | [PB, 6, 6 5]
yo vai daivāni pavitrāṇi veda pūto yajñiyo bhavati chandāṃsi vai daivāni pavitrāṇi tair droṇakalaśaṃ pāvayanti | [PB, 6, 6 6]
vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā punantu rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā punantv ādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā punantv etāni vai daivāni pavitrāṇi pūto yajñiyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 6, 6 7]
svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat taṃ devā na vyajānaṃs te 'trim upādhāvaṃs tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan yat prathamam apāhan sā kṛṣṇāvir abhavad yad dvitīyaṃ sā rajatā yat tṛtīyaṃ sā lohinī yayā varṇam abhyatṛṇat sā śuklāsīt | [PB, 6, 6 8]
tasmācchuklaṃ pavitraṃ śukraḥ somaḥ sa śukratvāya | [PB, 6, 6 9]
yaṃ dviṣyāt tasyaiteṣāṃ varṇānām api pavitre kuryāt pāpmanaivainaṃ tamasā vidhyati kṛṣṇam iva hi tamo yo 'sya priyaḥ syād āsaktiśuklaṃ kuryāj jyotir vai hiraṇyaṃ jyotir evāsmin dadhāti | [PB, 6, 6 10]
tasmād ātreyaṃ candreṇecchanty atrir hi tasya jyotiḥ | [PB, 6, 6 11]
abhyatṛṇat pavitraṃ vigṛhṇanti hastakāryam eva tad yajñasya kriyata etad vā udgātṝṇāṃ hastakāryaṃ yat pavitrasya vigrahaṇam | [PB, 6, 6 12]
na hastaveṣyān nirṛcchati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 6, 6 13]
yo 'pi na vigṛhṇāti prāṇād enam antaryanti | [PB, 6, 6 14]
taṃ brūyād vepamānaḥ prameṣyasa iti vepamāna eva pramīyate | [PB, 6, 6 15]
pra śukraitu devī manīṣāsmad rathaḥ sutaṣṭo na vājīty udgātā dhārām anumantrayate | [PB, 6, 6 16]
āyuṣe me pavasva varcase me pavasva viduḥ pṛthivyā divo janitrācchṛṇvantv āpo 'dhaḥ kṣarantīḥ somehodgāyety āha mahyaṃ tejase brahmavarcasāyeti | [PB, 6, 6 17]
eṣa vai somasyodgītho yat pavate somodgītham eva sāma gāyati | [PB, 6, 6 18]
achinnaṃ pāvayanti yajñaṃ caiva prāṇāṃś ca saṃtanvanti saṃtataṃ pāvayanti yajñasya saṃtatyai | [PB, 6, 6 19]

yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti mādhyandinam eva tat savanaṃ pāvayanti | [PB, 7, 3 3]
etāvanti vāva sarvāṇi sāmāni yāvanti mādhyandine pavamāne | [PB, 7, 3 4]
gāyatraṃ nidhanavad anidhanam aiḍam | [PB, 7, 3 5]
yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti sarvair eva tat sāmabhiḥ stuvanti | [PB, 7, 3 6]
ātmā vai yajñasya pavamāno mukhaṃ gāyatrī prāṇo gāyatraṃ yad gāyatryāṃ gāyatreṇa stuvanti mukhata eva tat prāṇān dadhati | [PB, 7, 3 7]
prāṇāpānā vā etāni chandāṃsi prāṇo gāyatrī vyāno bṛhaty apānas triṣṭub yad etaiś chandobhiḥ stuvanti prāṇāpānānām avicchedāya | [PB, 7, 3 8]
ime vai lokā etāni chandāṃsy ayam eva gāyatry ayaṃ madhyamo bṛhaty asāv uttamas triṣṭub yad etaiś chandobhiḥ saṃhitaiḥ stuvanty eṣāṃ lokānām avicchedāya | [PB, 7, 3 9]
yad anyac chando 'ntarā vyaveyād imāṃl lokān vicchindyāt | [PB, 7, 3 10]
gāyatreṇa stutvā nidhanavatā stuvantīyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva tad āyatanaṃ kriyate | [PB, 7, 3 11]
yad anidhanenāgre stuyur anāyatano yajamānaḥ syāt | [PB, 7, 3 12]
nidhanavatā stuvanti vīryaṃ vai gāyatrī vīryaṃ nidhanaṃ vīryeṇaiva tad vīryaṃ samardhayati | [PB, 7, 3 13]
aiḍena bṛhatīm ārabhante | [PB, 7, 3 14]
paśavo vā iḍā paśavo bṛhatī paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti | [PB, 7, 3 15]
bṛhatyāṃ bhūyiṣṭhāni sāmāni bhavanti | [PB, 7, 3 16]
tatrāpi triṇidhanam | [PB, 7, 3 17]
abaliṣṭha iva vā ayaṃ madhyamo lokas tasyaiva tad āyatanaṃ kriyate | [PB, 7, 3 18]
triṇidhanaṃ bhavati trīṇi savanānāṃ chidrāṇi tāni tenāpidhīyante | [PB, 7, 3 19]
triṇidhanaṃ bhavati traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 7, 3 20]
triṇidhanaṃ bhavaty etena vai mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ syāt | [PB, 7, 3 21]
dvyakṣarāṇi nidhanāni bhavanti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 7, 3 22]
anidhanam antato bhavati svargasya lokasyānatipādāya | [PB, 7, 3 23]
yan nidhanavat syād yajamānaṃ svargāl lokān nirhanyāt | [PB, 7, 3 24]
svāraṃ bhavati | [PB, 7, 3 25]
svareṇa vai devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati | [PB, 7, 3 26]
gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ | [PB, 7, 3 27]
prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇān eva tad ubhayato dadhāti tasmād ubhayataḥprāṇāḥ paśavaḥ | [PB, 7, 3 28]
yad gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ prāṇair eva praity apāne pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 7, 3 29]
{PB, 7, 4}
etad vai yajñasya svargyaṃ yan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ mādhyandinasya pavamānaḥ pavamānasya bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante svargasyaiva tal lokasyāyatane dīyante | [PB, 7, 4 1]
devā vai chandāṃsyabruvan yuṣmābhiḥ svargyaṃ lokam ayāmeti te gāyatrīṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvaṃs triṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvañ jagatīṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvann anuṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayālpakādiva vyāpnuvaṃs ta āsāṃ diśāṃ rasān pravṛhya catvāry akṣarāṇy upādadhuḥ sā bṛhaty abhavat tayemāṃl lokān vyāpnuvan | [PB, 7, 4 2]
bṛhatī maryā yayemāṃl lokān vyāpāmeti tad bṛhatyā bṛhattvam | [PB, 7, 4 3]
paśūn vā asyāntān upādadhuḥ paśavo vai bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante sva eva tad āyatane dīyante | [PB, 7, 4 4]
yannvity āhur anyāni chandāṃsi varṣīyāṃsi kasmād bṛhaty ucyata eṣā hīmāṃl lokān vyāpnon nānyacchandaḥ kiṃcana yāni sapta caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsi tāni bṛhatīm abhisaṃpadyante tasmād bṛhaty ucyate | [PB, 7, 4 5]
yannvity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kasmād bṛhatyā madhyandine stuvantīti | [PB, 7, 4 6]
bahiṣpavamānena vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ bṛhatyā madhyandine 'stabhnuvaṃs tasmād bṛhatyā madhyandinaṃ stuvanty ādityaṃ hy eṣā madhyandine dādhāra | [PB, 7, 4 7]
yair u kaiśca chandobhir madhyandine stuvanti tāni triṣṭubham abhisaṃpadyante tasmāt triṣṭubho na yanti mādhyandināt savanāt | [PB, 7, 4 8]
{PB, 7, 5}
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa śocann amahīyamāno 'tiṣṭhat sa etad āmahīyavam apaśyat tenemāḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā amahīyanta yad amahīyanta tasmād āmahīyavam | [PB, 7, 5 1]
tā asmāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tāsāṃ divi sad bhūmy ādada iti prāṇān ādatta tā enaṃ prāṇeṣv ātteṣu punar upāvartanta tābhya ugraṃ śarma mahi śrava iti punaḥ prāṇān prāyacchat tā asmād ud evāyodhaṃs tāsāṃ stauṣa iti manyūn avāśṛṇāt tato vai tasmai tāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta | [PB, 7, 5 2]
tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 5 3]
prajānāṃ ca vā eṣā sṛṣṭiḥ pāpavasīyasaś ca vidhṛtir yad āmahīyavam | [PB, 7, 5 4]
vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 5 5]
devā vai yaśaskāmāḥ sattram āsatāgnir indro vāyur makhas te 'bruvan yan no yaśa ṛchāt tan naḥ sahāsad iti teṣāṃ makhaṃ yaśa ārchat tad ādāyāpākrāmat tad asya prāsahāditsanta taṃ paryayatanta svadhanuḥ pratiṣṭabhyātiṣṭhat tasya dhanurārtnir ūrdhvā patitvā śiro 'chinat sa pravargyo 'bhavad yajño vai makho yat pravargyaṃ pravṛñjanti yajñasyaiva tacchiraḥ pratidadhati | [PB, 7, 5 6]
tad devā yaśo vyabhajanta tasyāgnī rauravaṃ prābṛhata | [PB, 7, 5 7]
tad vai sa paśuvīryaṃ prābṛhata paśavo vai rauravam | [PB, 7, 5 8]
paśumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 5 9]
agnir vai rūras tasyaitad rauravam | [PB, 7, 5 10]
asurā vai devān paryayatanta tata etāv agnī rūrau viṣvañcau stobhāv apaśyat tābhyām enān pratyauṣat te pratyuṣyamāṇā aravanta yad aravanta tasmād rauravam | [PB, 7, 5 11]
athendro yaudhājayaṃ prābṛhata tad vai sa vajraṃ prābṛhata vajro vai yaudhājayam | [PB, 7, 5 12]
vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 5 13]
indro vai yudhājit tasyaitad yaudhājayam | [PB, 7, 5 14]
yudhā maryā ajaiṣmeti tasmād yaudhājayam | [PB, 7, 5 15]
atha vāyur auśanaṃ prābṛhata | [PB, 7, 5 16]
tad vai sa prāṇavīryaṃ prābṛhata prāṇā vā auśanam | [PB, 7, 5 17]
sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 5 18]
vāyur vā uśanās tasyaitad auśanam | [PB, 7, 5 19]
uśanā vai kāvyo 'surāṇāṃ purohita āsīt taṃ devāḥ kāmadughābhir upāmantrayanta tasmā etāny auśanāni prāyacchan kāmadughā vā auśanāni | [PB, 7, 5 20]
kāmadughā enam upatiṣṭhante ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 5 21]
{PB, 7, 6}
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tūṣṇīṃ manasādhyāyat tasya yan manasy āsīt tad bṛhat samabhavat | [PB, 7, 6 1]
sa ādīdhīta garbho vai me 'yam antarhitas taṃ vācā prajanayā iti | [PB, 7, 6 2]
sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sā vāg rathantaram anvapadyata | [PB, 7, 6 3]
rathaṃ maryāḥ kṣepṇātārīd iti tad rathantarasya rathantaratvam | [PB, 7, 6 4]
tato bṛhad anuprājāyata bṛhan maryā idaṃ sa jyog antarabhūd iti tad bṛhato bṛhattvam | [PB, 7, 6 5]
yathā vai putro jyeṣṭha evaṃ bṛhat prajāpateḥ | [PB, 7, 6 6]
jyeṣṭhabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etat | [PB, 7, 6 7]
pra jyaiṣṭhyam āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 6 8]
yan nv ity āhur bṛhat pūrvaṃ prajāpatau samabhavat kasmād rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśa iti | [PB, 7, 6 9]
bṛhad eva pūrvaṃ samabhavad rathantaraṃ tu pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭyāsṛjata tasmāt pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe | [PB, 7, 6 10]
tayoḥ samānaṃ nidhanam āsīt tasmin nātiṣṭhetāṃ ta ājim aitāṃ tayor has iti bṛhat prāṇam udajayad as iti rathantaram apānam abhisamaveṣṭata | [PB, 7, 6 11]
prāṇāpānau vai bṛhadrathantare jyog āmayāvina ubhe kuryād apakrāntau vā etasya prāṇāpānau yasya jyog āmayati prāṇāpānāv evāsmin dadhāti | [PB, 7, 6 12]
yan nv ity āhur ubhe bṛhadrathantare bahirṇidhane kasmād bṛhad bahirṇidhanāni bhajate 'ntarṇidhanāni rathantaram iti | [PB, 7, 6 13]
prāṇo bṛhat tasmād bahirṇidhanāni bhajate bahir hi prāṇo 'pāno rathantaraṃ tasmād antarṇidhanāni bhajate 'ntar hy apānaḥ | [PB, 7, 6 14]
mahāvṛkṣau vai bṛhadrathantare nidhane na samarpye | [PB, 7, 6 15]
yad vai mahāvṛkṣau samṛcchete bahu tatra vibhagnaṃ prabhagnaṃ śete | [PB, 7, 6 16]
airaṃ vai bṛhad aiḍaṃ rathantaraṃ mano vai bṛhad vāg rathantaraṃ sāma vai bṛhad ṛg rathantaraṃ prāṇo vai bṛhad apāno rathantaram asau vai loko bṛhad ayaṃ rathantaram etāni manasānvīkṣyodgāyet kﾱptābhyām evābhyām udgāyati | [PB, 7, 6 17]
{PB, 7, 7}
paśavo vai bṛhadrathantare aṣṭākṣareṇa prathamāyā ṛcaḥ prastauty aṣṭāśaphāṃs tat paśūn avarunddhe | [PB, 7, 7 1]
dvyakṣareṇottarayor ṛcoḥ prastauti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 7, 7 2]
pañcākṣareṇa rathantarasya pratiharati pāṅktāṃs tat paśūn avarunddhe | [PB, 7, 7 3]
caturakṣareṇa bṛhataḥ pratiharati catuṣpadas tat paśūn avarunddhe | [PB, 7, 7 4]
na vai bṛhan na rathantaram ekaṃ chando 'yacchat tataḥ kakubhāv uttare upādadhus tasmād bṛhatī prathamā kakubhāv uttare tasmād bṛhadrathantare ekarcena kurvanti na hi te ekaṃ chando 'yacchat | [PB, 7, 7 5]
nava bṛhato rohān rohati nava prāṇāḥ prāṇān evāvarunddhe | [PB, 7, 7 6]
trīn prathamāyāṃ rohati bhūtaṃ bhavad bhaviṣyat tān evāvarunddhe trīn madhyamāyāṃ rohaty ātmānaṃ prajāṃ paśūṃs tān evāvarunddhe trīn uttamāyāṃ rohati traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 7, 7 7]
sarvān kāmān avarunddhe ya evaṃ vidvān bṛhato rohān rohati | [PB, 7, 7 8]
vajreṇa vā etat prastotodgātāram abhipravartayati yad rathantaraṃ prastauti samudram antardhāyodgāyed vāg ity ādeyaṃ vāg vai samudraḥ samudram evāntardadhāty ahiṃsāyai | [PB, 7, 7 9]
balavad geyaṃ vajram evaṃ pravṛttaṃ pratyudgṛhṇāti | [PB, 7, 7 10]
valvalā kurvatā geyam abhilobhayateva vajram evābhilobhayati | [PB, 7, 7 11]
kṣipraṃ geyaṃ svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [PB, 7, 7 12]
devaratho vai rathantaram akṣareṇākṣareṇa pratiṣṭhāpayatodgeyam areṇāreṇa hi rathaḥ pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 7, 7 13]
yo vai devaratham ananvālabhyātiṣṭhaty avāsmāt padyata iyaṃ vai devaratha imām ālabhyodgāyen nāsmād avapadyate | [PB, 7, 7 14]
īśvaraṃ vai rathantaram udgātuś cakṣuḥ pramathitoḥ prastūyamāne saṃmīlet svar dṛśaṃ prativīkṣeta nainaṃ cakṣur jahāti | [PB, 7, 7 15]
prajananaṃ vai rathantaraṃ yat tasthuṣa ity āhāsthāyukodgātur vāg bhavaty api prajananaṃ hanty asthuṣa iti vaktavyaṃ susthuṣa iti vā sthāyukodgātur vāg bhavati na prajananam api hanti | [PB, 7, 7 16]
pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta tair devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ rathantaraṃ mahimnā nāśaknod utpatat | [PB, 7, 7 17]
tasya vaśiṣṭho mahimno vinidhāya tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam ait tān saṃbhṛtyodgāyet | [PB, 7, 7 18]
yas te goṣu mahimā yas te apsu rathe vā te stanayitnau ya u te yas te agnau mahimā tena saṃbhava rathantara draviṇavan na edhi | [PB, 7, 7 19]
{PB, 7, 8}
apo vā ṛtvyam ārchat tāsāṃ vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhe vyavartata tato vasu vāmaṃ samabhavat tasmin mitrāvaruṇau paryapaśyatāṃ tāv abrūtāṃ vāmaṃ maryā idaṃ deveṣv ājanīti tasmād vāmadevyam | [PB, 7, 8 1]
tat parigṛhṇantāv abrūtām idam avidāvedaṃ nau mābhyarttiḍhvam iti tat prajāpatir abravīn mad vā etaddhy ajani mama vā etad iti tad agnir abravīn māṃ vā etad anvajani mama vā etad iti tad indro 'bravīcchreṣṭhasthā vā etad ahaṃ vaḥ śreṣṭho 'smi mama vā etad iti tad viśve devā abruvann asmaddevatyaṃ vā etad yad adbhyo 'dhi samabhūd asmākaṃ vā etad iti tat prajāpatir abravīt sarveṣāṃ na idam astu sarva idam upajīvāmeti tat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadhuḥ sarvadevatyaṃ vai vāmadevyam | [PB, 7, 8 2]
yat kavatīṣu tena prājāpatyaṃ ko hi prajāpatir yad aniruktāsu tena prājāpatyam anirukto hi prajāpatiḥ | [PB, 7, 8 3]
yad gāyatrīṣu tenāgneyaṃ gāyatracchandā hy agniḥ | [PB, 7, 8 4]
yat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadhus tenaindraṃ sarvāṇi hi pṛṣṭhānīndrasya niṣkevalyāni | [PB, 7, 8 5]
yan maitrāvaruṇo 'nuśaṃsati tena maitrāvaruṇam | [PB, 7, 8 6]
yad bahudevatyam uttamaṃ padaṃ tena vaiśvadevaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 7, 8 7]
prajāpatir vā etāṃ gāyatrīṃ yonim apaśyat sa ādīdhītāsmād yoneḥ pṛṣṭhāni sṛjā iti | [PB, 7, 8 8]
sa rathantaram asṛjata tad rathasya ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata | [PB, 7, 8 9]
sa bṛhad asṛjata tat stanayitnor ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata sa vairūpam asṛjata tad vātasya ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata | [PB, 7, 8 10]
sa vairājam asṛjata tad agner ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata | [PB, 7, 8 11]
sa śakvarīr asṛjata tad apāṃ ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata | [PB, 7, 8 12]
sa revatīr asṛjata tad gavāṃ ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata | [PB, 7, 8 13]
etair vā etāni saha ghoṣair asṛjyanta | [PB, 7, 8 14]
sarve 'smin ghoṣāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyā vāco vadanti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 8 15]
{PB, 7, 9}
pitā vai vāmadevyaṃ putrāḥ pṛṣṭhāni | [PB, 7, 9 1]
etasmād vā etāni yoner asṛjyanta | [PB, 7, 9 2]
tasmāt pṛṣṭhānāṃ stotraṃ vāmadevyenānuṣṭuvanti śāntyai | [PB, 7, 9 3]
yaddhi putro 'śāntaṃ carati pitā tacchamayati | [PB, 7, 9 4]
ayaṃ vai loko madhyamo vāmadevyam etasmād vā imau lokau viṣvañcāv asṛjyetāṃ bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ ca | [PB, 7, 9 5]
yad rathantareṇa stuvanti ye rathantarāḥ paśavo 'ntarīkṣaṃ ta upaśrayanti yad bṛhatā stuvanti ye bārhatāḥ paśavo 'ntarīkṣaṃ ta upaśrayanti te vāmadevyasya stotreṇāvaruddhāḥ | [PB, 7, 9 6]
dhruva āsīno vāmadevyenodgāyet paśūnām upavṛttyai | [PB, 7, 9 7]
upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 9 8]
antarikṣaṃ vai vāmadevyam adhūnvatevodgeyam adhūtam ivāntarikṣaṃ paśavo vai vāmadevyam ahiṃsatevodgeyaṃ paśūnām ahiṃsāyai | [PB, 7, 9 9]
katham iva vāmadevyaṃ geyam ity āhuḥ | [PB, 7, 9 10]
yathāṅkulī putrān saṃdaśyāsaṃbhindantī harati yathā vāto 'psu śanair vāti | [PB, 7, 9 11]
svadhūr vāmadevyaṃ geyam | [PB, 7, 9 12]
yo vai svadhūr vāmadevyaṃ gāyati svadhūr bhavati | [PB, 7, 9 13]
yāty asyānyo niyānena nānyasya niyānena yāti | [PB, 7, 9 14]
na bṛhato na rathantarasyānurūpaṃ geyaṃ svenaivāyatanena geyam āyatanavān bhavati | [PB, 7, 9 15]
devā vai paśūn vyabhajanta te rudram antarāyaṃs tān vāmadevyasya stotra upekṣate | [PB, 7, 9 16]
aniruktaṃ geyam | [PB, 7, 9 17]
yan nirāha rudrāya paśūn apidadhāti rudras tāṃ samāṃ paśūn ghātuko bhavati | [PB, 7, 9 18]
revatīṣu vāmadevyena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta | [PB, 7, 9 19]
āpo vai revatyaḥ paśavo vāmadevyam adbhya evāsmai paśūn prajanayati | [PB, 7, 9 20]
anavarttiḥ paśuto bhavati prajā svasya mīliteva bhavati | [PB, 7, 9 21]
kavatībhyo hy eti prajāpateḥ | [PB, 7, 9 22]
{PB, 7, 10}
imau vai lokau sahāstāṃ tau viyantāv abrūtāṃ vivāhaṃ vivahāvahai saha nāv astv iti | [PB, 7, 10 1]
tayor ayam amuṣmai śyaitaṃ prāyacchan naudhasam asāv asmai | [PB, 7, 10 2]
tata enayor nidhane viparyakrāmatāṃ devavivāho vai śyaitanaudhase | [PB, 7, 10 3]
pravasīyāṃsaṃ vivāham āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 10 4]
ito vā ime lokā ūrdhvāḥ kalpamānā yanty amuto 'rvāñcaḥ kalpamānā āyanti | [PB, 7, 10 5]
yad rathantareṇa stuvantīmaṃ lokaṃ tena yunakty antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyena naudhasenāmuṃ yad bṛhatā stuvanty amuṃ lokaṃ tena yunakty antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyena śyaitenemam | [PB, 7, 10 6]
kﾱptān imāṃllokān upāste ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 10 7]
bṛhadrathantare vai śyaitanaudhase yad rathantarāya naudhasaṃ prati prayuñjanti bṛhad evāsmai tat prati prayuñjanti bṛhaddhy etat parokṣaṃ yan naudhasaṃ yad bṛhate śyaitaṃ prati prayuñjanti rathantaram evāsmai tat prati prayuñjanti rathantaraṃ hy etat parokṣaṃ yacchyaitam | [PB, 7, 10 8]
ubhābhyāṃ bṛhadrathantarābhyāṃ stute ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 7, 10 9]
devā vai brahma vyabhajanta tānnodhāḥ kākṣīvata āgacchat te 'bruvann ṛṣir na āgaṃstasmai brahma dadāmeti tasmā etat sāma prāyacchaṃs tasmān naudhasaṃ brahma vai naudhasam | [PB, 7, 10 10]
brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati | [PB, 7, 10 11]
athaitacchyaitam | [PB, 7, 10 12]
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnābhivyāharat te 'smā atiṣṭhanta te śetyā abhavan yacchetyā abhavaṃs tasmācchyaitaṃ paśavo vai śyaitam | [PB, 7, 10 13]
paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati | [PB, 7, 10 14]
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā aśocaṃs tāḥ śyaitena huṃmā ity abhyajighrat tato vai tāḥ samaidhanta samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā yatraivaṃ vidvāñchyaitenodgāyati | [PB, 7, 10 15]
eṣa vai yajamānasya prajāpatir yad udgātā yacchyaitena hiṃkaroti prajāpatir eva bhūtvā prajā abhijighrati | [PB, 7, 10 16]
vasunidhanaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vasu paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 7, 10 17]
{PB, 8, 1}
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanam abhicaraṇīyasya brahmasāma kuryād abhinidhanaṃ mādhyandine pavamāne | [PB, 8, 1 1]
deveṣur vā eṣā yad vaṣaṭkāro 'bhīti vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharad abhītyevāsmai vajraṃ prahṛtya deveṣvā vaṣaṭkāreṇa vidhyati | [PB, 8, 1 2]
traikakubhaṃ paśukāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt tvam aṅga praśaṃsiṣa ity etāsu | [PB, 8, 1 3]
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta rāyovājo bṛhadgiriḥ pṛthuraśmis te 'bruvan ko naḥ putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro 'bravīt tāṃs trikakub adhinidhāyācarat sa etat sāmāpaśyad yat trikakub apaśyat tasmāt traikakubham | [PB, 8, 1 4]
sa ātmānam eva punar upādhāvat tvam aṅga praśaṃsiṣo devaḥ śaviṣṭha martyaṃ na tvad anyo maghavann asti ca marḍitendra bravīmi te vaca iti sa etena ca pragāthenaitena sāmnā sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata tān ebhyaḥ prāyacchat te pratyatiṣṭhan | [PB, 8, 1 5]
yaḥ paśukāmaḥ syād yaḥ pratiṣṭhākāma etasmin pragātha etena sāmnā stuvīta pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 1 6]
trivīryaṃ vā etat sāma trīndriyam aindrya ṛca aindraṃ sāmaindreti nidhanam indriya eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 1 7]
traiśokaṃ jyogāmayāvine brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 8, 1 8]
ime vai lokāḥ sahāsaṃs te 'śocaṃs teṣām indra etena sāmnā śucam apāhan yat trayāṇāṃ śocatām apāhaṃs tasmāt traiśokam | [PB, 8, 1 9]
yām asmād apāhan sā puṃścalīṃ prāviśad yām antarikṣāt sā klībaṃ yām amuṣmāt sainasvinam | [PB, 8, 1 10]
tasmāt teṣāṃ nāśaitavyā ya eṣām āśāmeti tasmā eva śuco 'pabhajate | [PB, 8, 1 11]
śucā vā eṣa viddho yasya jyog āmayati yat traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati śucam evāsmād apahanti | [PB, 8, 1 12]
diveti nidhanam upayanti vyuṣṭir vai divā vy evāsmai vāsayati | [PB, 8, 1 13]
{PB, 8, 2}
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ pratiṣṭhākāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 8, 2 1]
kaṇvo vā etat sāmarte nidhanam apaśyat sa na pratyatiṣṭhat sa vṛṣadaṃśasyāṣ iti kṣuvata upāśṛṇot sa tad eva nidhanam apaśyat tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhad yad etat sāma bhavati pratiṣṭhityai | [PB, 8, 2 2]
vasiṣṭhasya janitraṃ prajākāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 8, 2 3]
vasiṣṭho vā etat putrahataḥ sāmāpaśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad etat sāma bhavati prajātyai | [PB, 8, 2 4]
ātharvaṇaṃ lokakāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 8, 2 5]
atharvāṇo vā etal lokakāmāḥ sāmāpaśyaṃs tenāmartyaṃ lokam apaśyan yad etat sāma bhavati svargasya lokasya prajātyai | [PB, 8, 2 6]
abhīvartaṃ bhrātṛvyavate brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 8, 2 7]
abhīvartena vai devā asurān abhyavartanta yad abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati bhrātṛvyasyābhivṛtyai | [PB, 8, 2 8]
śrāyantīyaṃ yajñavibhraṣṭāya brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 8, 2 9]
prajāpatir uṣasam adhyait svāṃ duhitaraṃ tasya retaḥ parāpatat tad asyāṃ nyaṣicyata tad aśrīṇād idaṃ me mā duṣad iti tat sad akarot paśūn eva | [PB, 8, 2 10]
yacchrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati śrīṇāti caivainaṃ sac ca karoti | [PB, 8, 2 11]
{PB, 8, 3}
devāś ca vā asurāś caiṣu lokeṣv aspardhanta te devāḥ prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs tebhya etat sāma prāyacchad etenainān kālayiṣyadhvam iti tenainān ebhyo lokebhyo 'kālayanta yad akālayanta tasmāt kāleyam | [PB, 8, 3 1]
ebhyo vai lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ kālayate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 8, 3 2]
stomo vai deveṣu taro nāmāsīd yajño 'sureṣu vidadvasus te devās tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomena yajñam asurāṇām avṛñjata | [PB, 8, 3 3]
stomena yajñaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 8, 3 4]
sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te 'vacchidya tṛtīyasavanaṃ mādhyandinena savanena saha svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tad devāḥ kāleyena samatanvan yat kāleyaṃ bhavati tṛtīyasavanasya saṃtatyai | [PB, 8, 3 5]
vidadvasu vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti prastauti tṛtīyasavanam eva tad abhyativadati | [PB, 8, 3 6]
sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇi kāleyaṃ yat padaprastāvaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ yad bṛhato rohān rohati tena bārhataṃ yat stobhavān pratihāras tena bārhataṃ yad dravadiḍaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 3 7]
{PB, 8, 4}
sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te sarveṇa yajñena saha svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs te devāśchandāṃsyabruvan somam āharateti te jagatīṃ prāhiṇvan sā trīṇy akṣarāṇi hitvaikākṣarā bhūtvāgacchat triṣṭubhaṃ prāhiṇvan saikam akṣaraṃ hitvā tryakṣarā bhūtvāgacchad gāyatrīṃ prāhiṇvaṃś caturakṣarāṇi vai tarhi chandāṃsy āsan sā tāni cākṣarāṇi haranty āgacchad aṣṭākṣarā bhūtvā trīṇi ca savanāni hastābhyāṃ dve savane dantair daṃṣṭvā tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād dve aṃśumatī savane dhītaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ dantair hi tad daṃṣṭvā dhayanty aharat tasya ye hriyamāṇasyāṃśavaḥ parāpataṃs te pūtīkā abhavan yāni puṣpāṇy avāśīyanta tāny arjunāni yat prāprothat te praprothās tasmāt tṛtīyasavana āśiram avanayanti yam eva taṃ gāvaḥ somam adanti tasya taṃ rasam avanayanti sasomatvāya | [PB, 8, 4 1]
te triṣṭubjagatyau gāyatrīm abrūtām upa tvāyāveti sābravīt kiṃ me tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abrūtāṃ sābravīn mama sarvaṃ prātaḥsavanam aham uttare savane praṇayānīti tasmād gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ gāyatry uttare savane praṇayati | [PB, 8, 4 2]
tāṃ triṣṭup tribhir akṣarair upait saikādaśākṣarā bhūtvā prājāyata tāṃ jagaty ekenākṣareṇopait sā dvādaśākṣarā bhūtvā prājāyata | [PB, 8, 4 3]
tasmād āhur gāyatrī vāva sarvāṇi chandāṃsi gāyatrī hy etān poṣān puṣyanty aid iti | [PB, 8, 4 4]
indras tṛtīyasavanād bībhatsamāna udakrāmat tad devāḥ svādiṣṭhayeti asvadayan madiṣṭhayeti madvad akurvan pavasva soma dhārayety apāvayann indrāya pātave suta iti tato vai tad indra upāvartata yat svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayeti prastauti tṛtīyasavanasya sendratvāya | [PB, 8, 4 5]
svādiṣṭhā vai deveṣu paśava āsan madiṣṭhā asureṣu te devāḥ svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayeti paśūn asurāṇām avṛñjata | [PB, 8, 4 6]
paśūn bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 8, 4 7]
tāsu saṃhitam | [PB, 8, 4 8]
sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te 'vacchidya tṛtīyasavanaṃ mādhyandinena savanena saha svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tad devāḥ saṃhitena samadadhur yat samadadhus tasmāt saṃhitam | [PB, 8, 4 9]
kāleyaṃ purastād bhavati saṃhitam upariṣṭād etābhyāṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ saṃtāyate | [PB, 8, 4 10]
sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇi saṃhitaṃ yat padaprastāvaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ yad bṛhato rohān rohati tena bārhataṃ yat padanidhanaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 4 11]
{PB, 8, 5}
uṣṇikkakubhāv ete bhavataḥ | [PB, 8, 5 1]
uṣṇikkakubbhyāṃ vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat kakubhi parākramatoṣṇihā prāharat tasmāt kakubho madhyamaṃ padaṃ bhūyiṣṭhākṣaraṃ parākramaṇaṃ hi tad abhisamauhat tasmād uṣṇiha uttamaṃ padaṃ bhūyiṣṭhākṣaraṃ puro gurur iva hi vajraḥ | [PB, 8, 5 2]
vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 8, 5 3]
nāsike vā ete yajñasya yad uṣṇikkakubhau tasmāt samānaṃ chandaḥ satī nānā yajñaṃ vahatas tasmāt samānāyā nāsikāyāḥ satyā nānā prāṇāv uccarataḥ | [PB, 8, 5 4]
prāṇā vā uṣṇikkakubhau tasmāt tābhyāṃ na vaṣaṭkurvanti yad vaṣaṭkuryuḥ prāṇān agnau pradadhyuḥ | [PB, 8, 5 5]
tāsu saphaṃ vipham iva vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ tṛtīyasavanasya saphatvāyāthaitat pauṣkalam etena vai prajāpatiḥ puṣkalān paśūn asṛjata teṣu rūpam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavati paśuṣv eva rūpaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 8, 5 6]
purojitī vo andhasa iti padyā cākṣaryā ca virājau bhavataḥ padyayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyann akṣaryayā ṛṣayo nu prājānan yad ete padyā cākṣaryā ca virājau bhavataḥ svargasya lokasya prajñātyai | [PB, 8, 5 7]
tāsu śyāvāśvam | [PB, 8, 5 8]
śyāvāśvam ārvanānasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ dhanvodavahan sa etat sāmāpaśyat tena vṛṣṭim asṛjata tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhat tato gātum avindata gātuvid vā etat sāma | [PB, 8, 5 9]
vindate gātuṃ pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 8, 5 10]
indras tṛtīyasavanād bībhatsamāna udakrāmat taṃ devāḥ śyāvāśvenaihāyi ehiyety anvāhvayan sa upāvartata yad etat sāma bhavati tṛtīyasavanasya sendratvāya | [PB, 8, 5 11]
athaitad āndhīgavam andhīgur vā etat paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai madhye nidhanam aiḍaṃ bhavaty etena vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yan madhye nidhanam aiḍaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ syāt | [PB, 8, 5 12]
daśākṣaraṃ madhyato nidhanam upayanti daśākṣarā virāḍ virājy eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 5 13]
abhi priyāṇi pavata iti kāvaṃ prājāpatyaṃ sāma | [PB, 8, 5 14]
prajā vai priyāṇi paśavaḥ priyāṇi prajāyām eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 5 15]
raśmī vā etau yajñasya yad auśanakāve devakośo vā eṣa yajñam abhisamubjito yad ete antato bhavato yajñasyāriṣṭyai | [PB, 8, 5 16]
{PB, 8, 6}
devāḥ vai brahma vyabhajanta | [PB, 8, 6 558803_1]
tasya yaḥ rasaḥ atyaricyata tat yajñāyajñīyam abhavat | [PB, 8, 6 558803_2]
brahmanaḥ vai eṣa rasaḥ yat yajñāyajñīyam | [PB, 8, 6 558804_1]
yat yajñāyajñīyena stuvanti brahmanaḥ eva rase yajñam pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 8, 6 558804_2]
yoniḥ vai yajñāyajñīyam | [PB, 8, 6 558805_1]
etasmāt vai yoneḥ prajāpatiḥ yajñam asṛjata | [PB, 8, 6 558805_2]
tasmāt yajñāyajñīyam | [PB, 8, 6 558805_3]
tasmāt vai etena purā brāhmaṇāḥ bahiṣpavamānam astoṣata yoneḥ yajñam pratanavāmahai iti | [PB, 8, 6 558806_1]
yajñam tatas stuvanti yonau yajñam pratiṣṭhāpayanti | [PB, 8, 6 558806_2]
asureṣu vai sarvaḥ yajñaḥ āsīt | [PB, 8, 6 558807_1]
te devāḥ yajñāyajñīyam apaśyan | [PB, 8, 6 558807_2]
teṣām yajñā yajñā vaḥ agnaye iti agnihotram avṛñjata girā girā ca dakṣase iti darśa pūrṇamāsau _ _ vayam amṛtam jātavedasam iti cāturmāsyāṇi priyam mitram na śaṃsiṣam iti saumyam adhvaram | [PB, 8, 6 558807_3]
yajñā vaḥ agnaye girā ca dakṣase _ vayam amṛtam jātavedasam priyam mitram na śaṃsiṣam iti vai tarhi chandāṃsi āsan | [PB, 8, 6 558808_1]
te devāḥ abhyārambham abhinivartyam chandobhiḥ yajñam asurāṇām avṛñjata | [PB, 8, 6 558808_2]
chandobhiḥ yajñam bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte yaḥ evam veda | [PB, 8, 6 558809_1]
etat ha sma vai āha kūśāmbaḥ svāyavaḥ brahmā lātavyaḥ kam svid adya śiśumārī yajña pathe apyastā gariṣyati | [PB, 8, 6 558810_1]
eṣā vai śiśumārī yajña pathe apyastā yajñāyajñīyam | [PB, 8, 6 558811_1]
yat girā girā iti āha ātmānam tat udgātā girati | [PB, 8, 6 558811_2]
airam kṛtvā udgeyam | [PB, 8, 6 558812_1]
irāyām yajñam pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 8, 6 558812_2]
a pramāyukaḥ udgātā bhavati | [PB, 8, 6 558812_3]
vaiśvānare vai etat udgātā ātmānam pradadhāti yat _ _ vayam iti āha | [PB, 8, 6 558813_1]
praprīm vayam iti vaktavyam | [PB, 8, 6 558813_2]
vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati | [PB, 8, 6 558813_3]
yaḥ vai nihnuvānam chandaḥ upaiti pāpīyāḥ ujjagivāḥ bhavati | [PB, 8, 6 558814_1]
etat vai nihnuvānam chandaḥ yat na śaṃsiṣam iti | [PB, 8, 6 558814_2]
nu śaṃsiṣam iti vaktavyam su śaṃsiṣam iti _ | [PB, 8, 6 558814_3]
na nihnuvānam chandaḥ upaiti | [PB, 8, 6 558814_4]
vasīyāḥ ujjagivāḥ bhavati | [PB, 8, 6 558814_5]
yasya vai yajñāḥ vāc antāḥ bhavanti vācaḥ chidreṇa sravanti | [PB, 8, 6 558815_1]
ete vai yajñāḥ vāc antāḥ ye yajñāyajñīya antāḥ | [PB, 8, 6 558815_2]
etat vācaḥ chidram yat anṛtam | [PB, 8, 6 558815_3]
yat agniṣṭoma yājī anṛtam āha tat _ asya yajñaḥ sravati | [PB, 8, 6 558815_4]
akṣareṇa antatas pratiṣṭhāpyam | [PB, 8, 6 558815_5]
akṣareṇa eva yajñasya chidram apidadhāti | [PB, 8, 6 558815_6]

virāji eva antatas pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 6 558816_2]
{PB, 8, 7}
ito vai prātar ūrdhvāṇi chandāṃsi yujyante 'muto 'vāñci yajñāyajñīyasya stotre yujyante yajñā vo agnaye girā ca dakṣasa iti dvādaśākṣaraṃ pra vayam amṛtaṃ jātavedasam ity ekādaśākṣaraṃ priyaṃ mitraṃ na śaṃsiṣam ity aṣṭākṣaram | [PB, 8, 7 1]
anuṣṭubham uttamāṃ sampādayatīyaṃ vā anuṣṭub asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 7 2]
vāg vā anuṣṭub vācy eva pratitiṣṭhati jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jyaiṣṭhya eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 7 3]
katham iva yajñāyajñīyaṃ geyam ity āhur yathānaḍvān prasrāvayamāṇa ittham iva cettham iva ceti | [PB, 8, 7 4]
vaiśvānaraṃ vā etad udgātānu prasīdann etīty āhur yad yajñāyajñīyasyarcaṃ saṃpratyāheti parikrāmatevodgeyaṃ vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati | [PB, 8, 7 5]
vaiśvānare vā etad adhvaryuḥ sadasyān abhisṛjati yad yajñāyajñīyasya stotram upāvartayati prāvṛtenodgeyaṃ vaiśvānareṇānabhidāhāya | [PB, 8, 7 6]
na ha tu vai pitaraḥ prāvṛtaṃ jānanti yajñāyajñīyasya vai stotre pitaro yathāyathaṃ jijñāsanta ākarṇābhyāṃ prāvṛtyaṃ tad eva prāvṛtaṃ tad aprāvṛtaṃ jānanti pitaro na vaiśvānaro hinasti | [PB, 8, 7 7]
apaḥ paścāt patnya upasṛjanti vaiśvānaram eva tacchamayanty āpo hi śāntiḥ | [PB, 8, 7 8]
atho reta eva tat siñcanty āpo hi retaḥ | [PB, 8, 7 9]
dakṣiṇān ūrūn abhiṣiñcanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate | [PB, 8, 7 10]
mahad iva pratyūhyaṃ mana evāsya tajjanayanti | [PB, 8, 7 11]
udgātrā patnīḥ saṃkhyāpayanti retodheyāya | [PB, 8, 7 12]
hiṅkāraṃ prati saṃkhyāpayanti hiṃkṛtāddhi reto dhīyate | [PB, 8, 7 13]
ā tṛtīyāyāḥ saṃkhyāpayanti trivṛddhi retaḥ | [PB, 8, 7 14]
{PB, 8, 8}
devā vā agniṣṭomam abhijityokthāni nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te 'gnim abruvaṃs tvayā mukhenedaṃ jayāmeti so 'bravīt kiṃ me tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abruvan so 'bravīn maddevatyāsūkthāni praṇayān iti | [PB, 8, 8 1]
tasmād āgneyīṣūkthāni praṇayanti | [PB, 8, 8 2]
tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatracchandā hy agniḥ | [PB, 8, 8 3]
te 'gniṃ mukhaṃ kṛtvā sākam aśvenābhyakrāman yat sākam aśvenābhyakrāmaṃs tasmāt sākamaśvam | [PB, 8, 8 4]
tasmāt sākamaśvenokthāni praṇayanty etena hi tāny agre 'bhyajayan | [PB, 8, 8 5]
sa indro 'bravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti varuṇas taṃ varuṇo 'nvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrāvaruṇam anuśasyate | [PB, 8, 8 6]
sa evābravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti bṛhaspatis taṃ bṛhaspatir anvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrābārhaspatyam anuśasyate sa evābravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti viṣṇus taṃ viṣṇur anvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrāvaiṣṇavam anuśasyate | [PB, 8, 8 7]
paśūn vā ebhyas tān āharat paśavo vā ukthāni paśukāma ukthena stuvīta paśumān bhavati | [PB, 8, 8 8]
bṛhatā vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tasya tejaḥ parāpatat tat saubharam abhavat | [PB, 8, 8 9]
jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yad rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ rathantaraṃ saṃdhir nāntarā bṛhatā stuvantīti yat saubhareṇa stuvanti bṛhataiva tad antarā stuvanti bṛhato hy etat tejo yat saubharam | [PB, 8, 8 10]
yadi bṛhatsāmātirātraḥ syāt saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ bṛhad eva tat tejasā samardhayati | [PB, 8, 8 11]
yadi rathantarasāmnā saubharaṃ kuryād ajāmitāyai | [PB, 8, 8 12]
devānāṃ vai svargaṃ lokaṃ yatāṃ diśo 'vlīyanta tāḥ saubhareṇo ity udastabhnuvaṃs tato vai tā adṛṃhanta tataḥ pratyatiṣṭhaṃs tataḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prājānan yaḥ svargakāmaḥ syād yaḥ pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta pra svargaṃ lokaṃ jānāti pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 8 13]
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā āśanāyaṃs tābhyaḥ saubhareṇorg ity annaṃ prāyacchat tato vai tāḥ samaidhanta | [PB, 8, 8 14]
samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā yatraivaṃ vidvān saubhareṇodgāyati | [PB, 8, 8 15]
tā abruvan subhṛtaṃ no 'bhārṣīr iti tasmāt saubharam | [PB, 8, 8 16]
vṛṣṭiṃ vā abhyastāṃ prāyacchad annam eva | [PB, 8, 8 17]
yo vṛṣṭikāmaḥ syād yo 'nnādyakāmo yaḥ svargakāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta | [PB, 8, 8 18]
hīṣiti vṛṣṭikāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryād ūrg ity annādyakāmāyo iti svargakāmāya | [PB, 8, 8 19]
sarve vai kāmāḥ saubharaṃ sarveṣv eva kāmeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 8 20]
athaitan nārmedham | [PB, 8, 8 21]
nṛmedhasam āṅgirasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ śvabhir abhyāhvayan so 'gnim upādhāvat pāhi no agna ekayeti taṃ vaiśvānaraḥ paryudatiṣṭhat tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhat tato gātum avindata | [PB, 8, 8 22]
gātuvid vā etat sāma vindate gātuṃ pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 8, 8 23]
naiva hy etad ahno rūpaṃ na rātrer yad ukthānām | [PB, 8, 8 24]
kakup prathamāthoṣṇig atha purauṣṇig anuṣṭup tenānuṣṭubho na yanty acchāvākasāmnaḥ | [PB, 8, 8 25]
{PB, 8, 9}
hārivarṇaṃ bhavati | [PB, 8, 9 1]
asurā vā eṣu lokeṣv āsaṃs tān devā hariśriyam ity asmāl lokāt prāṇudanta virājasīty antarikṣād divo diva ity amuṣmāt | [PB, 8, 9 2]
tad ya evaṃ vedaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudyemāṃl lokān abhyārohati | [PB, 8, 9 3]
harivarṇo vā etat paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai | [PB, 8, 9 4]
aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yato rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena harivarṇo 'pāhanta yad etat sāma bhavati rakṣasām apahatyai | [PB, 8, 9 5]
pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta teṣāṃ yat tejo raso 'tyaricyata tad devāḥ samabharaṃs tad udvaṃśīyam abhavat | [PB, 8, 9 6]
sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ tejo yad udvaṃśīyaṃ tasmād vā etat purā sajātāya nākran pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai | [PB, 8, 9 7]
eṣa hy eva pṛṣṭhais tuṣṭuvāno ya udvaṃśīyena stuvate | [PB, 8, 9 8]
sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇy udvaṃśīyam | [PB, 8, 9 9]
gāyanti tvā gāyatriṇa eti rathantarasya rūpam eti hi rathantaram | [PB, 8, 9 10]
ādir bṛhata ūrdhvam iva hi bṛhat | [PB, 8, 9 11]
pariṣṭobho vairūpasya pariṣṭubhaṃ hi vairūpam | [PB, 8, 9 12]
anutodo vairājasyānutunnaṃ hi vairājam | [PB, 8, 9 13]
ardheḍā śakvarīṇām atisvāro revatīnām | [PB, 8, 9 14]
ardheḍayā vai devā asurān avahatyātisvāreṇa svargaṃ lokam ārohan | [PB, 8, 9 15]
tad ya evaṃ vedārdheḍayaiva bhrātṛvyam avahatyātisvāreṇa svargaṃ lokam ārohati | [PB, 8, 9 16]
ardheḍayā vai pūrvaṃ yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayanty atisvāreṇottaram ārabhante | [PB, 8, 9 17]
upainam uttaro yajño namati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 8, 9 18]
pāṅktaṃ vā etat sāma pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavo yajña eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 8, 9 19]
āṣṭādaṃṣṭre ṛddhikāmāya kuryāt | [PB, 8, 9 20]
aṣṭādaṃṣṭro vairūpo 'putro 'prajā ajīryat sa imāṃ lokān vicichidivān amanyata sa ete jarasi sāmanī apaśyat tayor aprayogād abibhet so 'bravīd ṛdhnavad yobhe sāmabhyāṃ stavātā iti | [PB, 8, 9 21]
ṛṣer vā etat prāśodbhūtaṃ yad āṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavata ṛddhyā eva | [PB, 8, 9 22]
{PB, 8, 10}
gāyatrīṣu brahmavarcasakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur gāyatryāṃ brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā gāyatrī saṃpadyate | [PB, 8, 10 1]
tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarunddhe | [PB, 8, 10 2]
gāyatrīṣu paśukāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣoṣṇik saṃpadyate | [PB, 8, 10 3]
paśavo vā uṣṇik paśūn evāvarunddhe | [PB, 8, 10 4]
gāyatrīṣu puruṣakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyuḥ kakubhi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā kakup saṃpadyate | [PB, 8, 10 5]
puruṣo vai kakup puruṣān evāvarunddhe | [PB, 8, 10 6]
virāṭsv annādyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā virāṭ saṃpadyate | [PB, 8, 10 7]
annaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāvarunddhe | [PB, 8, 10 8]
akṣarapaṅktiṣu jyaiṣṭhyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣānuṣṭup saṃpadyate | [PB, 8, 10 9]
jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jyaiṣṭhyam evāvarunddhe | [PB, 8, 10 10]
{PB, 9, 1}
devā vā ukthāny abhijitya rātriṃ nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te 'surān rātriṃ tamaḥ praviṣṭān nānuvyapaśyaṃs ta etam anuṣṭupśirasaṃ pragātham apaśyan virājaṃ jyotiḥ tān virājā jyotiṣānupaśyanto 'nuṣṭubhā vajreṇa rātrer nirāghnan | [PB, 9, 1 1]
yad eṣo 'nuṣṭupśirāḥ pragātho bhavati virājaiva jyotiṣānupaśyann anuṣṭubhā vajreṇa rātrer bhrātṛvyaṃ nirhanti | [PB, 9, 1 2]
tān samantaṃ paryāyaṃ prāṇudanta yat paryāyaṃ prāṇudanta tat paryāyāṇāṃ paryāyatvam | [PB, 9, 1 3]
prathamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanti prathamasya paryāyasya | [PB, 9, 1 4]
prathamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāya prathamarātrāt prāṇudanta | [PB, 9, 1 5]
pāntam ā vo andhasa iti prastauti | [PB, 9, 1 6]
ahar vai pāntam andho rātrir ahnaiva tad rātrim ārabhante | [PB, 9, 1 7]
tāsu vaitahavyam | [PB, 9, 1 8]
vītahavyaḥ śrāyaso jyog niruddha etat sāmāpaśyat so 'vagacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 9, 1 9]
tama iva vā ete praviśanti ye rātrim upayanti yad oko nidhanaṃ rātrer mukhe bhavati prajñātyai | [PB, 9, 1 10]
yadā vai puruṣaḥ svam oka āgacchati sarvaṃ tarhi prajānāti sarvam asmai divā bhavati | [PB, 9, 1 11]
te madhyamaṃ paryāyam aśrayanta teṣām aurdhvasadmanena vācam avṛñjata | [PB, 9, 1 12]
vācaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 9, 1 13]
triṇidhanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 9, 1 14]
yathā vā ahno mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ triṇidhanāyatanam evam eṣa rātrer madhyamaḥ paryāyas triṇidhanāyatanaḥ salokatvāya | [PB, 9, 1 15]
madhyamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanti madhyamasya paryāyasya madhyamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāyaṃ madhyamarātrāt prāṇudanta | [PB, 9, 1 16]
ta uttamaṃ paryāyam aśrayanta teṣāṃ ghṛtaścyunnidhanena paśūn avṛñjata paśavo vai ghṛtaścyutaḥ | [PB, 9, 1 17]
paśūn bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 9, 1 18]
uttamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanty uttamasya paryāyasyottamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāyam uttamarātrāt prāṇudanta | [PB, 9, 1 19]
tān sandhinābhipalāyanta | [PB, 9, 1 20]
tān āśvinenāsaṃhāyyam agamayan | [PB, 9, 1 21]
asaṃhāyyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ gamayati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 9, 1 22]
eṣā vā agniṣṭomasya saṃmā yad rātriḥ | [PB, 9, 1 23]
dvādaśa stotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa stotrāṇi rātriḥ | [PB, 9, 1 24]
eṣā vā ukthasya saṃmā yad rātriḥ | [PB, 9, 1 25]
trīṇy ukthāni tridevatyaḥ sandhiḥ | [PB, 9, 1 26]
yathā vā ahna ukthāny evam eṣa rātreḥ sandhir nānārūpāṇy ahna ukthāni nānārūpā ete tṛcā bhavanti | [PB, 9, 1 27]
rathantaraṃ pratiṣṭhākāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt | [PB, 9, 1 28]
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 9, 1 29]
bṛhat svargakāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt | [PB, 9, 1 30]
svargo loko bṛhat svarga eva loke pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 9, 1 31]
vāravantīyaṃ vā vāmadevyaṃ vā śrudhyaṃ vaiteṣām ekaṃ paśukāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt | [PB, 9, 1 32]
paśavo vā etāni sāmāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 9, 1 33]
āśvinaṃ hotānuśaṃsati | [PB, 9, 1 34]
prajāpatir vā etat sahasram asṛjata tad devebhyaḥ prāyacchat tasmin na samarādhayaṃs te sūryaṃ kāṣṭhāṃ kṛtvājim adhāvan | [PB, 9, 1 35]
teṣām aśvinau prathamāv adhāvatāṃ tāv anvavadan saha no 'stviti tāvabrūtāṃ kiṃ tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayethe ityabruvaṃs tāvabrūtām asmaddevatyam idam uktham ucyātā iti tasmād āśvinam ucyate | [PB, 9, 1 36]
sarvāḥ khalu devatāḥ śasyante | [PB, 9, 1 37]
kṣipraṃ śasyam ājim iva hy ete dhāvanty ā sūryasyodetoḥ śaṃset sūryaṃ hi kāṣṭhām akurvata | [PB, 9, 1 38]
{PB, 9, 2}
pāntam ā vo andhasa iti vaitahavyam anyakṣetraṃ vā ete prayanti ye rātrim upayanti yad okonidhanaṃ rātrer mukhe bhavaty okaso 'pracyāvāya | [PB, 9, 2 1]
pra va indrāya mādanam iti gaurīvitam | [PB, 9, 2 2]
brahma yad devā vyakurvata tato yad atyaricyata tad gaurīvitam abhavat | [PB, 9, 2 3]
atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atiriktam etat stotraṃ yad rātrir atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 9, 2 4]
vayam u tvā tad id arthā iti kāṇvam | [PB, 9, 2 5]
etena vai kaṇva indrasya sāṃvidyam agacchad indrasyaivaitena sāṃvidyaṃ gacchati | [PB, 9, 2 6]
indrāya madvane sutam iti śrautakakṣaṃ kṣatrasāma pra kṣatram evaitena bhavati | [PB, 9, 2 7]
ayaṃ ta indra soma iti daivodāsam | [PB, 9, 2 8]
agniṣṭomena vai devā imaṃ lokam abhyajayann antarikṣam ukthenātirātreṇāmuṃ ta imaṃ lokaṃ punar abhyakāmayanta ta ihety asmiṃl loke pratyatiṣṭhan yad etat sāma bhavati pratiṣṭhityai | [PB, 9, 2 9]
ūrdhvasadmanam api śarvarīṣu prohanti | [PB, 9, 2 10]
asurā vā eṣu lokeṣv āsaṃs tān devā ūrdhvasadmanenaibhyo lokebhyaḥ prāṇudanta | [PB, 9, 2 11]
tad ya evaṃ vedaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudya sva āyatane sattram āste | [PB, 9, 2 12]
ā tū na indra kṣumantam ity ākūpāram | [PB, 9, 2 13]
akūpārāṅgirasyāsīt tasyā yathā godhāyās tvag eva tvag āsīt tām etena triḥsāmnendraḥ pūtvā sūryatvacasam akarot tad vāva sā tarhy akāmayata yatkāmā etena sāmnā stuvate sa ebhyaḥ kāmaḥ samṛdhyate | [PB, 9, 2 14]
abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sutaṃ ity ārṣabhaṃ kṣatrasāma kṣatram evaitena bhavati | [PB, 9, 2 15]
idaṃ vaso sutam andha iti gāram etena vai gara indram aprīṇāt prīta evāsyaitenendro bhavati | [PB, 9, 2 16]
idaṃ hy anv ojaseti mādhucchandasaṃ prajāpater vā eṣā tanūr ayātayāmnī prayujyate | [PB, 9, 2 17]
ā tv etā niṣīdateti daivātitham | [PB, 9, 2 18]
devātithiḥ saputro 'śanāyaṃś carann araṇya urvārūṇy avindat tāny etena sāmnopāsīdat tā asmai gāvaḥ pṛśnayo bhūtvodatiṣṭhan yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai | [PB, 9, 2 19]
yoge yoge tavastaram iti saumedhaṃ rātriṣāma rātrer eva samṛddhyai | [PB, 9, 2 20]
indra suteṣu someṣv iti kautsam | [PB, 9, 2 21]
kutsaś ca luśaś cendraṃ vyahvayetāṃ sa indraḥ kutsam upāvartata taṃ śatena vārdhrībhir āṇḍayor abadhnāt taṃ luśo 'bhyavadat pramucyasva pari kutsād ihāgahi kim u tvāvān āṇḍayor baddha āsātā iti tāḥ saṃchidya prādravat sa etat kutsaḥ sāmāpaśyat tenainam anvavadat sa upāvartata | [PB, 9, 2 22]
yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya | [PB, 9, 2 23]
{PB, 9, 3}
yadi sattrāya dīkṣerann atha sāmy uttiṣṭhet somam apabhajya viśvajitātirātreṇa yajeta sarvavedasena sarvasmā eva dīkṣate sarvam āpnoti | [PB, 9, 3 1]
yā id dakṣiṇā dadāti tābhir iti prayuṅkte | [PB, 9, 3 2]
yadi paryāyair astutam abhivyucchet pañcadaśabhir hotre stuyuḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir itarebhyaḥ | [PB, 9, 3 3]
agne vivasvad uṣasa iti sandhinā stuyuḥ prāṇā vai trivṛt stomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā rathantaraṃ sāmnāṃ prāṇāṃś caivopayanti pratiṣṭhāṃ ca | [PB, 9, 3 4]
ṣaṣṭiṃ ca trīṇi ca śatāni hotā śaṃsati | [PB, 9, 3 5]
tāvatyaḥ saṃvatsarasya rātrayaḥ saṃvatsarasaṃmitābhir eva tad ṛgbhir āśīvinam āpnoti | [PB, 9, 3 6]
yad arvāk stuvanti tad astutaṃ yat samprati stuvanti tat stutaṃ yad atiṣṭuvanti tat suṣṭutam | [PB, 9, 3 7]
yady arvāk stuyur yāvatībhir na stuyus tāvatībhir vātiṣṭuyur bhūyo 'kṣarābhir vā | [PB, 9, 3 8]
yady atiṣṭuyur yāvatībhir atiṣṭuyus tāvatībhir vā na stuyuḥ kanīyo 'kṣarābhir vā | [PB, 9, 3 9]
yady arvāk stuyus trīḍam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ nidhanam ekeḍayā ye dve tābhyām eva tat samaṃ kriyate | [PB, 9, 3 10]
yady atiṣṭuyuḥ svāram agniṣṭomasāma kāryam ūnam iva vā etat sāmno yat svaras tenaiva tat samaṃ kriyate | [PB, 9, 3 11]
{PB, 9, 4}
yadi somau saṃsutau syātāṃ mahati rātreḥ prātaranuvākam upākuryāt | [PB, 9, 4 1]
pūrvo vācaṃ pūrvaś chandāṃsi pūrvo devatā vṛṅkte | [PB, 9, 4 2]
vṛṣaṇvatīṃ pratipadaṃ kuryād indro vai vṛṣā prātaḥsavanād evaiṣām indraṃ vṛṅkte | [PB, 9, 4 3]
atho khalv āhuḥ savanamukhe savanamukhe kāryā savanamukhāt savanamukhād evaiṣām indraṃ vṛṅkte | [PB, 9, 4 4]
susamiddhe hotavyam agnir vai sarvā devatāḥ sarvā eva devatāḥ paśyañ juhoti | [PB, 9, 4 5]
saṃveśāyopaveśāya gāyatryai chandase 'bhibhūtaye svāhā saṃveśāyopaveśāya triṣṭubhe chandase 'bhibhūtaye svāhā saṃveśāyopaveśāya jagatyai chandase 'bhibhūtaye svāheti juhoti | [PB, 9, 4 6]
chandāṃsi vā abhibhūtayas tair evainān abhibhavaty ubhe bṛhadrathantare kārye | [PB, 9, 4 7]
yatra vā indrasya harī tad indraḥ indrasya vai harī bṛhadrathantare yad ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ pūrva evendrasya harī ārabhante | [PB, 9, 4 8]
tauraśravase kārye | [PB, 9, 4 9]
turaśravasaś ca vai pārāvatānāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata ete turaśravāḥ sāmanī apaśyat tābhyām asmā indraḥ śalmalināṃ yamunāyā havyaṃ nirāvahat yat tauraśravase bhavato havyam evaiṣāṃ vṛṅkte | [PB, 9, 4 10]
pūrve 'bhiṣuṇuyuḥ | [PB, 9, 4 11]
yā vai pūrvāḥ prasnānti tāḥ pūrvās tīrthaṃ jayanti pūrva evendram ārabhante | [PB, 9, 4 12]
vihavyaṃ śasyam | [PB, 9, 4 13]
jamadagneś ca vā ṛṣīṇāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata etajjamadagnir vihavyam apaśyat tam indra upāvartata yad vihavyaṃ hotā śaṃsatīndram evaiṣāṃ vṛṅkte | [PB, 9, 4 14]
yadītaro 'gniṣṭomaḥ syād ukthaḥ kāryo yady uktho 'tirātro yo vai bhūyān yajñakratuḥ sa indrasya priyo bhūyasaivaiṣāṃ yajñakratunendraṃ vṛṅkte | [PB, 9, 4 15]
atho khalv āhur duṣprāpa iva vai paraḥ panthā yam evāgre yajñakratum ārabheta tasmān neyād iti | [PB, 9, 4 16]
sajanīyaṃ śasyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyam | [PB, 9, 4 17]
asyā amuṣyā adyaśvān mithunād ahorātrābhyām evainān nirbhajati | [PB, 9, 4 18]
{PB, 9, 5}
yadi somam akrītam apahareyur anyaḥ kretavyaḥ | [PB, 9, 5 1]
yadi krītaṃ yo 'nyo 'bhyāśaṃ syāt sa āhṛtyaḥ somavikrayaṇe tu kiṃcid dadyāt | [PB, 9, 5 2]
yadi somaṃ na vindeyuḥ pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyur yadi na pūtīkān arjunāni | [PB, 9, 5 3]
gāyatrī somam āharat tasyā anu visṛjya somarakṣiḥ parṇam achinat tasya yo 'ṃśuḥ parāpatat sa pūtīko 'bhavat tasmin devā ūtim avindann ūtīko vā eṣa yat pūtīkān abhiṣuṇvanty ūtim evāsmai vindanti | [PB, 9, 5 4]
pratidhuk ca prātaḥ pūtīkāś ca śṛtaṃ ca madhyandine pūtīkāś ca dadhi cāparāhṇe pūtīkāś ca | [PB, 9, 5 5]
somapītho vā etasmād apakrāmatīty āhur yasya somam apaharantīti sa oṣadhīś ca paśūṃś ca praviśati tam oṣadhibhyaś ca paśubhyaś cāvarunddhe | [PB, 9, 5 6]
indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasya yo nastaḥ somaḥ samadhāvat tāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni yo vapāyā utkhinnāyās tāni lohitatūlāni yāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni tāny abhiṣuṇuyād etad vai brahmaṇo rūpaṃ sākṣād eva somam abhiṣuṇoti | [PB, 9, 5 7]
śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ sad evainaṃ karoti | [PB, 9, 5 8]
yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi prohed vācaivainaṃ samardhayati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam indriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai | [PB, 9, 5 9]
pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ | [PB, 9, 5 10]
pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhate | [PB, 9, 5 11]
avabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣeta | [PB, 9, 5 12]
tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt | [PB, 9, 5 13]
{PB, 9, 6}
yadi kalaśo dīryeta vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma kuryāt | [PB, 9, 6 1]
avaṣaṭkṛto vā etasya somaḥ parāsicyate yasya kalaśo dīryate yad vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma bhavati vaṣaṭkṛta evāsya somo bhavati | [PB, 9, 6 2]
vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnām ity etāsu kāryam | [PB, 9, 6 3]
eṣa hi bahūnāṃ samane dīryate yat kalaśaḥ | [PB, 9, 6 4]
tad āhur na vā ārtyārtir anūdyārtyā vā eṣa ārtim anuvadati yaḥ kalaśe dīrṇe dadrāṇavatīṣu karotīti | [PB, 9, 6 5]
śrāyantīyam eva kāryam | [PB, 9, 6 6]
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etacchrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇāt prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa | [PB, 9, 6 7]
dugdha iva eṣa riricāno yasya kalaśo dīryate yacchrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa | [PB, 9, 6 8]
yadi śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma syād vaiṣṇavīṣv anuṣṭupsu vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ kuryāt | [PB, 9, 6 9]
yad vai yajñasya sravati vācaṃ pratisravati vāg anuṣṭup yajño viṣṇur vācaiva yajñasya chidram apidadhāti | [PB, 9, 6 10]
