yad vai yajñasya sravaty antataḥ sravati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ yajñasyaiva chidraṃ vārayate | [PB, 9, 6 11]
{PB, 9, 7}
yadi prātassavanāt somo 'tiricyeta asti somo ayaṃ suta iti marutvatīṣu gāyatreṣu stuyuḥ | [PB, 9, 7 1]
mādhyandinaṃ vā eṣa savanaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yaḥ prātassavanād atiricyate tasmān marutvatīṣu stuvanti marutvaddhi mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatraṃ hi prātassavanam | [PB, 9, 7 2]
yasmāt stomād atiricyate sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāya | [PB, 9, 7 3]
aindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati | [PB, 9, 7 4]
vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 9, 7 5]
yadi mādhyandināt savanād atiricyeta baṇ mahāṁ asi sūryety ādityavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ | [PB, 9, 7 6]
tṛtīyasavanaṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo mādhyandināt savanād atiricyate tasmād ādityavatīṣu stuvanty ādityaṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād u bṛhatīṣu bārhataṃ hi mādhyandinaṃ savanam | [PB, 9, 7 7]
yasmāt stomād atiricyeta sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāyaindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 9, 7 8]
yadi tṛtīyasavanād atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ | [PB, 9, 7 9]
yajño vai viṣṇuḥ śipiviṣṭo yajña eva viṣṇau pratitiṣṭhaty atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 9, 7 10]
etad anyat kuryur ukthāni praṇayeyur ukthāni vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo 'gniṣṭomād atiricyate ya ukthyebhyo 'tiricyetātirātraḥ kāryo rātriṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate ya ukthyebhyo 'tiricyate yadi rātrer atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhatā stuyur eṣa tu vā atiricyata ity āhur yo rātrer atiricyata iti | [PB, 9, 7 11]
amuṃ vā eṣa lokaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo rātrer atiricyate bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnoti | [PB, 9, 7 12]
{PB, 9, 8}
yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate dagdhvāsthīny upanahya yo nediṣṭhī syāt taṃ dīkṣayitvā saha yajeran | [PB, 9, 8 1]
etad anyat kuryur abhiṣutyānyat somam agṛhītvā grahān yāsau dakṣiṇā sraktis tad vā stuyur mārjālīye vā | [PB, 9, 8 2]
api vā etasya yajñe yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate tam etena niravadayante | [PB, 9, 8 3]
yāmena stuvanti yamalokam evainaṃ gamayanti | [PB, 9, 8 4]
tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti tṛtīye hi loke pitaraḥ | [PB, 9, 8 5]
parācībhiḥ stuvanti parāṅ hīto 'sau lokaḥ | [PB, 9, 8 6]
sarparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvanti | [PB, 9, 8 7]
arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhis tvacam apaghnate | [PB, 9, 8 8]
tā ṛco 'nubruvantas trir mārjālīyaṃ pariyanti savyān ūrūn āghnānāḥ | [PB, 9, 8 9]
stutam anuśaṃsaty amuṣminn evainaṃ loke nidhunvanti | [PB, 9, 8 10]
yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīty aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇate punaḥ panthānam apiyanti | [PB, 9, 8 11]
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipatkāryā ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhāti | [PB, 9, 8 12]
saṃvatsare 'sthīni yājayeyuḥ saṃvvatsaro vai sarvasya śāntir yat purā saṃvvatsarād yājayeyur vācam aruṣkṛtāṃ krūrām ṛccheyuḥ | [PB, 9, 8 13]
asaṃmitaṃ stotraṃ syād asaṃmito hyasau lokas trivṛtaḥ pavamānāḥ syuḥ saptadaśam itarat sarvam | [PB, 9, 8 14]
yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān evopayanti yat saptadaśam itarat sarvaṃ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evopayanti | [PB, 9, 8 15]
prāṇāpānair vā ete vyṛdhyanta ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīti maitrāvaruṇāgrān grahān gṛhṇate prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānair eva samṛdhyante | [PB, 9, 8 16]
{PB, 9, 9}
yasya kalaśa upadasyati kalaśam evāsyopadasyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ | [PB, 9, 9 1]
tad āhuḥ payo 'vanayed iti | [PB, 9, 9 2]
atho khalv āhur antarhitam iva vā etad yat payo hiraṇyam evāpo 'bhyavanayeddhiraṇyam abhyunnayed iti | [PB, 9, 9 3]
prāṇā vā āpo 'mṛtaṃ hiraṇyam amṛta evāsya prāṇān dadhāti sa sarvam āyur eti | [PB, 9, 9 4]
yasya nārāśaṃsa upavāyati nārāśaṃsam evāsyopavāyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ | [PB, 9, 9 5]
yam adhvaryur antato grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tasyāptum avanayet | [PB, 9, 9 6]
prāyaścittyai vai graho gṛhyate prāyaścittyaivāsmai prāyaścittiṃ karoti | [PB, 9, 9 7]
yadi pītāpītau somau saṃgaccheyātām antaḥparidhyaṅgārān nirvartya juhuyāddhutasya cāhutasya cāhutasya hutasya ca pītāpītasya somasyendrāgnī pibataṃ sutaṃ svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ | [PB, 9, 9 8]
prajāpataye svāhety abhakṣaṇīyasya juhuyād uttarārdhyapūrvārdhya uparavaḥ | [PB, 9, 9 9]
indur indum avāgād ity avavṛṣṭasya bhakṣayet | [PB, 9, 9 10]
tasya ta indav indrapītasyendriyavataḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi | [PB, 9, 9 11]
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra ity ājyenābhyupākṛtasya juhuyād agnīdhraṃ paretya bhūtānāṃ jātaḥ patir eka āsīt sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyām utemāṃ tasmai ta indo haviṣā vidhema svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ | [PB, 9, 9 12]
yadi grāvāpiśīryate paśubhir yajamāno vyṛdhyate paśavo vai grāvāṇo dyutānasya mārutasya sāmnā stuyuḥ | [PB, 9, 9 13]
mārutā vai grāvāṇaḥ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati | [PB, 9, 9 14]
yadi somam abhidahed grahān adhvaryuḥ spāśayeta stotrāṇy udgātā śastrāṇi hotātha yathāpūrvaṃ yajñena careyuḥ pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam ārabhate 'vabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣate tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt purā dvādaśyā dīkṣeta yad dvādaśīm atinayed antardhīyeta | [PB, 9, 9 15]
{PB, 9, 10}
yadi mahāvīro bhidyeta taṃ bhinnam abhimṛśed ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ | [PB, 9, 10 1]
asuryaṃ vā etasmād varṇaṃ kṛtvā teja indriyaṃ vīryam annādyaṃ prajāḥ paśavo 'pakrāmanti yasya yūpo virohati sa īśvaraḥ pāpīyān bhavitoḥ | [PB, 9, 10 2]
tvāṣṭraṃ paśuṃ bahurūpam ālabheta tvaṣṭā vai paśūnāṃ rūpāṇāṃ vikartā tam eva tad upadhāvati sa enaṃ tejasendriyeṇa vīryeṇānnādyena prajayā paśubhiḥ punas samardhayati saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ | [PB, 9, 10 3]
{PB, 10, 1}
agninā pṛthivyauṣadhibhis tenāyaṃ lokas trivṛd vāyunāntarikṣeṇa vayobhis tenaiṣa lokas trivṛd yo 'yam antar ādityena divā nakṣatrais tenāsau lokas trivṛd etad eva trivṛta āyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 1]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 2]
tam u pratiṣṭhetyāhus trivṛddhy evaiṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ | [PB, 10, 1 3]
ardhamāsa eva pañcadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 4]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 5]
taṃ caujo balam ity āhur ardhamāsaśo hi prajāḥ paśava ojo balaṃ puṣyanti | [PB, 10, 1 6]
saṃvatsara eva saptadaśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartava etad eva saptadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 7]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 8]
tam u prajāpatir ity āhuḥ saṃvatsaraṃ hi prajāḥ paśavo 'nuprajāyante | [PB, 10, 1 9]
āditya evaikaviṃśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa etad evaikaviṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 10]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 11]
tam u devatalpa ity āhuḥ pra devatalpam āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 12]
trivṛd eva triṇavasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 13]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 14]
tam u puṣṭir ity āhus trivṛddhy evaiṣa puṣṭaḥ | [PB, 10, 1 15]
devatā eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanaṃ trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśa etad eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 16]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 17]
tam u nāka ity āhur na hi prajāpatiḥ kasmaicanākam | [PB, 10, 1 18]
chandāṃsy eva chandomānām āyatanam eṣaiṣāṃ bandhutā | [PB, 10, 1 19]
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 1 20]
tān u puṣṭir ity āhuḥ paśavo hi chandomāḥ | [PB, 10, 1 21]
{PB, 10, 2}
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so 'tāmyat tasmai vāgjyotir udagṛhṇāt so 'bravīt ko me 'yaṃ jyotir udagṛhṇād iti svaiva te vāg ity abravīt tām abravīd virājaṃ tvā chandasāṃ jyotiḥ kṛtvā yajāntā iti | [PB, 10, 2 1]
tasmād yo virājaṃ stomaṃ sampadyate taṃ jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭoma ity ācakṣate virāḍḍhi chandasāṃ jyotiḥ | [PB, 10, 2 2]
jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 2 3]
anuṣṭup ca vai saptadaśaś ca samabhavatāṃ sānuṣṭup caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsy asṛjata ṣaḍuttarān stomān saptadaśas tāv etān madhyataḥ prājanayatām | [PB, 10, 2 4]
trivṛcca triṇavaś ca rāthantarau tāv ajaś cāśvaś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau rāthantaraṃ prācīnaṃ pradhūnutaḥ | [PB, 10, 2 5]
pañcadaśaś caikaviṃśaś ca bārhatau tau gauś cāviś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau bārhataṃ prācīnaṃ bhāskurutaḥ | [PB, 10, 2 6]
evaṃ vai vidvāṃsam āhur api grāmyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ vāca ājānāti | [PB, 10, 2 7]
{PB, 10, 3}
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa ātmann ṛtvam apaśyat tata ṛtvijo 'sṛjata yad ṛtvād asṛjata tad ṛtvijām ṛtviktvaṃ tair etaṃ dvādaśāham upāsīdat so 'rādhnot | [PB, 10, 3 1]
pitā no 'rātsīd iti māsā upāsīdaṃs te dīkṣayaivārādhnuvann upasatsu trayodaśam adīkṣayan so 'nuvyam abhavat tasmād upasatsu didīkṣāṇo 'nuvyaṃ bhavaty eva ca hi trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ cakṣate naiva ca | [PB, 10, 3 2]
eko dīkṣetaiko hi prajāpatir arādhnod dvādaśa dīkṣeran dvādaśa hi māsā arādhnuvaṃś caturviṃśatir dīkṣeraṃś caturviṃśatir hy ardhamāsā arādhnuvan | [PB, 10, 3 3]
yadi pañcaviṃśo dīkṣeteme pañceme pañceme pañceme pañceme catvāro 'sāv eka iti nirdiśeyur yasmā arāddhikāmāḥ syus tam evārāddhir anveti sarva itare rādhnuvanti | [PB, 10, 3 4]
yo vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiṃ vedāśnute gārhapataṃ pra gārhapatam āpnoti | [PB, 10, 3 5]
saṃvatsaro vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiḥ sa eva prajāpatis tasya māsā eva saha dīkṣiṇaḥ | [PB, 10, 3 6]
vindate saha dīkṣiṇo 'śnute gārhapatyaṃ pra gārhapatyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 3 7]
yo vai chandasāṃ svarājaṃ vedāśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti bṛhatī vāva chandasāṃ svarāḍ aśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 3 8]
tām etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā dvādaśopasado dvādaśa prasutaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśad etā rātrayo bhavanti ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā bṛhatī | [PB, 10, 3 9]
jāyate vāva dīkṣayā punīta upasadbhir devalokam eva sutyayāpyeti | [PB, 10, 3 10]
etāvad vāva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ yad etā rātrayo dvādaśa paurṇamāsyo dvādaśaikāṣṭakā dvādaśāmāvāsyā yāvad eva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ tad etenāptvāvarunddhe dvādaśāhena | [PB, 10, 3 11]
triṃśadakṣarā vā eṣā virāḍ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhaty ṛtubhir virāji | [PB, 10, 3 12]
dvātriṃśadakṣarā vā eṣānuṣṭub vāg anuṣṭup catuṣpādaḥ paśavo vācā paśūn dādhāra tasmād vācā siddhā vācāhūtā āyanti tasmād u nāma jānate | [PB, 10, 3 13]
{PB, 10, 4}
bhūtaṃ pūrvo 'tirātro bhaviṣyad uttaraḥ pṛthivī pūrvo 'tirātro dyaur uttaro 'gniḥ pūrvo 'tirātra āditya uttaraḥ prāṇaḥ pūrvo 'tirātra udāna uttaraḥ | [PB, 10, 4 1]
cakṣuṣī atirātrau kanīnike agniṣṭomau yasmād antarā agniṣṭomāv atirātrābhyāṃ tasmād antare satyau kanīnike bhuṅktaḥ | [PB, 10, 4 2]
saṃvatsarasya vā etau daṃṣṭrau yad atirātrau tayor na svaptavyaṃ saṃvatsarasya daṃṣṭrayor ātmānaṃ ned apidadhānīti | [PB, 10, 4 3]
tad āhuḥ ko 'svaptum arhati yad vāva prāṇo jāgāra tad eva jāgaritam iti | [PB, 10, 4 4]
gāyatrīṃ vā etāṃ jyotiḥpakṣām āsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham aṣṭau madhya ukthā agniṣṭomāv abhito bhāsā svargaṃ lokam etyājarasaṃ brahmādyam annam atti dīpyamānaḥ | [PB, 10, 4 5]
triḥ purastād rathantaraṃ upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ tanvate | [PB, 10, 4 6]
jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat triḥ purastād rathantaram upayantīti saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad ajāmi | [PB, 10, 4 7]
pratnavatyaḥ prāyaṇīyasyāhnaḥ pratipado bhavanti teno eva tad ajāmi | [PB, 10, 4 8]
trir vevopariṣṭād rathantaram upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhād uttiṣṭhanti | [PB, 10, 4 9]
{PB, 10, 5}
trayo vā ete trirātrā yad eṣa dvādaśāho gāyatramukhaḥ prathamo gāyatramadhyo dvitīyo gāyatrottamas tṛtīyaḥ | [PB, 10, 5 1]
yasmād gāyatramukhaḥ prathamas tasmād ūrdhvo 'gnir dīdāya yasmād gāyatramadhyo dvitīyas tasmāt tiryaṅ vāyuḥ pavate yasmād gāyatrottamastṛtīyastasmād arvāṅādityastapati | [PB, 10, 5 2]
tejasā vai gāyatrī prathamaṃ trirātraṃ dādhāra padairdvitīyam akṣaraistṛtīyam | [PB, 10, 5 3]
trivṛdvai gāyatryāstejas trivṛt prāyaṇīyam ahas tena prathamastrirātro dhṛtas tripadā gāyatrī trirātrī madhye tena dvitīyas trirātro dhṛtaś caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī caturviṃśaḥ saptamam ahas tena tṛtīyastrirātro dhṛtaḥ | [PB, 10, 5 4]
tejasā vā ete prayanti tejo madhye dadhati tejo 'bhyudyanti jyotiṣā vā ete prayanti jyotir madhye dadhati jyotir abhyudyanti cakṣuṣā vā ete prayanti cakṣur madhye dadhati cakṣur abhyudyanti prāṇena vā ete prayanti prāṇaṃ madhye dadhati prāṇam abhyudyanti ye gāyatryā prayanti gāyatrīṃ madhye dadhati gāyatrīm abhyudyanti | [PB, 10, 5 5]
tantraṃ vā etad vitāyate yad eṣa dvādaśāhas tasyaite mayūkhā yad gāyatry asaṃvyāthāya | [PB, 10, 5 6]
girikṣidauccāmanyaveti hovācābhipratārī kākṣaseniḥ kathaṃ dvādaśāha iti yathārān nemiḥ paryety evam enaṃ gāyatrī paryeti avisraṃsāya yathārā nābhau dhṛtā evam asyāṃ dvādaśāho dhṛtaḥ | [PB, 10, 5 7]
anuṣṭubhaṃ vā etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham | [PB, 10, 5 8]
aṣṭābhir vā akṣarair anuṣṭup prathamaṃ dvādaśāhasyāhar udyacchaty ekādaśabhir dvitīyaṃ dvādaśabhis tṛtīyam | [PB, 10, 5 9]
akṣaraṃ tryakṣaram ucchiṣyate tad evottaraṃ trirātram anuvidadhāti | [PB, 10, 5 10]
chandāṃsy evāsyās tṛtīyaṃ trirātraṃ vahanti | [PB, 10, 5 11]
tāṃ vā etāṃ pratīcīṃ tiraścīṃ parācīm āsate 'nnādyāya tasmāt pratyañcaṃ tiryañcaṃ parāñcaṃ prajāḥ paśum upajīvanti | [PB, 10, 5 12]
chandāṃsi vā anyonyasya lokam abhyadhyāyan gāyatrī triṣṭubhas triṣṭub jagatyā jagatī gāyatryās tāni vyauhan yathālokaṃ tato vai tāni yaṃ yaṃ kāmam akāmayanta tam asanvan | [PB, 10, 5 13]
yatkāmo vyūḍhacchandasā dvādaśāhena yajate so 'smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate | [PB, 10, 5 14]
oko vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho yatho vai manuṣyā imaṃ lokam āviṣṭā evaṃ devatā dvādaśāham āviṣṭā devatā ha vā etena yajate ya evaṃ vidvān dvādaśāhena yajate | [PB, 10, 5 15]
gṛhā vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho nāgṛhatāyā bhayyam | [PB, 10, 5 16]
yo vai dvādaśāham agniṣṭomena kalpamānaṃ veda kalpate 'smai prātaḥsavanenaiva prathamas trirātraḥ kalpate mādhyandinena dvitīyas tṛtīyasavanena tṛtīyo 'gniṣṭomasāmnaiva daśamam ahaḥ kalpate | [PB, 10, 5 17]
kalpate 'smai ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 5 18]
{PB, 10, 6}
eti prety āśumad vītimad rukmat tejasvad yuñjānaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ trivṛtaḥ stomasya gāyatrasya chandaso rathantarasya sāmnaḥ | [PB, 10, 6 1]
vṛṣavad vṛtravad rayimad viśvavad upasthitaṃ dvitīyasyāhno rūpaṃ pañcadaśasya stomasya traiṣṭubhasya chandaso bṛhataḥ sāmnaḥ | [PB, 10, 6 2]
udvat trivad digvat gomad ṛṣabhavat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ saptadaśasya stomasya jāgatasya chandaso vairūpasya sāmnaḥ | [PB, 10, 6 3]
rājanvaj janavadvat sūryavad virāḍanutodavac caturthasyāhno rūpam ekaviṃśasya stomasyānuṣṭubhasya chandaso vairājasya sāmnaḥ | [PB, 10, 6 4]
citravacchiśumat paṅktiḥ śakvarī vyūnākṣarā gomad ṛṣabhavad vajryabhimat pañcamasyāhno rūpaṃ triṇavasya stomasya pāṅktasya chandasaḥ śakvarīṇāṃ sāmnaḥ | [PB, 10, 6 5]
parivat prativat saptapadā dvipadā vinārāśaṃsā gomad ṛṣabhavat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ trayastriṃśasya stomasya sarveṣāṃ chandasāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ sāmnaḥ | [PB, 10, 6 6]
yasmād eṣā samānā satī ṣaḍahavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād virūpaḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ | [PB, 10, 6 7]
virūpam enam anuprajāyate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 6 8]
{PB, 10, 7}
agna iti prathamasyāhno rūpam agnivibhakter agnim iti dvitīyasyāgnineti tṛtīyasyāgnir iti caturthasya | [PB, 10, 7 1]
devā vai śriyam aicchaṃs tāṃ na prathame 'hany avindan na dvitīye na tṛtīye tāṃ caturthe 'hany avindan vindate śriyaṃ ya evaṃ vedāgner iti pañcamasya teno śrīḥ pratyupoditety āhuḥ | [PB, 10, 7 2]
aprativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 10, 7 3]
agna iti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti | [PB, 10, 7 4]
yasmād eṣā samānā saty agnivibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartvādityas tapati | [PB, 10, 7 5]
{PB, 10, 8}
indreti prathamasyāhno rūpam indravibhakter indram iti dvitīyasyendreṇeti tṛtīyasyendra iti caturthasyendrād iti pañcamasyendreti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti yasmād eṣā samānā satīndravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv oṣadhayaḥ pacyante | [PB, 10, 8 1.1]
{PB, 10, 9}
yad ṛcā prastauti tat prathamasyāhno rūpam svaravibhakter yat purastāt stobhaṃ tad dvitīyasya yad ubhayataḥ stobhaṃ tat tṛtīyasya yad anutunnaṃ tac caturthasya yad abhyārabdhaṃ tat pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 10, 9 1]
svarāṇāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī svaravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartu vāyuḥ pavate | [PB, 10, 9 2]
{PB, 10, 10}
padanidhanaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam nidhanavibhakter bahirṇidhanaṃ dvitīyasya diṅnidhanaṃ tṛtīyasyenidhanaṃ caturthasyāthakāraṇidhanaṃ pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī nidhanavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād ime lokāḥ saha santo nānaiva | [PB, 10, 10 1.1]
{PB, 10, 11}
dravadiḍaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam iḍāvibhakter ūrdhveḍaṃ dvitīyasya pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tṛtīyasyeḍābhir aiḍaṃ caturthasyādhyardheḍaṃ pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam iḍānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satīḍāvibhaktir nānārūpā tasmāt samānāḥ santaḥ paśavo nānārūpāḥ | [PB, 10, 11 1.1]
{PB, 10, 12}
bharadvājāyanā vai sattram āsata tān apṛcchan kiṃ prathamenāhnā kuruteti praivaimeti kiṃ dvitīyenety avasam evākurmahīti kiṃ tṛtīyeneti pary evāplavāmahīti kiṃ caturtheneti sataiva sad apyadadhmeti kiṃ pañcameneti prāṇān eva vicchindanta aimeti kiṃ ṣaṣṭhenetīdam evāgacchāmeti | [PB, 10, 12 1]
yasya padena prastauty atha svāram abhi vāva tena devāḥ paśūn apaśyan yat purastāt stobhaṃ atha svāram ud eva tenāsṛjanta yad ubhayataḥ stobham atha svāram ebhya eva tena lokebhyo devāḥ paśubhyo 'nnādyaṃ prāyacchan yad anutunnam atha svāram upaiva tenāśikṣan yasya madhye nidhanam atha svāraṃ garbhāṃs tenādadhata tān ihavatā svāreṇa prājanayan | [PB, 10, 12 2]
imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ padanidhanenābhyajayann amuṃ bahirṇidhanenāntarikṣaṃ diṅnidhanenāmṛtatvam īnidhanenāgacchan brahmavarcasam athanidhanenāvārundhatāsminn eva loka ihanidhanena pratyatiṣṭhan | [PB, 10, 12 3]
imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ dravadiḍenābhyajayann amum ūrdhveḍenāntarikṣaṃ pariṣṭubdheḍena pratiṣṭhām iḍābhir aiḍenāvārundhata pratiṣṭhāyādhyardheḍena vyajayantāsminn eva loka iheḍena pratyatiṣṭhan | [PB, 10, 12 4]
na vāk saṃvatsaram ativadatīḍaiva saṃvatsaram ativadati garbheṇa saṃvatsare paryāvṛtya prajāyate tenātivadati | [PB, 10, 12 5]
tā vā etāś catasraḥ ṣaḍahaṃ parācya iḍā atiyanty eṣānunūtaiṣā viṣūcy eṣā pratīcy etad dvīḍam | [PB, 10, 12 6]
saṃvatsaro 'gnir vāk saṃvatsaro yad agnir vibhajyate vācam eva tad vibhajanti | [PB, 10, 12 7]
dve dve akṣare vibhajanti dvau dvau hi māsāv ṛtur atho māsānām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate | [PB, 10, 12 8]
ṣaḍ ahāni vibhajanti ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyā ṛtūnāṃ pratiṣṭhityā atho ṛtūnām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate ṣaḍ u puruṣā yān agnir anuvihriyate | [PB, 10, 12 9]
yad idaṃ bahudhāgnir vihriyate tad asāv ādityaḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratyaṅ tasmād ete devate vibhaktim ānaśāte nāto 'nyā kācana | [PB, 10, 12 10]
{PB, 11, 1}
stomo yujyate sattriyebhyo 'harbhyaḥ pratnavatībhiś copavatībhiś ca | [PB, 11, 1 1]
yat pratnavatyo upavatībhyaḥ pūrvā yujyante brahma tat pūrvaṃ kṣatrād yujyate brahma hi pūrvaṃ kṣatrāt | [PB, 11, 1 2]
manas tat pūrvaṃ vāco yujyate mano hi pūrvaṃ vāco yaddhi manasābhigacchati tad vācā vadati | [PB, 11, 1 3]
bṛhat tat pūrvaṃ rathantarād yujyate bṛhaddhi pūrvaṃ rathantarād vijityā tu vai rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe | [PB, 11, 1 4]
saṃbhāryās tṛcā bhavanti yathāśiṣṭhān vahiṣṭhān saṃbhared evam evaitān saṃbharanti gatyai | [PB, 11, 1 5]
nava bhavanti navāhasya yuktyā ṛcarcaivāhar yunakti yathā prārthasya śamyā avadadhyād evam evaitan navāhasya śamyā avadadhāti gatyai | [PB, 11, 1 6]
trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya | [PB, 11, 1 7.1]
{PB, 11, 2}
ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu | [PB, 11, 2 1]
nirāhāvanty ājyāni bhavanti yuktam eva tair āhvayati | [PB, 11, 2 2]
agna āyāhi vītaya ā no mitrāvaruṇāyāhi suṣamā hi ta indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ iti | [PB, 11, 2 3]
{PB, 11, 3}
pra somāso vipaścita iti gāyatrī bhavati pretyā abhi droṇāni babhrava ity abhikrāntyai sutā indrāya vāyava iti saṃskṛtyai pra soma deva vītaya iti pretyai pra tu draveti pretyai pra vā etenāhnā yanti | [PB, 11, 3 1]
gāyatraṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 3 2]
yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 11, 3 3]
āśvaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 3 4]
aśvo vai bhūtvā prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa prājāyata bahur abhavat prajāyate bahur bhavaty āśvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 3 5]
ekākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti rathantarasyānativādāya | [PB, 11, 3 6]
anativādyenaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 11, 3 7]
somasāma bhavati | [PB, 11, 3 8]
yathā vā imā anyā oṣadhayaḥ evaṃ soma āsīt sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat somasāmāpaśyat tena rājyamādhipatyam agacchad yaśo 'bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavati somasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 3 9]
yaudhājayaṃ bhavati yad eva yaudhājayasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 11, 3 10]
auśanaṃ yad auśanasya stomaḥ | [PB, 11, 3 11]
{PB, 11, 4}
abhi tvā śūra nonuma ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 4 1]
kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai | [PB, 11, 4 2]
taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣahaṃ vasor mandānam andhaso 'bhivatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 4 3]
indraṃ gīrbhir havāmaha iti havanta evainam | [PB, 11, 4 4]
tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam eva tad yunakti | [PB, 11, 4 5]
rathantaraṃ bhavati brahma vai rathantaraṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramya prayanti | [PB, 11, 4 6]
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate | [PB, 11, 4 7]
vāmadevyaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate | [PB, 11, 4 8]
naudhasaṃ bhavati brahma vai naudhasaṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramante | [PB, 11, 4 9]
kāleyaṃ bhavati samānaloke vai kāleyaṃ ca rathantaraṃ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāṃ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate | [PB, 11, 4 10]
dravadiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ | [PB, 11, 4 11]
{PB, 11, 5}
pra somāso madacyuta iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāty ayā pavasva devayur ity eti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ pavate 'har yato harir iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bṛhad eva tad etasminn ahani yunakti tad yuktaṃ śva ārabhante pra sunvānāyāndhasa iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṇyam iva hy etad ahar abhi priyāṇi pavate canohita ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 5 1]
yajñā yajñā vo agnaya ity agnir vai yajño yajña eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 11, 5 2]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 11, 5 3]
saṃhitaṃ bhavati vyakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaiva sattram āsate | [PB, 11, 5 4]
saphaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 5 5]
saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvan yat samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpya sattram āsate | [PB, 11, 5 6]
ākṣāraṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 5 7]
aṣṭau vā etāḥ kāmadughā āsaṃs tāsām ekā samaśīryata sā kṛṣir abhavad ṛdhyate 'smai kṛṣau ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 11, 5 8]
tāsu devāsurā aspardhanta te devā asurān kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇānudanta nudate bhrātṛvyaṃ kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 5 9]
ebhyo vai lokebhyo raso 'pākrāmat taṃ prajāpatir ākṣāreṇākṣārayad yad ākṣārayat tad ākṣārasyākṣāratvam | [PB, 11, 5 10]
tasmād yaḥ purā puṇyo bhūtvā paścāt pāpīyān syād ākṣāraṃ brahmasāma kurvītātmany eved indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam ākṣārayati | [PB, 11, 5 11]
januṣaikarcau bhavato 'hno dhṛtyai yad vā etasyāhno 'dhṛtaṃ tad etābhyāṃ dādhāra | [PB, 11, 5 12]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 5 13]
gaurīvitir vā etacchāktyo brāhmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavat | [PB, 11, 5 14]
atiriktaṃ vā etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitenāhīnāñchvastanavad bhavaty api prajāyā upakﾱptam | [PB, 11, 5 15]
vṛṣā vā etad vājisāma vṛṣabho retodhā adya stuvanti śvaḥ prajāyate | [PB, 11, 5 16]
anuṣṭubhi chandasāṃ kriyate 'nuṣṭubbhi chandasāṃ yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau reto dhatte prajātyai | [PB, 11, 5 17]
prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 11, 5 18]
dvyudāsaṃ bhavaty etau vā udāsau svargasya lokasyāvasānadarśau pūrveṇa pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti | [PB, 11, 5 19]
tad yathādaḥ pūrvedyuḥ spaṣṭaṃ tṛṇodakam anvavasyanto yanty evam eva tābhyāṃ svargaṃ lokam anvavasyanto yanti | [PB, 11, 5 20]
gautamaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 5 21]
sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 5 22]
yad u caivānuṣṭubhasya madhye nidhanasya brāhmaṇaṃ tad u caitasya | [PB, 11, 5 23]
kāvaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 5 24]
lokavindu sāma vindate lokaṃ kāvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 5 25]
svāram u svareṇa svareṇa hi devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati | [PB, 11, 5 26]
yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 5 27]
vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāci yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhito vācy eva tad yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti taṃ vāco 'dhi śva ārabhante | [PB, 11, 5 28]
trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya | [PB, 11, 5 29]
{PB, 11, 6}
pavasva vāco agriya iti dvitīyasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 11, 6 1]
pavasveti rāthantaraṃ rūpam agriya iti bārhatam ubhe rūpe samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāya | [PB, 11, 6 2]
pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta ity anurūpo bhavati vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 11, 6 3]
pūrvam u tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam | [PB, 11, 6 4]
anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 11, 6 5]
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 11, 6 6]
vṛṣaṇvantas tṛcā bhavatīndriyasya vīryasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 11, 6 7]
tṛca uttamo bhavati | [PB, 11, 6 8]
yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 11, 6 9]
pañcadaśa eva stomo bhavati | [PB, 11, 6 10]
ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhati ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ | [PB, 11, 6 11]
{PB, 11, 7}
ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu | [PB, 11, 7 1]
nirāhopasthitāny ājyāni bhavanti | [PB, 11, 7 2]
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha indram id gāthino bṛhad indre agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ | [PB, 11, 7 3]
{PB, 11, 8}
vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai | [PB, 11, 8 1]
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 8 2]
punānas soma dhārayeti dhṛtyai | [PB, 11, 8 3]
vṛṣā śoṇo abhikanikradad gā iti | [PB, 11, 8 4]
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa samṛddhā vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 11, 8 5]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 11, 8 6]
yauktāśvaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 8 7]
yuktāśvo vā āṅgirasaḥ śiśū jātau viparyaharat tasmān mantro 'pākrāmat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad yauktāśvam apaśyat taṃ mantra upāvartata tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma yauktāśvaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 11, 8 8]
āyāsye bhavataḥ | [PB, 11, 8 9]
ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annādyam āśnāt taṃ śug ārchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa ete āyāsye apaśyat tābhyāṃ śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hata āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 8 10]
ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tām ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayati vṛṣṭim āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 8 11]
annādyaṃ vāva tad ebhyo lokebhyo 'pākrāmat tad ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayaty annādyam āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 8 12]
vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 8 13]
vasiṣṭho vā etena vaiḍavaḥ stutvāñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ | [PB, 11, 8 14]
{PB, 11, 9}
tvām iddhi havāmaha iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 9 1]
abhipravaḥ surādhasam iti yuñjate vai pūrveṇāhnā hy etena prayanti | [PB, 11, 9 2]
tvām idā hyo nara ity adya caiva hyaś ca samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāya | [PB, 11, 9 3]
bṛhad bhavati varṣma vai bṛhad varṣma dvitīyam ahar varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmākramante | [PB, 11, 9 4]
śyaitaṃ bhavati sāmnorvāho yajñasya santatyai | [PB, 11, 9 5]
mādhucchandasaṃ bhavati sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 9 6]
ūrdhveḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ | [PB, 11, 9 7]
{PB, 11, 10}
yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavati | [PB, 11, 10 1]
madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 11, 10 2]
pavasva madhumattama iti pavanta iva hy etenāhnā madhumattama ity annaṃ vai madhv annādyam eva tad yajamāne dadhāti | [PB, 11, 10 3]
indram accha sutā ima itīndriyasya vīryasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 11, 10 4]
ayaṃ pūṣā rayir bhaga ity anuṣṭubhaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 10 5]
vṛṣāmatīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇa iti jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 11, 10 6]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 11, 10 7]
hāviṣmataṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 10 8]
haviṣmāṃś ca vai haviṣkṛccāṅgirasāvāstāṃ dvitīye 'hani haviṣmān arādhnon navame 'hani haviṣkṛt | [PB, 11, 10 9]
ayaṃ haviṣmān ity eva jātam ahar jātaṃ somaṃ prāha devebhyaḥ sāmnaivāsmā āśiṣam āśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ | [PB, 11, 10 10]
śaṅku bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai yad vā adhṛtaṃ śaṅkunā tad dādhāra | [PB, 11, 10 11]
tad u sīdantīyam ity āhur etena vai prajāpatir ūrdhva imān lokān asīdad yad asīdat tat sīdantīyasya sīdantīyatvam ūrdhva imān lokān sīdati sīdantīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 10 12]
sujñānaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 10 13]
svarvad vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ svarṇidhanaṃ bārhatam | [PB, 11, 10 14]
svarṇidhanaṃ bhavati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 11, 10 15]
plavau vā etāv upohante svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [PB, 11, 10 16]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 11, 10 17]
krauñcaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 10 18]
vāg vai krauñcaṃ vāg dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai | [PB, 11, 10 19]
yāmaṃ bhavati | [PB, 11, 10 20]
etena vai yamo 'napajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam āśnutānapajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam aśnute yāmena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 11, 10 21]
etena vai yamī yamaṃ svargaṃ lokam agamayat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ | [PB, 11, 10 22]
{PB, 11, 11}
ehy ū ṣu bravāṇi ta ity ehivatyo bhavanti tṛtīyasyāhna upahavāya santatyai | [PB, 11, 11 1]
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāya | [PB, 11, 11 2]
evā hy asi vīrayur iti samānaṃ vadantīdam ittham asad iti | [PB, 11, 11 3]
indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitayā vardhanti | [PB, 11, 11 4]
sākamaśvaṃ bhavaty ukthānām abhijityā abhikrāntyai | [PB, 11, 11 5]
etena hy agra ukthāny adhyajayann etenābhyakrāman | [PB, 11, 11 6]
āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kﾱptiś cānnādyaṃ ca samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyata idam ittham asad iti | [PB, 11, 11 7]
kṣatraṃ vā etad ahar abhinirvadati yat pañcadaśaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāma bhavati brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca sayujī karoti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhati brahmaṇe kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti | [PB, 11, 11 8]
brahma vai pūrvam ahaḥ kṣatraṃ dvitīyaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāma bhavati brahma tad yaśasārdhayati brahma hi gāyatrī | [PB, 11, 11 9]
tad u samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyate samṛddhyai | [PB, 11, 11 10]
āṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavataḥ | [PB, 11, 11 11]
aiyāhā iti vā indro vṛtram ahann aiyādohoveti nyagṛhṇād vārtraghne sāmanī vīryavatī | [PB, 11, 11 12]
ojo evaitābhyāṃ vīryam avarunddhe | [PB, 11, 11 13]
pañcadaśa eva stomo bhavaty ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ | [PB, 11, 11 14]
{PB, 12, 1}
davidyutatyā ruceti tṛtīyasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 12, 1 1]
davidyutatī vai gāyatrī pariṣṭobhantī triṣṭub gavāśīr jagatī trīṇi rūpāṇi samārabhate trirātrasyāvisraṃsāya | [PB, 12, 1 2]
ete asṛgram indava ity anurūpo bhavati | [PB, 12, 1 3]
eta iti vai prajāpatir devān asṛjatāsṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pitṝṃs tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 12, 1 4]
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 1 5]
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 1 6]
rājā medhābhir īyate pavamāno manāv adhy antarikṣeṇa yātava iti | [PB, 12, 1 7]
antarikṣadevatyas tṛco bhavaty antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 12, 1 8]
pañcarco bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 1 9]
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyupayanti | [PB, 12, 1 10]
saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai | [PB, 12, 1 11]
{PB, 12, 2}
agnināgniḥ samidhyata ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 2 1]
pūrve eva tad ahanī samiddhe tṛtīyam ahar abhisaminddhe | [PB, 12, 2 2]
mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam iti rāthantaram maitrāvaruṇam | [PB, 12, 2 3]
huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpam | [PB, 12, 2 4]
rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati | [PB, 12, 2 5]
indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣusa ity aindram | [PB, 12, 2 6]
sam iva vā ime lokā dadṛśire 'ntarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 12, 2 7]
tā huve yayor idam iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam | [PB, 12, 2 8]
huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 2 9]
{PB, 12, 3}
uccā te jātam andhasa iti gāyatrī bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 1]
udvad vā etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 12, 3 2]
andhasvatī bhavaty ahar vā andho 'hna ārambhaḥ | [PB, 12, 3 3]
abhi somāsa āyava iti | [PB, 12, 3 4]
abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaityubhau hi varṇāvetad ahaḥ | [PB, 12, 3 5]
tisro vāca īrayati pravahnir iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante | [PB, 12, 3 6]
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hyetad ahaḥ | [PB, 12, 3 7]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 3 8]
vaiṣṭambhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 9]
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā vaiṣṭambhair vyaṣṭabhnuvaṃs tad vaiṣṭambhasya vaiṣṭambhatvam | [PB, 12, 3 10]
diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 3 11]
paurūmadgaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 12]
ahar vā etad avlīyamānaṃ tad rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tasmād devāḥ paurūmadgena rakṣāṃsyapāghnann apa pāpmānaṃ hate paurūmadgena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 3 13]
devāś ca vāsurāś cāspardhanta te devā asurāṇāṃ paurūmadgena puro 'majjayan yat puro 'majjayaṃstasmāt paurūmadgaṃ pāpmānam evaitena bhrātṛvyaṃ majjayati | [PB, 12, 3 14]
gautamaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 15]
yad eva gautamasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 3 16]
ubhayataḥstobhaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 12, 3 17]
antarikṣaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 18]
antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyam antarikṣa eva tad antarikṣeṇa stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 12, 3 19]
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 20]
as iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ has iti bārhataṃ tṛtīyam eva tad rūpam upayanti samṛddhyai | [PB, 12, 3 21]
aṅgirasāṃ saṃkrośo bhavati | [PB, 12, 3 22]
etena vā aṅgirasaḥ saṃkrośamānāḥ svargaṃ lokam āpan svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 3 23]
{PB, 12, 4}
yaddyāva indra te śatam iti śatavatyo bhavanti | [PB, 12, 4 1]
śatavad vai paśūnāṃ rūpaṃ sahasravat paśūnām evaitābhī rūpam avarunddhe | [PB, 12, 4 2]
vayaṃ gha tvā sutāvanta iti satobṛhatyo varṣīyaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya | [PB, 12, 4 3]
taraṇir it siṣāsati vājaṃ purandhyā yujā ā va indraṃ puruhūtaṃ name girety āvad akṣaram uddhatam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad etad āvadakṣaraṃ bhavaty ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 12, 4 4]
pañcanidhanaṃ vairūpaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati diśāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 4 5]
pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 4 6]
diśāṃ vā etat sāma yad vairūpaṃ diśo hy evaitenābhivadati | [PB, 12, 4 7]
atha yat pañcanidhanaṃ tenartūnāṃ pañca hy ṛtavaḥ | [PB, 12, 4 8]
ṛtubhiś ca vā ime lokā digbhiś cāvṛtās teṣv evobhayeṣu yajamānaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yajamānaṃ vā anupratitiṣṭhantam udgātā pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ vidvān vairūpeṇodgāyati | [PB, 12, 4 9]
digvad bhavati bhrātṛvyasyāpanuttyai | [PB, 12, 4 10]
diśaṃ viśam iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 4 11]
has ity upariṣṭād diśāṃ nidhanam upayanti tena bārhatam | [PB, 12, 4 12]
rāthantaro vā ayaṃ loko bārhato 'sāv ubhe eva tad bṛhadrathantarayo rūpeṇāparādhnoti | [PB, 12, 4 13]
anaḍvāhau vā etau devayānau yajamānasya yad bṛhadrathantare tāv eva tad yunakti svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [PB, 12, 4 14]
aśvavad bhavati prajātyai | [PB, 12, 4 15]
yathā maṇḍūka āṭ karoty evaṃ nidhanam upayanty ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 12, 4 16]
dvādaśa vairūpāṇi bhavanti dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 12, 4 17]
virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 4 18]
mahāvaiṣṭambhaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 4 19]
yadā vai puruṣo 'nnam atty athāntarato viṣṭabdhaḥ | [PB, 12, 4 20]
diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 4 21]
satobṛhatīṣu stuvanti pūrvayor ahnoḥ pratyudyamāya | [PB, 12, 4 22]
rauravam acchāvākasāma bhavati | [PB, 12, 4 23]
agnir vai rūro rudro 'gniḥ | [PB, 12, 4 24]
agnir vā etasya paśūn apakramayati yasya paśavo 'pakrāmanty agnir eva tasya paśūn abhikramayati yasya paśavo 'bhikrāmanti | [PB, 12, 4 25]
abhy abhy evāsya paśavaḥ krāmanti ya evaṃ vidvān rauraveṇa stuvate | [PB, 12, 4 26]
pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 4 27]
{PB, 12, 5}
tisro vāca udīrata iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante | [PB, 12, 5 1]
udvad vā etat trivad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 12, 5 2]
ā sotā pariṣiñcateti parivatyo bhavanti | [PB, 12, 5 3]
anto vai tṛtīyam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai | [PB, 12, 5 4]
sakhāya āniṣīdatety uddhatam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad āha niṣīdatety ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 12, 5 5]
sutāso madhumattamā ity anuṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 12, 5 6]
pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspata iti | [PB, 12, 5 7]
vitatam iva vā idam antarikṣam antareme antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 12, 5 8]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 5 9]
pāṣṭhauhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 5 10]
paṣṭhavāḍvā etenāṅgirasaś caturthasyāhno vācaṃ vadantīm upāśṛṇot sa ho vāg iti nidhanam upait tad asyābhyuditaṃ tad ahar avasat | [PB, 12, 5 11]
vācaḥ sāma bhavati | [PB, 12, 5 12]
vāg vai dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai | [PB, 12, 5 13]
niṣkirīyāḥ sattram āsata te tṛtīyam ahar na prājānaṃs tān etat sāma gāyamānān vāg upāplavat tena tṛtīyam ahaḥ prājānaṃs te 'bruvann iyaṃ vāva nas tṛtīyam ahar adīdṛśad iti tṛtīyasyaivaiṣāhno dṛṣṭiḥ | [PB, 12, 5 14]
śauktaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 5 15]
śuktir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 5 16]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 5 17]
tvāṣṭrīsāma bhavati | [PB, 12, 5 18]
indraṃ vā akṣyāmayiṇaṃ bhūtāni nāsvāpayaṃs tam etena tvāṣṭryo 'svāpayaṃs tad vāva tās tarhy akāmayanta | [PB, 12, 5 19]
kāmasani sāma tvāṣṭrīsāma kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 12, 5 20]
indro vṛtrād bibhyad gāṃ prāviśat taṃ tvāṣṭryo 'bruvañ janayāmeti tam etaiḥ sāmabhir ajanayañ jāyāmahā iti vai sattram āsate jāyanta eva | [PB, 12, 5 21]
ariṣṭaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 5 22]
devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta yaṃ devānām aghnan na sa samabhavad yam asurāṇāṃ saṃ so 'bhavat te devās tapo 'tapyanta ta etad ariṣṭam apaśyaṃs tato yaṃ devānām aghnat saṃ so 'bhavad yam asurāṇāṃ na sa samabhavad anenāriṣāmeti tad ariṣṭasyāriṣṭatvam ariṣṭyā evāriṣṭam antataḥ kriyate | [PB, 12, 5 23]
trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 5 24]
dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti caturthasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 5 25]
{PB, 12, 6}
pra maṃhiṣṭhāya gāyateti | [PB, 12, 6 1]
yad gāyateti mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate | [PB, 12, 6 2]
taṃ te madaṃ gṛṇīmasīti madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 12, 6 3]
śrudhī havaṃ tiraścyā iti śrutyā eva | [PB, 12, 6 4]
pramaṃhiṣṭhīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 6 5]
pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāvartayat tam astṛṇuta bhrātṛvyavān pramaṃhiṣṭhīyenokthāni praṇayeta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyaṃ vasīyān ātmanā bhavati | [PB, 12, 6 6]
hārivarṇaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 6 7]
indraś ca vai namuciś cāsuraḥ samadadhātāṃ na no naktaṃ na divā hanan nārdreṇa na śuṣkeṇeti tasya vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditye 'pāṃ phenena śiro 'chinad etad vai na naktaṃ na divā yat vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditya etan nārdraṃ na śuṣkaṃ yad apāṃ phenas tad enaṃ pāpīyaṃ vācaṃ vadad anvavartata vīrahannadruho 'druha iti tan narcā na sāmnāpahantum aśaknot | [PB, 12, 6 8]
hārivarṇasyaiva nidhanenāpāhata | [PB, 12, 6 9]
apa śucaṃ hate hārivarṇasya nidhanena śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 6 10]
tairaścyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 6 11]
aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yanto rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena tiraścyāṅgirasas tiryaṅ paryavaid yat tiryaṅ paryavait tasmāt tairaścyaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ tairaścyenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate tairaścyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 6 12]
saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai | [PB, 12, 6 13]
{PB, 12, 7}
pra ta āśvinīḥ pavamāna dhenava iti caturthasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 12, 7 1]
āpte trirātre gāyatryā rūpeṇa prayanti prati vai gāyatryā rūpam | [PB, 12, 7 2]
jagatī pratipad bhavati jāgatam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ jagatyā eva taj jagatīm abhisaṃkrāmanti | [PB, 12, 7 3]
yad ato 'nyā pratipatsyāt pratikūlaṃ vānukūlaṃ vā syāt | [PB, 12, 7 4]
pavamāno ajījanad ity anurūpo bhavati | [PB, 12, 7 5]
janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati | [PB, 12, 7 6]
pūrvam u caiva tadrūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 7 7]
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 7 8]
ṣaḍṛcau bhavata ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 7 9]
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanty ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 12, 7 10]
{PB, 12, 8}
janasya gopā ajaniṣṭa jāgṛviḥ ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 8 1]
janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati | [PB, 12, 8 2]
ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā iti bārhataṃ maitrāvaruṇam | [PB, 12, 8 3]
bṛhad etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati | [PB, 12, 8 4]
indro dadhīco asthibhir iti dādhīcas tṛco bhavati | [PB, 12, 8 5]
dadhyaṅ vā āṅgiraso devānāṃ purodhānīya āsīd annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhā annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 8 6]
iyaṃ vām asya manmana ity aindrāgnam | [PB, 12, 8 7]
indrāgnī pūrvyastutir abhrād vṛṣṭir ivājanīty ānuṣṭubhī vai vṛṣṭir ānuṣṭubham etad ahar yac caturthaṃ samīcyau virājau dadhāty annādyāya stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 8 8]
{PB, 12, 9}
pavasva dakṣasādhana iti gāyatrī bhavati siddhyai | [PB, 12, 9 1]
yat pavasveti tad bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 12, 9 2]
tavāhaṃ soma rarāṇa sakhya indo dive dive purūṇi babhro ni caranti māmava paridhīṃr ati tāṁ ihīti | [PB, 12, 9 3]
ati hy āyañchakunā iva paptimety ati hy apatat | [PB, 12, 9 4]
punāno akramīd abhīti | [PB, 12, 9 5]
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 12, 9 6]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 9 7]
caturṇidhanam ātharvaṇaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 9 8]
catuṣpadānuṣṭub ānuṣṭubham etad ahar yaccaturtham | [PB, 12, 9 9]
bheṣajaṃ vā ātharvaṇāni bheṣajam eva tat karoti | [PB, 12, 9 10]
nidhanakāmaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 9 11]
ekaṃ vā anyena niruktena nidhanena kāmaṃ sanoty athaitan nidhanakāmaṃ sarveṣāṃ kāmānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 9 12]
āṣṭādaṃṣṭraṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 9 13]
yad evāṣṭādaṃṣṭrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 9 14]
ābhīśavaṃ bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 9 15]
yad vā adhṛtam abhīśunā tad dādhāra | [PB, 12, 9 16]
anutunnaṃ gāyati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 12, 9 17]
caturṇidhanam āṅgirasaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai | [PB, 12, 9 18]
svaḥpṛṣṭhaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 12, 9 19]
sattrāsāhīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 9 20]
yad vā asurāṇām asoḍham āsīt tad devāḥ sattrāsāhīyenāsahanta satrainān asakṣmahīti tat sattrāsāhīyasya sattrāsāhīyatvam | [PB, 12, 9 21]
satrā bhrātṛvyaṃ sahate sattrāsāhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 9 22]
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 12, 9 23]
vṛṣaṇvatyo gāyatrayo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 9 24.1]
{PB, 12, 10}
pibā somam indra mandatu tvā yaṃ te suṣāva haryaśvādriḥ sotur bāhubhyāṃ suyato 'nārvety āyatam iva vai caturtham ahas tasyaiva yatyai | [PB, 12, 10 1]
viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhibhūtaraṃ nara ity atijagatī varṣīyaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya | [PB, 12, 10 2]
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yajjyāyasaś chandasaḥ kanīyaś chanda upaiti yad eṣā caturthe 'hany atijagatī kriyate 'napabhraṃśāya | [PB, 12, 10 3]
yo rājā carṣaṇīnām iti | [PB, 12, 10 4]
rājye hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan rājyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti | [PB, 12, 10 5]
chandobhir vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ vairājasya nidhanenādṛṃhaṃs tasmāt parāṅ cārvāṅ cādityas tapati parāṅ cārvāṅ cekāraḥ | [PB, 12, 10 6]
prastāvaṃ prastutya viṣṭambhān viṣṭabhnoti mukhata eva tad annādyaṃ dhatte mukhaṃ hi sāmnaḥ prastāvaḥ | [PB, 12, 10 7]
daśakṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 10 8]
triṃśatkṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti bhūyaso 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 10 9]
vairājaṃ sāma bhavati virāṭsu stuvanti vairājā viṣṭambhāḥ samīcīr virājo dadhāty annādyāya | [PB, 12, 10 10]
anutunnaṃ gāyati retodheyāyānutunnāddhi reto dhīyate | [PB, 12, 10 11]
dakṣiṇa ūrāv udgātur agniṃ manthanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate | [PB, 12, 10 12]
upākṛte 'hiṅkṛte manthanti jātam abhihiṅkaroti | [PB, 12, 10 13]
tasmājjātaṃ putraṃ paśavo 'bhihiṅkurvanti | [PB, 12, 10 14]
tasmai jātāyāmīmāṃsanta gārhapatye praharāmā3 āgnīdhrā3 āhavanīyā3 iti | [PB, 12, 10 15]
āhavanīye praharanty etadāyatano vai yajamāno yadāhavanīye svam eva tad āyatanaṃ jyotiṣmat karoti | [PB, 12, 10 16]
jyotiṣmān brahmavarcasī bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 10 17]
abhijuhoti śāntyā ājyenābhijuhoti tejo vā ājyaṃ teja eva tad ātman dhatte | [PB, 12, 10 18]
preddho agne dīdihi puro na iti virājābhijuhoty annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 10 19]
traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati | [PB, 12, 10 20]
atijagatīṣu stuvanty ahna utkrāntyā ud vā etenāhnā krāmanti | [PB, 12, 10 21]
diveti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyā apa pāpmānaṃ hate traiśokena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 10 22]
bhāradvājasya pṛśny achāvākasāma bhavati | [PB, 12, 10 23]
annaṃ vai devāḥ pṛśnīti vadanty annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 12, 10 24]
iḍābhir aiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 10 25]
{PB, 12, 11}
pari priyā divaḥ kavir iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai caturtham ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai | [PB, 12, 11 1]
tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 12, 11 2]
somaḥ punāna ūrmiṇāvyavāraṃ vidhāvati agre vācaḥ pavamānaḥ kanikradad iti | [PB, 12, 11 3]
agraṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchann agram evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti | [PB, 12, 11 4]
purojitī vo andhasa iti virājau vairājaṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 12, 11 5]
somaḥ pavate janitā matīnām iti prātassavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītaṃ taṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayanti | [PB, 12, 11 6]
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 12, 11 7]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 12, 11 8]
aurṇāyavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 11 9]
aṅgiraso vai sattram āsata teṣām āptaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo loka āsīt panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prājānaṃs teṣāṃ kalyāṇa āṅgiraso dhyāyam udavrajat sa ūrṇāyuṃ gandharvam apsarasāṃ madhye preṅkhayamāṇam upait sa iyām iti yāṃ yām abhyadiśat sainam akāmayata tam abhyavadat kalyāṇā3 ity āpto vai vaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prajānīthedaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣy atha mā tu voco 'ham adarśam iti | [PB, 12, 11 10]
sa ait kalyāṇaḥ so 'bravīd āpto vai naḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prajānīma idaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣyāma iti kas te 'vocad ity aham evādarśam iti tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam āyann ahīyata kalyāṇo 'nṛtaṃ hi so 'vadat sa eṣaḥ śvitraḥ | [PB, 12, 11 11]
svargyaṃ vā etat sāma svargalokaḥ puṇyaloko bhavaty aurṇāyavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 11 12]
bṛhatkaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 11 13]
sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ tvaṃ hīty annādyasyāvaruddhyai hīti vā annaṃ pradīyate ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati | [PB, 12, 11 14]
ātīṣādīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 11 15]
āyur vā ātīṣādīyam āyuṣo 'varuddhyai | [PB, 12, 11 16]
ā tamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvanti | [PB, 12, 11 17]
nānadaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 11 18]
jyāyo'bhyārambham atihāya pañcamam ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhna ārambhas tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai | [PB, 12, 11 19]
ṣoḍaśākṣareṇa prastauti ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati | [PB, 12, 11 20]
āndhīgavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 11 21]
padyā vā anyā virāḍ akṣaryānyāsmāl lokāt padyayā virājānnādyamavarunddhe 'muṣmād akṣaryayobhayor anayor lokayor annādyam avarunddha āndhīgavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 11 22]
vātsapraṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 11 23]
etasmin vai vairājaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ pratitiṣṭhati vātsapreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 11 24]
vatsaprīr bhālandanaḥ śraddhāṃ nāvindata sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad vātsapram apaśyat sa śraddhām avindata śraddhāṃ vindāmahā iti vai sattram āsate vindate śraddhām | [PB, 12, 11 25]
īnidhanaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 11 26]
{PB, 12, 12}
agniṃ vo vṛdhantam iti | [PB, 12, 12 1]
avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam eva tathā vardhayanti | [PB, 12, 12 2]
vayam u tvām apūrvyety apūrvāṃ hy etarhi prajāpates tanūm agacchann apūrvam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti | [PB, 12, 12 3]
imam indra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭham amartyaṃ madam iti jyaiṣṭhyaṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan jyaiṣṭhyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti | [PB, 12, 12 4]
saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 12 5]
sindhukṣid vai rājanyarṣir jyog aparuddhaś caran sa etat saindhukṣitam apaśyat so 'vāgacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhati saindhukṣitena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 12, 12 6]
saubharaṃ bhavati bṛhatas tejaḥ | [PB, 12, 12 7]
pannam iva vai caturtham ahas tad etena bṛhatas tejasottabhnoti saubhareṇa | [PB, 12, 12 8]
vasiṣṭhasya priyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 12 9]
etena vai vasiṣṭha indrasya premāṇam agacchat premāṇaṃ devatānāṃ gacchati vāsiṣṭhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ | [PB, 12, 12 10]
{PB, 12, 13}
indraśca bṛhacca samabhavatāṃ tam indraṃ bṛhad ekayā tanvātyaricyata tasyā abibhedanayā mābhibhaviṣyatīti so 'bravīt ṣoḍaśī te 'yaṃ yajñakratur astv iti sa ṣoḍaśy abhavat tad asya janma | [PB, 12, 13 1]
ati śriyā bhrātṛvyaṃ ricyate yo gāyatrīṣu dvipadāsu bṛhatā ṣoḍaśinā stute | [PB, 12, 13 2]
upa no haribhiḥ sutam ity etā vai gāyatryo dvipadā etāsu stotavyam | [PB, 12, 13 3]
indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etām anuṣṭubham apaharasaṃ prāyacchat tayā nāstṛṇuta yad astṛto vyanadat tan nānadasya nānadatvam | [PB, 12, 13 4]
taṃ punar upādhāvat tasmai saptānāṃ hotrāṇāṃ haro nirmāya prāyacchat tam astṛṇuta | [PB, 12, 13 5]
stṛṇute taṃ yaṃ tustūrṣate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 13 6]
tasmāddharivatīṣu stuvanti harivatīḥ śaṃsanti harivatīṣu graho gṛhyate haro hy asmai nirmāya prāyacchat | [PB, 12, 13 7]
ekaviṃśāyatano vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī sapta hi prātassavane hotrā vaṣaṭkurvanti sapta mādhyandine savane sapta tṛtīyasavane | [PB, 12, 13 8]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati | [PB, 12, 13 9]
gaurīvitirvā etacchāktyo brahmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavad atiriktaṃ etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinaṃ śvastanavān bhavaty api prajāyā upakﾱptaḥ | [PB, 12, 13 10]
viśālaṃ libujayā bhūtyābhyadhād iti hovācopoditir gopāleyo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadam akar gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinam astoṣṭāñjasā śriyam upāgān na śriyā avapadyata iti | [PB, 12, 13 11]
eṣa vai viśālaṃ libujayā bhūtyābhidadhāti yo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadaṃ kṛtvā gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinā stute 'ñjasā śriyam upaiti na śriyā avapadyate | [PB, 12, 13 12]
śakvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta vajrī syām iti | [PB, 12, 13 13]
vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vajraḥ śakvaryo vajreṇaivāsmai vajraṃ spṛṇoti vajrī bhavati | [PB, 12, 13 14]
anuṣṭupsu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta na mā vāg ativadet | [PB, 12, 13 15]
vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vāg anuṣṭub vajreṇaivāsmai vācaṃ spṛṇoti nainaṃ vāg ativadati | [PB, 12, 13 16]
asāvi soma indra ta ity etāsu stotavyam | [PB, 12, 13 17]
virāṭsv annādyakāmaḥ ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vairājam annaṃ vajreṇaivāsmā annaṃ spṛṇoty annādo bhavati | [PB, 12, 13 18]
pra vo mahe mahe vṛdhe bharadhvam ity etāsu stotavyam | [PB, 12, 13 19]
trayastriṃśadakṣarā vā etā virājo yad ekaviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhā sā yad dvādaśa prajātiḥ sā | [PB, 12, 13 20]
pratiṣṭhāya prajāyate no cāntasthāyāṃ jīyate ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 13 21]
atha vā etā ekapadās tryakṣarā viṣṇoś chando bhurijaḥ śakvaryaḥ | [PB, 12, 13 22]
etābhir vā indro vṛtram ahan kṣipraṃ vā etābhiḥ pāpmānaṃ hanti kṣipraṃ vasīyān bhavati | [PB, 12, 13 23]
catustriṃśadakṣarāḥ saṃstuto bhavati trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evopayanty ariṣṭyai | [PB, 12, 13 24]
hiraṇyaṃ saṃpradāyaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvate jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati | [PB, 12, 13 25]
aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa upatiṣṭhati sāmyekṣyāya bhrātṛvyalokam eva sa vidhamaṃs tiṣṭhati | [PB, 12, 13 26]
ekākṣaraṃ vai devānām avamaṃ chanda āsīt saptākṣaraṃ paramaṃ navākṣaram asurāṇām avamaṃ chanda āsīt pañcadaśākṣaraṃ paramaṃ devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta tān prajāpatir ānuṣṭubho bhūtvāntarātiṣṭhat taṃ devāsurā vyahvayanta sa devān upāvartata tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ | [PB, 12, 13 27]
bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 13 28]
te devā asurāṇām ekākṣareṇaiva pañcadaśākṣaram avṛñjata dvyakṣareṇa caturdaśākṣaraṃ tryakṣareṇa trayodaśākṣaraṃ caturakṣareṇa dvādaśākṣaraṃ pañcākṣareṇaikādaśākṣaraṃ ṣaḍakṣareṇa daśākṣaraṃ saptākṣareṇa navākṣaram aṣṭābhir evāṣṭāv avṛñjata | [PB, 12, 13 29]
evam eva bhrātṛvyād bhūtiṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 13 30]
aparuddhayajña iva vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī kanīyasvina iva vai tarhi devā āsan bhūyasvino 'surāḥ kanīyasvinaḥ bhūyasvinaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 13 31]
yasmād anyo na paro 'sti jāto ya ābabhūva bhuvanāni viśvā | [PB, 12, 13 32]
jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 12, 13 33]
ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 12, 13 34]
{PB, 13, 1}
govit pavasva vasuviddhiraṇyavid iti pañcamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 13, 1 1]
govid vā etad vasuviddhiraṇyavid yacchakvaryaḥ | [PB, 13, 1 2]
paśavaś śakvaryaḥ sarvaṃ paśubhir vindate | [PB, 13, 1 3]
tvaṃ suvīro asi soma viśvavid ityeṣa vāva suvīro yasya paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 13, 1 4]
tās te kṣarantu madhumad ghṛtaṃ paya iti madhumad vai ghṛtaṃ payaḥ paśavaḥ kṣaranti tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 13, 1 5]
pavamānasya viśvavid ity anurūpo bhavati | [PB, 13, 1 6]
viśvam eva tad vittam abhivadati viśvaṃ hi paśubhir vindate | [PB, 13, 1 7]
pra te sargā asṛkṣateti sṛṣṭānīva hyetarhyahāni | [PB, 13, 1 8]
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 1 9]
saptarcau bhavataḥ chandasāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 13, 1 10]
caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 1 11]
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 13, 1 12]
triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥ | [PB, 13, 1 13]
{PB, 13, 2}
tava śriyo varṣyasyeva vidyuta ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 2 1]
śrīr vai paśavaḥ śrīḥ śakvaryaḥ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 13, 2 2]
agneś cikitra uṣasām ivetaya itītānīva hyetarhyahānīty ā te yatante rathyo yathā pṛthag ity eva hyetarhyahāni yatante | [PB, 13, 2 3]
purūruṇā ciddhy asty avo nūnaṃ vāṃ varuṇeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajati | [PB, 13, 2 4]
uttiṣṭhann ojasā sahety aindram | [PB, 13, 2 5]
pañca vā ṛtava utthānasya rūpam ojasā sahety ojasaiva vīryeṇa sahottiṣṭhanti | [PB, 13, 2 6]
indrāgnī yuvām ima iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam | [PB, 13, 2 7]
rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yacchakvaryo rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 2 8]
{PB, 13, 3}
arṣā soma dyumattama iti viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti | [PB, 13, 3 1]
brahma vai gāyatrī yajño viṣṇur brahmaṇy eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 13, 3 2]
soma uṣvāṇa stotṛbhir iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaitās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati | [PB, 13, 3 3]
yat soma citram ukthyam iti gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 13, 3 4]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 13, 3 5]
yaṇvaṃ bhavati paśavo vai yaṇvaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 3 6]
santataṃ gāyati yajñasya saṃtatyai | [PB, 13, 3 7]
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 13, 3 8]
śākalaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 3 9]
etena vai śakalaḥ pañcame 'hani pratyatiṣṭhat pratitiṣṭhati śākalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 3 10]
vārśaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 3 11]
vṛśo vaijānas tryaruṇasya traidhātavasyaikṣvākasya purohita āsīt sa aikṣvāko 'dhāvayat brāhmaṇakumāraṃ rathena vyachinat sa purohitam abravīt tava mā purodhāyām idam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vārśaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 13, 3 12]
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 13, 3 13]
mānavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 3 14]
etena vai manuḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati mānavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 3 15]
ānūpaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 3 16]
etena vai vadhryaśva ānūpaḥ paśūnāṃ bhūmānam āśnuta paśūnāṃ bhūmānam aśnuta ānūpena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 3 17]
vāmraṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 3 18]
sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ yaṃ vai gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ praśaṃsanti vāma iti taṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti | [PB, 13, 3 19]
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam | [PB, 13, 3 20]
triṇidhanam āgneyaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 3 21]
agniḥ sṛṣṭo nodadīpyata taṃ prajāpatir etena sāmnopādhamat sa udadīpyata dīptiś ca vā etat sāma brahmavarcasaṃ ca dīptiṃ caivaitena brahmavarcasaṃ cāvarunddhe | [PB, 13, 3 22]
śaiśavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 3 23]
śiśur vā āṅgiraso mantrakṛtāṃ mantrakṛd āsīt sa pitṝn putrakā ity āmantrayata taṃ pitaro 'bruvan na dharmaṃ karoṣi yo naḥ pitṝn sataḥ putrakā ity āmantrayasa iti so 'bravīd ahaṃ vāva vaḥ pitāsmi yo mantrakṛd asmīti te deveṣv apṛcchanta te devā abruvann eṣa vāva pitā yo mantrakṛd iti tad vai sa udajayad ujjayati śaiśavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 3 24]
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 13, 3 25]
viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 3 26]
{PB, 13, 4}
indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etacchandobhya indriyaṃ vīryaṃ nirmāya prāyacchad etena śaknuhīti tacchakvarīṇāṃ śakvarītvaṃ sīmānam abhinat tat simā mahnyām akarot tan mahnyā mahān ghoṣa āsīt tan mahānāmnyaḥ | [PB, 13, 4 1]
diśaḥ pañcapadā dādhārartūn ṣaṭpadā chandāṃsi saptapadā puruṣaṃ dvipadā | [PB, 13, 4 2]
dvyopaśāḥ saṃstutā bhavanti tasmād dvyopaśāḥ paśavaḥ | [PB, 13, 4 3]
iḍe abhito 'thakāraṃ tasmācchṛṅge tīkṣṇīyasī stūpāt | [PB, 13, 4 4]
upakṣudrā gāyati tasmād upakṣudrāḥ paśavaḥ | [PB, 13, 4 5]
asaṃśliṣṭā gāyati tasmād asaṃśliṣṭāḥ paśavaḥ | [PB, 13, 4 6]
nānārūpā gāyati tasmān nānārūpāḥ paśavaḥ | [PB, 13, 4 7]
āpo vai kṣīrarasā āsaṃste devāḥ pāpavasīyasād abibhayur yad apa upanidhāya stuvate pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai | [PB, 13, 4 8]
vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 13, 4 9]
gāyatram ayanaṃ bhavati brahmavarcasakāmasya svarṇidhanaṃ madhunāmuṣmiṃlloka upatiṣṭhate traiṣṭubham ayanaṃ bhavaty ojaskāmasyāthakāraṇidhanam ājyenāmuṣmiṃlloka upatiṣṭhate jāgatam ayanaṃ bhavati paśukāmasyeḍānidhanaṃ payasāmuṣmiṃlloka upatiṣṭhate | [PB, 13, 4 10]
añjasāryo mālyaḥ śakvarīḥ prārautsīd iti hovācālammaṃ pārijānataṃ rajanaḥ kauṇeyo yady enāḥ pratiṣṭhāpaṃ śakṣyatīty etad vā etāsām añja etat pratiṣṭhitā ya ābhiḥ kṣipraṃ prastutya kṣipram udgāyati | [PB, 13, 4 11]
śakvarībhiḥ stutvā purīṣeṇa stuvate | [PB, 13, 4 12]
paśavo vai śakvaryo goṣṭhaḥ purīṣaṃ goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartayanty avisraṃsāya | [PB, 13, 4 13]
indro madāya vāvṛdha ity avardhanta hy etarhi | [PB, 13, 4 14]
tāsu bārhadgiram | [PB, 13, 4 15]
svādor itthā viṣuvata iti viṣuvān vai pañcamam ahas tāsu rāyovājīyam | [PB, 13, 4 16]
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta pṛthuraśmir bṛhadgirī rāyovājas te 'bruvan ko na imān putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro 'bravīt tān adhinidhāya paricārya caran vardhayaṃs tān vardhayitvābravīt kumārakā varān vṛṇīdhvam iti kṣatraṃ mahyam ity abravīt pṛthuraśmis tasmā etena pārthuraśmena kṣatraṃ prāyacchat kṣatrakāma etena stuvīta kṣatrasyaivāsya prakāśo bhavati brahmavarcasaṃ mahyam ity abravīt bṛhadgiris tasmā etena bārhadgireṇa prāyacchat brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati paśūn mahyam ity abravīd rāyovājas tasmā etena rāyovājīyena paśūn prāyacchat paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati | [PB, 13, 4 17]
pārthuraśmaṃ rājanyāya brahmasāma kuryāt bārhadgiraṃ brāhmaṇāya rāyovājīyaṃ vaiśyāya svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 4 18]
{PB, 13, 5}
asāvy aṃśur madāyeti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 13, 5 1]
abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhad yaśa ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaityubhau hi varṇāvetad ahaḥ | [PB, 13, 5 2]
prāṇā śiśur mahīnām iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ mahyo hi simāḥ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati | [PB, 13, 5 3]
pavasva vājasātaya iti vaiṣṇavyo 'nuṣṭubho bhavanti | [PB, 13, 5 4]
yajño vai viṣṇur yad atra nāpi kriyate tad viṣṇunā yajñenāpi karoti | [PB, 13, 5 5]
indur vājī pavate gonyoghā iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati | [PB, 13, 5 6]
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 13, 5 7]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 13, 5 8]
saṃtani bhavati pañcamasyāhnas santatyai | [PB, 13, 5 9]
vāg vā eṣā pratatā yad dvādaśāhas tasyā eṣa viṣuvān yat pañcamam ahas tām evaitena saṃtanoti | [PB, 13, 5 10]
cyāvanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 5 11]
prajātir vai cyāvanaṃ prajāyate bahur bhavati cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 5 12]
ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tāṃ prajāpatiś cyāvanenācyāvayad yad acyāvayat taccyāvanasya cyāvanatvaṃ cyāvayati vṛṣṭiṃ cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 5 13]
krośaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 5 14]
etena vā indra indrakrośe viśvāmitrajamadagnī imā gāva ityākrośat paśūnām avaruddhyai krośaṃ kriyate | [PB, 13, 5 15]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 13, 5 16]
ṛṣabhaḥ śākvaro bhavati | [PB, 13, 5 17]
paśavo vai śakvaryaḥ paśuṣveva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante | [PB, 13, 5 18]
pārthaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 5 19]
etena vai pṛthī vainya ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam aśnute pārthena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 5 20]
aṣṭeḍaḥ padastobho bhavati | [PB, 13, 5 21]
indro vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat taṃ ṣoḍaśabhir bhogaiḥ paryabhujat sa etaṃ padastobham apaśyat tenāpāveṣṭayad apaveṣṭayann iva gāyet pāpmano 'pahatyai | [PB, 13, 5 22]
pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ padastobhenāpāhatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate padastobhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 5 23]
pador uttamam apaśyat tat padastobhasya padastobhatvam | [PB, 13, 5 24]
dvādaśanidhano bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 5 25]
dāśaspatyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 5 26]
yāṃ vai gāṃ praśaṃsanti dāśaspatyeti tāṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti | [PB, 13, 5 27]
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 5 28]
{PB, 13, 6}
ā te agna idhīmahi iti | [PB, 13, 6 1]
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva | [PB, 13, 6 2]
indrāya sāma gāyateti pūrṇāḥ kakubhas tenānaśanāyuko bhavati | [PB, 13, 6 3]
puruṣo vai kakup puruṣam eva tan madhyataḥ prīṇāti | [PB, 13, 6 4]
asāvi soma indra ta iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati | [PB, 13, 6 5]
saṃjayaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 6 6]
devāś ca vā asurāśca samadadhata yatare naḥ saṃjayāṃs teṣāṃ naḥ paśavo 'sān iti te devā asurān saṃjayena samajayan yat samajayaṃs tasmāt saṃjayaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai saṃjayaṃ kriyate | [PB, 13, 6 7]
saumitraṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 6 8]
dīrghajihvī vā idaṃ rakṣo yajñahā yajñiyān avalihaty acarat tām indraḥ kayācana māyayā hantuṃ nāśaṃsatātha ha sumitraḥ kutsaḥ kalyāṇa āsa tam abravīd imām acchābrūṣveti tām acchābrūta sainam abravīn nāhaitanna śuśruva priyam iva tu me hṛdayasyeti tām ajñapayat tāṃ saṃskṛte 'hatāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma saumitraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 13, 6 9]
sumitraḥ san krūram akar ity enaṃ vāg abhyavadat taṃ śug ārchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat saumitram apaśyat tena śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hate saumitreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 6 10]
mahāvaiśvāmitraṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 6 11]
pāpmānaṃ hatvā yad amahīyanta tan mahāvaiśvāmitrasya mahāvaiśvāmitratvam | [PB, 13, 6 12]
hāyā ihayā ohā oheti paśūn evaitena nyauhanta | [PB, 13, 6 13]
trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai | [PB, 13, 6 14]
dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ santatyai | [PB, 13, 6 15]
triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥ | [PB, 13, 6 16]
{PB, 13, 7}
jyotir yajñasya pavate madhu priyam iti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 13, 7 1]
jyotir vai gāyatrī chandasāṃ jyotiḥ revatī sāmnāṃ jyotis trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ jyotir eva tat samyak saṃdadhāty api ha putrasya putro jyotiṣmān bhavati | [PB, 13, 7 2]
madhu priyam iti paśavo vai revatyo madhu priyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 13, 7 3]
madintamo matsara indriyo rasa itīndriyaṃ vai vīryaṃ rasaḥ paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati | [PB, 13, 7 4]
asṛkṣata pra vājina ity anurūpo bhavati | [PB, 13, 7 5]
sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāni | [PB, 13, 7 6]
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 7 7]
daśarcau bhavato daśākṣarā virāṭ vairājam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 7 8]
uttaro daśarco bhavati sodarka indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya | [PB, 13, 7 9]
yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan | [PB, 13, 7 10]
caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 7 11]
dhvasre vai puruṣantī tarantapurumīḍhābhyāṃ vaidadaśvibhyāṃ sahasrāṇy aditsatāṃ tāv aikṣetāṃ kathaṃ nāv idam āttam apratigṛhītaṃ syād iti tau praty etāṃ dhvasrayoḥ puruṣantyor ā sahasrāṇi dadmahe tarat sa mandī dhāvatīti tato vai tat tayor āttam apratigṛhītam abhavat | [PB, 13, 7 12]
āttam asyāpratigṛhītaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 13, 7 13]
vinārāśaṃso bhavaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai mānuṣasya ca daivasya ca | [PB, 13, 7 14]
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 13, 7 15]
trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ | [PB, 13, 7 16]
{PB, 13, 8}
imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedasa ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan | [PB, 13, 8 1]
prati vāṃ sūra udita iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam | [PB, 13, 8 2]
anto vai sūro 'nta etat ṣaṣṭham ahar ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 8 3]
bhinddhi viśvā apa dviṣa ity aindraṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan | [PB, 13, 8 4]
yajñasya hi stha ṛtvija ity aindrāgnaṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 8 5]
{PB, 13, 9}
indrāyendo marutvata iti marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti | [PB, 13, 9 1]
marutvaddhi mādhyandinaṃ savanam | [PB, 13, 9 2]
mṛjyamānaḥ suhastya iti simānāṃ rūpam | [PB, 13, 9 3]
samānaṃ vai simānāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ ca simābhyo hy adhi revatyaḥ prajāyante | [PB, 13, 9 4]
etam u tyaṃ daśa kṣipa ity ādityā ādityā vā imāḥ prajās tāsām eva madhyataḥ pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 13, 9 5]
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 13, 9 6]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 13, 9 7]
iṣovṛdhīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 9 8]
paśavo vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyā iṣe vai pañcamam ahar vṛdhe ṣaṣṭham avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitena vardhayanti | [PB, 13, 9 9]
krauñcaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 9 10]
kruṅṅ eṣyam ahar avindad eṣyam iva vai ṣaṣṭham ahar ahar evaitena vindanti | [PB, 13, 9 11]
vājadāvaryo bhavanti | [PB, 13, 9 12]
annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai yadā hi vā annam atha gaur athāśvo 'tha puruṣo vājī | [PB, 13, 9 13]
revatyo bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 9 14]
ṣaṇṇidhanī ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai | [PB, 13, 9 15]
āpo vai revatyas tā yat pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryur apaśur yajamānaḥ syāt paśūn asya nirdaheyur yatra vā āpo vivartante tad oṣadhayo jāyante 'tha yatrāvatiṣṭhante nirmṛtukās tatra bhavanti tasmāt pavamāne kurvanti parācā hi pavamānena stuvate | [PB, 13, 9 16]
methī vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ rajjuḥ krauñcaṃ vatso vājadāvaryo revatyo mātaro yad etāny evaṃ sāmāni kriyanta evam eva prattāṃ dugdhe | [PB, 13, 9 17]
aukṣṇorandhre bhavataḥ | [PB, 13, 9 18]
ukṣṇorandhro vā etābhyāṃ kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 9 19]
vājajid bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvaṃ vā ete vājaṃ jayanti ye ṣaṣṭham ahar āgacchanti | [PB, 13, 9 20]
annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 9 21]
varuṇasāma bhavati | [PB, 13, 9 22]
etena vai varuṇo rājyam ādhipatyam agacchad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati varuṇasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 9 23]
aṅgirasāṃ goṣṭho bhavati | [PB, 13, 9 24]
paśavo vai revatyo goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartayanty avisraṃsāya | [PB, 13, 9 25]
ihavad vāmadevyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 9 26]
etena vai vāmadevo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhānnasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 9 27]
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 13, 9 28]
marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 9 29]
{PB, 13, 10}
yātayāmāny anyāni chandāṃsy ayātayāmā gāyatrī tasmād gāyatrīṣu stuvanti | [PB, 13, 10 1]
surūpakṛtnum ūtaya ity abhyārambheṇa ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai | [PB, 13, 10 2]
ubhe yad indra rodasī iti ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai | [PB, 13, 10 3]
revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 10 4]
apāṃ vā eṣa raso yad revatyo revatīnāṃ raso yad vāravantīyaṃ sarasā eva tad revatīḥ prayuṅkte yad vāravantīyena pṛṣṭhena stuvate | [PB, 13, 10 5]
revad vā etad raivatyaṃ yad vāravantīyam asya revān raivatyo jāyate | [PB, 13, 10 6]
revān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 13, 10 7]
keśine vā etad dālbhyāya sāmāvirabhavat tad enam abravīd agātāro mā gāyanti mā mayodgāsiṣur iti kathaṃ ta āgā bhagava ity abravīd āgeyam evāsmy āgāyann iva gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai tad alammaṃ pārijānataṃ paścādakṣaṃ śayānam etām āgāṃ gāyantam ajānāt tam abravīt puras tvā dadhā iti tam abruvan ko nv ayaṃ kasmā alam ity alaṃ nu vai mahyam iti tad alammasyālammatvam | [PB, 13, 10 8]
iheheti gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 10 9]
ṛṣabho raivato bhavati | [PB, 13, 10 10]
paśavo vai raivatyaḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante | [PB, 13, 10 11]
śyeno bhavati | [PB, 13, 10 12]
śyeno ha vai pūrvapretāni vayāṃsy āpnoti pūrvapretānīva vai pūrvāṇy ahāni teṣām āptyai śyenaḥ kriyate | [PB, 13, 10 13]
śyeno vā etad ahaḥ saṃpārayitum arhati sa hi vayasām āśiṣṭhas tasyānapahananāya sampāraṇāyaitat kriyate 'nto hi ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca | [PB, 13, 10 14]
brahmavādino vadanti yad bṛhadāyatanāni pṛṣṭhāny athaite dve gāyatryau dve jagatyau kva tarhi bṛhatyo bhavantīti | [PB, 13, 10 15]
ye dve jagatyoḥ pade te gāyatryā upasaṃpadyete tat sarvā bṛhatyo bhavanty āyatane pṛṣṭhāni yātayatyāyatanavān bhavati | [PB, 13, 10 16]
ṣaṭpadāsu stuvanti ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai | [PB, 13, 10 17]
saptapadayā yajati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 10 18]
{PB, 13, 11}
parisvāno giriṣṭhā iti parivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti sarvasya paryāptyai | [PB, 13, 11 1]
samunveyo vasūnām iti paśavo vai vasu paśūnām avaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 11 2]
taṃ vaḥ sakhāyo madāyeti vālakhilyāḥ | [PB, 13, 11 3]
vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca | [PB, 13, 11 4]
yad etau vālakhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgāyāvyavasraṃsāya santatyai | [PB, 13, 11 5]
somāḥ pavanta indava ity anuṣṭubho nibhasado bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 11 6]
ayā pavā pavasvainā vasūnīti triṣṭubhas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 13, 11 7]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 13, 11 8]
vaidanvatāni bhavanti | [PB, 13, 11 9]
vidanvān vai bhārgava indrasya pratyahaṃs taṃ śug ārchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etāni vaidanvatāny apaśyat taiḥ śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hate vaidanvatais tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 11 10]
bharadvājasya loma bhavati paśavo vai loma paśūnām avaruddhyai | [PB, 13, 11 11]
tad u dīrgham ity āhur āyur vai dīrgham āyuṣo 'varuddhyai | [PB, 13, 11 12]
kārṇaśravasaṃ bhavati śṛṇvanti tuṣṭuvānam | [PB, 13, 11 13]
karṇaśravā vā etad āṅgirasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai | [PB, 13, 11 14]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 13, 11 15]
madhuścyunnidhanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 11 16]
paramasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai paramaṃ vā etad annādyaṃ yan madhu | [PB, 13, 11 17]
prajāpater vā etau stanau yad ghṛtaścyunnidhanaṃ ca madhuścyunnidhanaṃ ca yajño vai prajāpatis tam etābhyāṃ dugdhe yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ dugdhe | [PB, 13, 11 18]
krauñce bhavataḥ | [PB, 13, 11 19]
kruṅṅ eṣyam ahar avindad eṣyamiva vai ṣaṣṭham ahar aharevaitābhyām vindati | [PB, 13, 11 20]
śnauṣṭaṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 11 21]
śnuṣṭir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāt lokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 13, 11 22]
agner vā etad vaiśvānarasya sāma dīdihīti nidhanam upayanti dīdāyeva hy agnir vaiśvānaraḥ | [PB, 13, 11 23]
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ | [PB, 13, 11 24]
{PB, 13, 12}
brahmavādino vadanti prāyaṇato dvipadāḥ kāryā udayanatā3 iti | [PB, 13, 12 1]
udayanata eva kāryāḥ puruṣo vai dvipadāḥ pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 13, 12 2]

gūrdo bhavati | [PB, 13, 12 4]
gaupāyanānāṃ vai sattram āsīnānāṃ kirātakulyāv asuramāye antaḥparidhy asūn prākiratāṃ te agne tvaṃ no antama ity agnim upāsīdaṃs tenāsūn aspṛṇvaṃs tad vāva te tarhy akāmayanta kāmasani sāma gūrdaḥ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 13, 12 5]
gotamasya bhadraṃ bhavati | [PB, 13, 12 6]
āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ | [PB, 13, 12 7]
etena vai gotamo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchat tasmād ye ca parāñco gotamād ye cārvāñcas ta ubhaye gotamā ṛṣayo bruvate | [PB, 13, 12 8]
udvaṃśaputro bhavati | [PB, 13, 12 9]
yad vā udvaṃśīyaṃ tad udvaṃśaputraḥ | [PB, 13, 12 10]
ardheḍām atisvarati | [PB, 13, 12 11]

kﾱpta upariṣṭād ṛk sāma ca vimucyete abhy u svareṇa saptamam ahaḥ svarati santatyai | [PB, 13, 12 13]
ūhuṣīva vā etarhi vāg yadā ṣaḍahaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate na bahu vaden nānyaṃ pṛcchen nānyasmai prabrūyāt | [PB, 13, 12 14]
madhu vāśayed ghṛtaṃ vā yathohuṣo vahaṃ pratyanakti tathā tat | [PB, 13, 12 15]

{PB, 14, 1}
āpyante vā etat stomāś chandāṃsi yat ṣaḍaha āpyate | [PB, 14, 1 1]

pra kāvyam uśaneva bruvāṇa iti gāyatryā rūpeṇa prayanti | [PB, 14, 1 3]
iyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya prayanti | [PB, 14, 1 4]
triṣṭup pratipad bhavati | [PB, 14, 1 5]

harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 14, 1 8]
dvādaśarcau bhavataḥ | [PB, 14, 1 9]

caturviṃśatir bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai | [PB, 14, 1 11]
dṛta aindrota iti hovācābhipratārī kākṣasenir ye mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ gacchanti kva te tato bhavanti pra rājan pakṣiṇaḥ patanty avāpakṣāḥ padyante | [PB, 14, 1 12]
ye vai vidvāṃsas te pakṣiṇo ye 'vidvāṃsas te 'pakṣās trivṛtpañcadaśāv eva stomau pakṣau kṛtvā svargaṃ lokaṃ prayanti | [PB, 14, 1 13]

{PB, 14, 2}
mūrdhānaṃ divo aratim pṛthivyā ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 2 1]
mūrdhā vā eṣa divo yas tṛtīyas trirātraḥ | [PB, 14, 2 2]
vaiśvānaram ṛta ājātam agnim iti vaiśvānara iti vā agneḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati | [PB, 14, 2 3]
pra vo mitrāya gāyateti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī vai mitrāvaruṇayoḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainau tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati | [PB, 14, 2 4]
indrāyāhi citrabhānav ity ārbhavam aindram ṛbhavo vā indrasya priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati | [PB, 14, 2 5]
tam īḍiṣva yo arciṣety aniruktam aindrāgnaṃ devatānām anabhidharṣāyottamārdhe nirāha devatānām apraṇāśāya stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 2 6]
{PB, 14, 3}
vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavatyahno dhṛtyai | [PB, 14, 3 1]
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hyetad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 3 2]
punānaḥ soma dhārayeti dhṛtyai | [PB, 14, 3 3]
pro ayāsīd indur indrasya niṣkṛtam iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṣeṇyam iva hyetad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 3 4]
jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 14, 3 5]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 3 6]
saṃtani bhavati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai | [PB, 14, 3 7]
yathā vai vyokasau vipradravata evam ete ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca vipradravatas tau yathā samānīya saṃyujyād evam evaite etena sāmnā saṃyunakti | [PB, 14, 3 8]
sauparṇaṃ bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [PB, 14, 3 9]
yajño vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat sa suparṇarūpaṃ kṛtvācarat taṃ devā etaiḥ sāmabhirārabhanta yajña iva vā eṣa yacchandomā yajñasyaivaiṣa ārambhaḥ | [PB, 14, 3 10]
rohitakūlīyaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai | [PB, 14, 3 11]
etena vai viśvāmitro rohitābhyāṃ rohitakūla ājim ajayat | [PB, 14, 3 12]
viśvāmitro bharatānām anasvatyāyāt so 'dantibhir nāma janatayāṃśaṃ prāsyatemāṃ māṃ yūyaṃ vasnikāṃ jayāthemāni mahyaṃ yūyaṃ pūrayātha yadīmāvidaṃ rohitāvaśmācitaṃ kūlam udvahāta iti sa ete sāmanī apaśyat tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhat sa udajayat | [PB, 14, 3 13]
ājir vā eṣa pratato yad dvādaśāhas tasyaite ujjityai | [PB, 14, 3 14]
kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 3 15]
tejo vā etad rathantarasya yat kaṇvarathantaram sarasam eva tad rathantaraṃ prayuṅkte yat kaṇvarathantareṇa saptame 'hani stuvate | [PB, 14, 3 16]
jāmi dvādaśāhasyāstīti ha smāhogradevo rājanir bārhataṃ ṣaṣṭham ahar bārhataṃ saptamaṃ yat kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati tenājāmi | [PB, 14, 3 17]
gauṅgavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 3 18]
agnir akāmayatānnādaḥ syām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad gauṅgavam apaśyat tenānnādo 'bhavad yad annaṃ vitvā agardad yad agaṅgūyat tad gauṅgavasya gauṅgavatvam annādyasyāvaruddhyai gauṅgavaṃ kriyate | [PB, 14, 3 19]
yat sāma devatāḥ praśaṃsati tena yajamānāḥ satyāśiṣaḥ satyāśiṣo 'sāmeti vai sattram āsate satyāśiṣa eva bhavanti | [PB, 14, 3 20]
āyāsyaṃ bhavati tiraścīnanidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 14, 3 21]
ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annam āśnāt sa vyabhraṃśata sa etāny āyāsyāny apaśyat tair ātmānaṃ samaśrīṇād vibhraṣṭam iva vai saptamam ahar yad etat sāma bhavaty ahar eva tena saṃśrīṇāti | [PB, 14, 3 22]
pravadbhargavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 3 23]
pravatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyannudvatodāyan | [PB, 14, 3 24]

{PB, 14, 4}
vayaṃ gha tvā sutāvanta iti satobṛhatyo varṣīyaśchanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya | [PB, 14, 4 1]
