abhinidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 4 4]
abhinidhanena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tam astṛṇuta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyam abhinidhanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 4 5]
vaikhānasaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 4 6]
vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsaṃs tān rahasyur devamalimluḍ munimaraṇe 'mārayat taṃ devā abruvan kva tarṣayo 'bhūvann iti tān praiṣam aicchat tān nāvindat sa imān lokān ekadhāreṇāpunāt tān munimaraṇe 'vindat tān etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vaikhānasaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 4 7]
{PB, 14, 5}
yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 14, 5 1]
eṣa sya dhārayā suta iti kakubhaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa triṣṭubhaḥ | [PB, 14, 5 2]
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yat jyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa triṣṭubho bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya | [PB, 14, 5 3]
sakhāya āniṣīdateti vālakhilyā vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca yad etau vālakhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgāyāvyavasraṃsāya santatyai | [PB, 14, 5 4]
purojitī vo andhasa iti virāḍ annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 5 5]
pra vājy akṣār ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtiḥ | [PB, 14, 5 6]
atho etaddhyevaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante | [PB, 14, 5 7]
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā ity etacchandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt | [PB, 14, 5 8]
ye somāsaḥ parāvatīti parāvatam iva vā etarhi yajño gatas tam evaitenānvicchanti | [PB, 14, 5 9]
gāyatryaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 14, 5 10]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 5 11]
dakṣaṇidhanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 5 12]
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmāt sṛṣṭā abalā ivācchadayaṃs tāsv etena sāmnā dakṣāyety ojo vīryam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavaty oja eva vīryam ātman dhatte | [PB, 14, 5 13]
śārkaraṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 5 14]
indraṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny astuvan sa śarkaraṃ śiśumārarṣim upetyābravīt stuhi meti so 'paḥ praskandann abravīd etāvato 'haṃ tvāṃ stuyām iti tasmād apāṃ vegam avejayat sa hīna ivāmanyata sa etat sāmāpaśyat tenāpo 'nusamāśnuta tad vāva sa tarhyakāmayata kāmasani sāma śārkaraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 14, 5 15]
plavo bhavati | [PB, 14, 5 16]
samudraṃ vā ete prasnāntīty āhur ye dvādaśāham upayantīti yo vā aplavaḥ samudraṃ prasnāti na sa tata udeti yat plavo bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [PB, 14, 5 17]
ativiśvāni duritā taremeti yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṭutaṃ duśśastaṃ tad etena taranti | [PB, 14, 5 18]
ekādaśākṣaraṇidhano bhavaty ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub ojovīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasy eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 14, 5 19]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 5 20]
kārtayaśaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 5 21]
hīti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyai | [PB, 14, 5 22]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate kārtayaśena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 5 23]
sauhaviṣaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 5 24]
suhavir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 5 25]
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā iti puruṣaś chandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 14, 5 26]
jarābodhīyaṃ bhavaty annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 5 27]
annaṃ vai jarābodhīyaṃ mukhaṃ gāyatrī mukha eva tad annaṃ dhatte 'nnam atti | [PB, 14, 5 28]
annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 14, 5 29]
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 14, 5 30]
iḍāntāḥ pāvamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍāḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 5 31]
{PB, 14, 6}
ā te vatso mano yamad ity apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva | [PB, 14, 6 1]
tvaṃ na indrābhareti pūrṇāḥ kakubhaḥ | [PB, 14, 6 2]
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yajjyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etāḥ pūrṇāḥ kakubho bhavanty anapabhraṃśāya | [PB, 14, 6 3]
yad indra citraṃ ma iha nāsti tvādātam adrivo rādhas tanno vidadvasa ubhayāhastyābhareti rāddhim evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 14, 6 4]
vātsaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 6 5]
vatsaś ca vai medhātithiś ca kāṇvāv āstāṃ taṃ vatsaṃ medhātithir ākrośad abrāhmaṇo 'si śūdrāputra iti so 'bravīd ṛtenāgniṃ vyayāva yataro nau brahmīyān iti vātsena vatso vyain maidhātithena medhātithis tasya na loma ca nauṣat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vātsaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 14, 6 6]
sauśravasaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 6 7]
upagur vai sauśravasaḥ kutsasyauravasya purohita āsīt sa kutsaḥ paryaśapad ya indraṃ yajātā iti sa indraḥ suśravasam upetyābravīd yajasva māśanāyāmi vā iti tam ayajata sa indraḥ puroḍāśahastaḥ kutsam upetyābravīd ayakṣata mā kva te pariśaptam abhūd iti kas tvā yaṣṭeti suśravā iti sa kutsa aurava upagoḥ sauśravasasyodgāyata audumbaryā śiro 'chinat sa suśravā indram abravīt tvattanād vai medam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma sauśravasaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 14, 6 8]
vīṅkaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 6 9]
cyavano vai dādhīco 'śvinoḥ priya āsīt so 'jīryat tam etena sāmnāpsu vyaiṅkayatāṃ taṃ punaryuvānam akurutāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma vīṅkaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 14, 6 10]
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya | [PB, 14, 6 11]
{PB, 14, 7}
śiśuṃ jajñānaṃ haryataṃ mṛjantīty aṣṭamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 14, 7 1]
śiśur iva vā eṣa saptamenāhnā jāyate tam aṣṭamenāhnā mṛjanti | [PB, 14, 7 2]
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 7 3]
harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 14, 7 4]
navarcā bhavanti | [PB, 14, 7 5]
pañcarco bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 7 6]
vāṇavān bhavaty anto vai vāṇo 'nta etad aṣṭamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 14, 7 7]
trayas tṛcā bhavanti prāṇāpānānāṃ santatyai | [PB, 14, 7 8]
catuścatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavatyojasyeva tadvīrye pratitiṣṭhatyojovīryaṃ triṣṭup | [PB, 14, 7 9]
{PB, 14, 8}
agniṃ vo devam agnibhiḥ sajoṣā ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 8 1]
agnibhir ity eva pūrvāṇy ahāni abhisamiddhānyaṣṭamam ahar abhisaminddhe | [PB, 14, 8 2]
mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha iti bārhataṃ maitrāvaruṇam | [PB, 14, 8 3]
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya | [PB, 14, 8 4]
tam indraṃ vājayāmasītyaindram | [PB, 14, 8 5]
aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayan navamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena vājayanti | [PB, 14, 8 6]
indre agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam aindrāgnam | [PB, 14, 8 7]
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 8 8]
{PB, 14, 9}
adhvaryo adribhiḥ sutam iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai | [PB, 14, 9 1]
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 2]
abhi somāsa āyava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 3]
dhartā divaḥ pavate kṛtvyo rasa ity adhṛta iva vā eṣas tryaho yad dharteti dhṛtyā eva | [PB, 14, 9 4]
jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubho loke kriyante | [PB, 14, 9 5]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 9 6]
vairūpaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 7]
paśavo vai vairūpaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 9 8]
āśu bhārgavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 9]
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā āśunābhyadhinvaṃs tad āśor āśutvam | [PB, 14, 9 10]
mārgīyavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 11]
devaṃ vā etaṃ mṛgayur iti vadanty etena vai sa ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam aśnute mārgīyaveṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 12]
saumitraṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 13]
yad eva saumitrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 9 14]
aiṭataṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 15]
iḍhan vā etena kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 16]
sākamaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva sākamaśvasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 9 17]
tad u dhurāṃ sāmety āhuḥ prāṇā vai dhuraḥ prāṇānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 9 18]
vilambasauparṇaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 19]
ātmā vā eṣa sauparṇānāṃ yad aṣṭame 'hani pakṣāv etāv abhito bhavato ye saptamanavamayor vīva vā antarātmā pakṣau lambate yadantarātmā pakṣau vilambate tasmād vilambasauparṇam | [PB, 14, 9 20]
svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai sauparṇaṃ kriyate | [PB, 14, 9 21]
dvihiṃkāraṃ vāmadevyaṃ bhavatyannādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 9 22]
dvitīyaṃ hy etad rūpaṃ yac chandomāḥ | [PB, 14, 9 23]
paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn saṃdadhāti | [PB, 14, 9 24]
gāyatrapārśvaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 25]
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā gāyatrapārśvena samatanvaṃs tasmād gāyatrapārśvam | [PB, 14, 9 26]
trirātro yad vyaśīryata tam etaiḥ sāmabhir abhiṣajyan gāyatrapārśvenopāyacchan santaninā samatanvan saṃkṛtinā samaskurvan pratiṣṭhitau pūrvau trirātrāv apratiṣṭhita eṣa yad etāny eva sāmāni kriyanta etasyaiva pratiṣṭhityai | [PB, 14, 9 27]
pauruhanmanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 28]
puruhanmā vā etena vaikhānaso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 29]
abhyāghātyaṃ bhavaty abhyāghātyasāmāno hi chandomāḥ | [PB, 14, 9 30]
dvaigataṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 31]
dvigad vā etena bhārgavo dviḥ svargaṃ lokam agacchad āgatya punar agacchat dvayoḥ kāmayor avaruddhyai dvaigataṃ kriyate | [PB, 14, 9 32]
hārāyaṇaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 33]
indras tejaskāmo haraskāmas tapo 'tapyata sa etaddhārāyaṇam apaśyat tena tejo haro 'vārunddha tejasvī harasvī bhavati hārāyaṇena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 34]
achidraṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 35]
yad vā etasyāhnaś chidram āsīt tad devā acchidreṇāpyauhaṃs tad acchidrasyācchidratvam | [PB, 14, 9 36]
bārhadukthaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 37]
bṛhaduktho vā etena vāmneyo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhānnādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 9 38]
udvad bhārgavaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 9 39]
pravatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan | [PB, 14, 9 40]
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 9 41]
{PB, 14, 10}
ka īṃ veda sute saceti satobṛhatyaḥ | [PB, 14, 10 1]
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yas saptame 'hani satobṛhatyo bhavanti nāṣṭame tasmād aṣṭame kāryā anapabhraṃśāya | [PB, 14, 10 2]
tadāhuḥ śithilam iva vā etacchando yat satobṛhatītyeṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā bṛhatī yā punaḥpadā yad indra prāg apāg udag iti diśāṃ vimarśaḥ pratiṣṭhityai | [PB, 14, 10 3]
tāsu naipātithaṃ brahmasāma | [PB, 14, 10 4]
sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 10 5]
ubhayaṃ śṛṇavacca neti | [PB, 14, 10 6]
yacca pṛṣṭhāni yāni caitānyahāni teṣām ubhayeṣāṃ santatyai | [PB, 14, 10 7]
tāsu vaiyaśvam | [PB, 14, 10 8]
vyaśvo vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyā etat pṛṣṭhānām antataḥ kriyate stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 10 9]
{PB, 14, 11}
pavasva deva āyuṣag indraṃ gacchatu te mada iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti | [PB, 14, 11 1]
abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhad yaśa ityamīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saharūpam upaityubhau hi varṇāvetadahaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 2]
prāṇā śiśur mahīnām iti prāṇavatyo bhavanti prāṇān eva tad yajamāne dadhāti | [PB, 14, 11 3]
abhī no vājasātamam ityabhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 4]
pavasva soma mahān samudra ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho etaddhyevaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāśchandāṃsyāpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā ity etacchandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt | [PB, 14, 11 5]
hinvanti sūram usraya iti gāyatryaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 14, 11 6]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 11 7]
svāśirām arko bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 8]
annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai prāṇā vai svāśiraḥ prāṇānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 11 9]
surūpaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 10]
paśavo vai surūpaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 11 11]
bhāsaṃ bhavati bhāti tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 12]
padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 13]
svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat sa na vyarocata tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan sa vyarocata yad vai tadbhā abhavat tad bhāsasya bhāsatvam | [PB, 14, 11 14]
tama iva vā etāny ahāni yacchandomās tebhya etena sāmnā vivāsayati | [PB, 14, 11 15]
kākṣīvataṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 16]
kakṣīvān vā etenauśijaḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kākṣīvatena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 17]
āsitaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 18]
asito vā etena daivalas trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ dṛṣṭim apaśyat trayāṇāṃ kāmānām avaruddhyā āsitaṃ kriyate | [PB, 14, 11 19]
aiṣiraṃ bhavati prajātirvā aiṣirāṇi prajāyate bahurbhavatyaiṣireṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 20]
traitaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 14, 11 21]
padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 22]
nāthavindu sāma vindate nāthaṃ nāthavindūny etānyahāni yat chandomā nātham evaitair vindate | [PB, 14, 11 23]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 14, 11 24]
kautsaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 25]
etena vai kutso 'ndhaso vipānam apaśyat sa ha sma vai surādṛtinopavasathaṃ dhāvayaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai kautsaṃ kriyate | [PB, 14, 11 26]
śuddhāśuddhīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 27]
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so 'śuddho 'manyata sa etacchuddhāśuddhīyam apaśyat tenāśudhyacchudhyati śuddhāśuddhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 28]
krauñcaṃ bhavati yad eva krauñcasya brāhmaṇaṃ yat dvitīye 'hani | [PB, 14, 11 29]
rayiṣṭhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 30]
paśavo vai rayiṣṭhaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 11 31]
audalaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 32]
udalo vā etena vaiśvāmitraḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavatyaudalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 33]
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā iti puruṣachandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadāś chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 14, 11 34]
viśoviśīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 11 35]
agnir akāmayata viśo viśo 'tithis syāṃ viśo viśa ātithyam aśnuvīyeti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad viśoviśīyam apaśyat tena viśo viśo 'tithir abhavat viśo viśa ātithyam āśnuta viśo viśo 'tithir bhavati viśo viśa ātithyam aśnute viśoviśīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 36]
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 14, 11 37]
iḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaśchandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ | [PB, 14, 11 38]
{PB, 14, 12}
preṣṭhaṃ vo atithim ityātithyasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate | [PB, 14, 12 1]
aindra no gadhi priya itīndriyasya vīryasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 14, 12 2]
purāṃ bhindur yuvā kavir amitaujā ajāyatendro viśvasya karmaṇo dhartā vajrī puruṣṭuta iti dhṛtyā eva | [PB, 14, 12 3]
auśanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 12 4]
uśanā vai kāvyo 'kāmayata yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānāṃ lokas tāvantaṃ spṛṇuyām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad auśanam apaśyat tena tāvantaṃ lokam aspṛṇod yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānām āsīt tad vāva sa tarhyakāmayata kāmasani sāmauśanaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe | [PB, 14, 12 5]
sāṃvartaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 12 6]
devānāṃ vai yajñaṃ rakṣāṃsyajighāṃsaṃs tānyetena indraḥ saṃvartam apāvapad yat saṃvartam apāvapat tasmāt sāṃvartaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ sāṃvartenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate sāṃvartena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 14, 12 7]
mārutaṃ bhavati | [PB, 14, 12 8]
māsā vai raśmayo maruto raśmayo maruto vai devānāṃ bhūyiṣṭhā bhūyiṣṭhā asāmeti vai sattram āsate bhūyiṣṭhā eva bhavantyṛtumanti pūrvāṇyahāny anṛtavaḥ chandomā yad etat sāma bhavati tenaitāny ahāny ṛtumanti bhavanti | [PB, 14, 12 9]
catuścatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavatyojasyeva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭup | [PB, 14, 12 10]
{PB, 15, 1}
akrān samudraḥ parame vidharmann iti navamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati | [PB, 15, 1 1]
paramaṃ vā etad ahar vidharma vidharma vā etad anyair aharbhir ahar yan navamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ hi variṣṭham | [PB, 15, 1 2]
matsi vāyum iṣṭaye rādhase na iti vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati | [PB, 15, 1 3]
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai | [PB, 15, 1 4]
daśarco bhavati daśākṣarā virāṭ vairājam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 15, 1 5]
saprabhṛtayo bhavantīndriyasya vīryasya rasasyānaticārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan | [PB, 15, 1 6]
aṣṭarco bhavati | [PB, 15, 1 7]
aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarunddhe | [PB, 15, 1 8]
ṣaḍṛcā bhavanty ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai | [PB, 15, 1 9]
catvāraḥ ṣaḍṛcā bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 15, 1 10]
savān uttamaḥ ṣaḍṛco bhavaty ubhayasya parokṣapratyakṣasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 15, 1 11]
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti | [PB, 15, 1 12]
aṣṭācatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai | [PB, 15, 1 13]
{PB, 15, 2}
aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭham ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 2 1]
gacchantīva vā ete ye navamam ahar gacchanti | [PB, 15, 2 2]
yo dīdāya samiddha sve duroṇa iti dīdāyeva hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvānaḥ svāhutam iti svāhuto hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhir āhuto viśvataḥ pratyañcam iti viśvato hy eṣa pratyaṅ | [PB, 15, 2 3]
tvaṃ varuṇa uta mitro agna iti vāruṇyeṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati | [PB, 15, 2 4]
mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam iti rāthantaraṃ maitrāvaruṇam | [PB, 15, 2 5]
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya | [PB, 15, 2 6]
mahāṃ indro ya ojasetyaindram aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayan navamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena mahayanti | [PB, 15, 2 7]
tā huve yayor idam iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam | [PB, 15, 2 8]
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya stomaḥ | [PB, 15, 2 9]
{PB, 15, 3}
pavamānasya jighnato hareś candrā asṛkṣateti harivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 15, 3 1]
pavamānasya jighnata iti vai bṛhato rūpaṃ hareś candrā asṛkṣateti jagatyā ubhayoḥ saharūpam upaiti sāmnaś ca chandasaś ca | [PB, 15, 3 2]
parīto ṣiñcatā sutam iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai navamam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai | [PB, 15, 3 3]
asāvi somo aruṣo vṛṣā harir iti jagatyas satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 15, 3 4]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 3 5]
bharadvājasyādārasṛd bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 6]
divodāsaṃ vai bharadvājapurohitaṃ nānājanāḥ paryayatanta sa upāsīdad ṛṣe gātuṃ me vindeti tasmā etena sāmnā gātum avindad gātuvid vā etatsāmānena dāre nāsṛnmeti tad adārasṛto 'dārasṛttvaṃ vindate gātuṃ na dāre dhāvaty adārasṛtā tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 7]
surūpaṃ bhavati yad eva surūpasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 3 8]
hariśrīnidhanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 9]
paśavo vai hariśriyaḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 10]
saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati yad eva saindhukṣitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 3 11]
gatanidhanaṃ bābhravaṃ bhavati gatyai | [PB, 15, 3 12]
babhrur vā etena kaumbhyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 13]
iḍānāṃ saṃkṣāro bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 14]
paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti | [PB, 15, 3 15]
ṛṣabhaḥ pāvamāno bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 16]
paśavo vai chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante | [PB, 15, 3 17]
pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 18]
pṛṣṭhaṃ vā etad ahnāṃ yan navamaṃ pṛṣṭha eva tat pṛṣṭhena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 15, 3 19]
kaulmalabarhiṣaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 20]
kulmalabarhir vā etena svargaṃ lokam apaśyat prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kaulmalabarhiṣeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 21]
arkapuṣpaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 22]
annaṃ vai devā arka iti vadanti rasam asya puṣpam iti sarasam evānnādyam avarunddhe 'rkapuṣpeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 23]
dairghyaśravasaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 3 24]
dīrghaśravā vai rājanya ṛṣir jyog aparuddho 'śanāyaṃś caran sa etad dairghaśravasam apaśyat tena sarvābhyo digbhyo 'nnādyam avārunddha sarvābhyo digbhyo 'nnādyam avarunddhe dairghaśravasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 25]
vaiyaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva vaiyaśvasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 3 26]
ābhīśavaṃ yad ābhīśavasya | [PB, 15, 3 27]
devasthānaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai saṃskṛti bhavati saṃskṛtyai | [PB, 15, 3 28]
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā devasthāne tiṣṭhantaḥ saṃkṛtinā samaskurvaṃs tat saṃkṛteḥ saṃkṛtitvaṃ devasthānena vai devāḥ svarge loke pratyatiṣṭhan svarge loke pratiṣṭhām ety etat | [PB, 15, 3 29]
varuṇāya devatā rājyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa etad devasthānam apaśyat tato vai tās tasmai rājyāyātiṣṭhanta tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya | [PB, 15, 3 30]
kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 15, 3 31]
bhargo bhargeṇa tuṣṭuvāno bhavati yaśo yaśasā | [PB, 15, 3 32]
vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati yad eva vāsiṣṭhasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 3 33]
dīrghatamaso 'rko bhavaty annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 15, 3 34]
sāmarājaṃ bhavati sāmrājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati sāmarājñā tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 35]
tad u saṃvad ity āhuḥ saṃvatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan | [PB, 15, 3 36]
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ | [PB, 15, 3 37]
{PB, 15, 4}
śrāyanta iva sūryam iti sūryavatyo bhavanti | [PB, 15, 4 1]
ādityadevatyaṃ hy etad ahar anto vai sūro 'nta etan navamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai | [PB, 15, 4 2]
yata indra bhayāmahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi maghavañchagdhi tava tan na ūtaye vidviṣo vimṛdho jahīti dviṣaścaiva mṛdhaśca navamenāhnā vihatya daśamenāhnottiṣṭhanti | [PB, 15, 4 3]
śrīr vai śrāyantīyaṃ śrīr navamam ahaḥ śriyam eva tacchriyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [PB, 15, 4 4]
samantaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 4 5]
samantena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta purodhākāmaḥ samantena stuvīta | [PB, 15, 4 6]
āgneyī pṛthivyāgneyo brāhmaṇa aindrī dyaur aindro rājanyo 'ntarikṣeṇa dyāvāpṛthivī samante antarikṣeṇaivainaṃ samantaṃ karoti vindate paśūn pra purodhām āpnoti ya evaṃ vidvān samantena stuvate stomaḥ | [PB, 15, 4 7]
{PB, 15, 5}
tvaṃ somāsi dhārayur iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 1]
tvaṃ hyaṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 2]
pavasva devavītaya iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 3]
parityaṃ haryataṃ harim iti parivatyo bhavantyanto vai navamam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai | [PB, 15, 5 4]
pavasva soma mahe dakṣāyetyakṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho etaddhyevaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmāḥ kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā ity etacchandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt | [PB, 15, 5 5]
upoṣu jātam apturam iti gāyatryas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāt jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante | [PB, 15, 5 6]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 5 7]
āśvasūktaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 8]
agniṃ vai pūrvair aharbhir ājuhoty athaitad ādityadevatyam ahaḥ śukra āhuta ity asau vā ādityaḥ śukras tam evaitenājuhoti | [PB, 15, 5 9]
śāmmadaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 10]
śammad vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 11]
dāvasunidhanaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 12]
āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ | [PB, 15, 5 13]
dāvasur vā etad āṅgirasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjat yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai | [PB, 15, 5 14]
pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 15]
parācībhir vā anyābhir iḍābhī reto dadhadety athaitat pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ prajātyai tasmāt parāñco garbhāḥ sambhavanti pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād u te 'vācīnabilebhyo nāvapadyanta etena hy eva te dhṛtāḥ | [PB, 15, 5 16]
hāviṣkṛtaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai kṛtānuvāda eva saḥ | [PB, 15, 5 17]
sauparṇaṃ bhavati yad eva sauparṇasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 5 18]
vaiśvamanasaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 19]
viśvamanasaṃ vā ṛṣim adhyāyam udvrajitaṃ rakṣo 'gṛhṇāt tam indro 'cāyad ṛṣiṃ vai rakṣo 'grahīd iti tam abhyavadad ṛṣe kas tvaiṣa iti sthāṇur iti brūhīti rakṣo 'bravīt sa sthāṇur ity abravīt tasmai vā etena praharety asmā iṣīkāṃ vajraṃ prayacchann abravīt tenāsya sīmānam abhinat saiṣendreṇateṣīkā pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ vaiśvamanasenāpāhatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate vaiśvamanasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 20]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 5 21]
nihavo bhavaty annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [PB, 15, 5 22]
hīti vā annaṃ pradīyata ītyagnir annam atti | [PB, 15, 5 23]
ṛṣayo vā indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ nāpaśyan sa vasiṣṭho 'kāmayata katham indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ paśyeyam iti sa etaṃ nihavam apaśyat tato vai sa indraṃ pratyakṣam apaśyat sa enam abravīd brāhmaṇaṃ te vakṣyāmi yathā tvatpurohitā bharatāḥ prajaniṣyante 'tha mānyebhya ṛṣibhyo mā pravoca iti tasmā etān stomabhāgān abravīt tato vai vasiṣṭhapurohitā bharatāḥ prājāyanta sendraṃ vā etat sāma yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya | [PB, 15, 5 24]
yadvāhiṣṭhīyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 25]
brahmayaśasaṃ vā etāni sāmāny ṛcā śrotrīyāṇi brahmayaśasī bhavati yadvāhiṣṭhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 26]
āsitaṃ bhavati yad evāsitasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 5 27]
sādhraṃ bhavati siddhyai | [PB, 15, 5 28]
ākūpāraṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 29]
akūpāro vā etena kaśyapo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchajjemānaṃ mahimānaṃ gacchaty ākūpāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 30]
vidharma bhavati dharmasya vidhṛtyai | [PB, 15, 5 31]
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsyāpyante kiṃchandasaśchandomā iti puruṣacchandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai | [PB, 15, 5 32]
śrudhyaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 5 33]
paśavo vai śrudhyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [PB, 15, 5 34]
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnā śrūdhiyā ehiyety anvahvayat ta enam upāvartanta yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnām upāvṛttyai | [PB, 15, 5 35]
upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃ veda | [PB, 15, 5 36]
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyantīḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaśchandomāḥ paśuṣveva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ | [PB, 15, 5 37]
{PB, 15, 6}
āgneyīṣu pūrveṣām ahnām ukthāni praṇayantyathaitasyāhna āgneyyaindryāṃ praṇayantyubhayor eva rūpayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 15, 6 1]
aidhmavāhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 6 2]
āgneyyaindrīṣu stuvanti brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca sayujīkaroti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti brāhmaṇe kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti | [PB, 15, 6 3]
traikakubhaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 6 4]
ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ traikakubham | [PB, 15, 6 5]
udvaṃśīyaṃ bhavati yad evodvaṃśīyasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 6 6]
aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai | [PB, 15, 6 7]
{PB, 15, 7}
gāyatraṃ vai saptamam ahas traiṣṭubham aṣṭamaṃ jāgataṃ navamam athaitad ānuṣṭubham ahar yad daśamam | [PB, 15, 7 1]
tad āhur yad anuṣṭubhaṃ stomyāṃ pratyakṣam upeyuḥ parāṃ parāvataṃ yajamāno gacchen na pratitiṣṭhed iti yā vai caturviṃśatir gāyatryas tā aṣṭādaśānuṣṭubho 'nuṣṭubham eva tat stomyāṃ parokṣam upayanti pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 15, 7 2]
prajāpatiṃ vā etenāhnā pariveviṣati tanna vyavavadyaṃ yad vai śreṣṭhe pariviṣyamāṇo vadaty annādyasya so 'vagrahas tasmān na vyavavadyam annādyasyānavagrāhāya | [PB, 15, 7 3]
tad u vyavavadyaṃ yathā śreṣṭhāya baliṃ hriyamāṇaṃ panthānaṃ paryanuvedayati gatyai tathā tat | [PB, 15, 7 4]
yāvaty anuṣṭup tāvatīṃ vācaṃ sampādya vibrūyus tad v anatiriktaṃ svasyo caiva yajñasyāriṣṭyai | [PB, 15, 7 5]
abhi vā ete devān ārohantīty āhur ye daśabhir aharbhiḥ stuvata iti pañcānām ahnām anurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti yathābhyāruhya pratyavarohet tathā tan navarco bhavati yā evāmūḥ prayacchan yā avadadhāti tā etā udasyati | [PB, 15, 7 6]
vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajaty ādityaiṣā bhavatīyaṃ vā aditir asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati | [PB, 15, 7 7]
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya | [PB, 15, 7 8]
{PB, 15, 8}
suṣamiddho na āvahety āpriya ājyāni bhavanti | [PB, 15, 8 1]
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etāny āpriya ājyāny apaśyat tair ātmānam āprīṇāt dugdha iva vā eṣa riricāno yo daśabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvāno yad etāny āpriya ājyāni bhavanty ātmānam evaitair āprīṇāti | [PB, 15, 8 2]
yad adya sūra udita iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam anto vai sūro 'nta etad daśamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyā ut tvā madantu somā ity udvad aindram utthānasya rūpam | [PB, 15, 8 3]
indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti stomaḥ | [PB, 15, 8 4]
{PB, 15, 9}
uccā te jātam andhasa ity udvatyo gāyatryo bhavanty utthānasya rūpam | [PB, 15, 9 1]
punānas soma dhārayeti panthānam eva tat paryavayanti | [PB, 15, 9 2]
ā jāgṛvir vipra ṛtaṃ matīnām iti yad āpte pravatīḥ kuryur atipadyeran yad āvatyo bhavanty anatipādāya | [PB, 15, 9 3]
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam | [PB, 15, 9 4]
āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kﾱptiś cānnādyaṃ ca kﾱptiṃ caivaitenānnādyaṃ cābhyuttiṣṭhanti | [PB, 15, 9 5]
ājigaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai | [PB, 15, 9 6]
ājir vā eṣa pratato yat dvādaśāhas tasyaitad ujjityai | [PB, 15, 9 7]
ābhīkaṃ bhavaty abhikrāntyai | [PB, 15, 9 8]
aṅgirasas tapas tepānāḥ śucam aśocaṃs ta etat sāmāpaśyaṃs tān abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tena śucam aśamayanta yad abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tasmād ābhīkaṃ yām eva pūrvair aharbhiḥ śucaṃ śocanti tām etenātra śamayitvottiṣṭhanti | [PB, 15, 9 9]
utsedho bhavati | [PB, 15, 9 10]
utsedhena vai devāḥ paśūn udasedhan niṣedhena paryagṛhṇan | [PB, 15, 9 11]
antarotsedhaniṣedhau yajñāyajñīyam | [PB, 15, 9 12]
paśavo 'nnādyaṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ paśūn eva tad annādyam utsedhaniṣedhābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāti | [PB, 15, 9 13]
mādhyandine vai pavamāne devā yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohaṃs tad ya evaṃ veda mādhyandina evaitat pavamāne yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohati | [PB, 15, 9 14]
atho parokṣam anuṣṭubhaṃ sampadyate 'har eṣā vai pratyakṣam anuṣṭup yad yajñāyajñīyaṃ tad yat tṛtīyasavane kuryuḥ pratyakṣam anuṣṭubham ṛccheyus tasmān mādhyandine kurvanti tena parokṣam anuṣṭubham upayanti | [PB, 15, 9 15]
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati | [PB, 15, 9 16]
etad vai yajñasya śvastanaṃ yad gaurīvitam etadāyatano yajamāno yan madhyandino yad gaurīvitaṃ madhyandine bhavati śvastanam eva tad yajamāna ātman dhatte stomaḥ | [PB, 15, 9 17]
